/ /dpal ldan sa skya pa'i bstan 'dzin ngor rdzong rnam gnyis kyi gsung ngag rin po che'i phyag len gyi rim pa 'ga' zhig las brtsams te so so'i bzhed srol rnams legs par bshad
pa lugs gnyis zab don gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba bzhugs so//

rgya gar skad du/ shrI dharmma swa mI lo ka tsakShu bhaTTa ra ka sarba gu ru bhyo na maH bindhA tra wA kyo ba sudho mri te na karmma rka bhA sa manta bha baksa kA shaH bod
skad du/ dpal chos kyi rje 'jig rten gyi mig rje btsun bla ma thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gsung gi bdud rtsis nor 'dzin gyi thig le 'dir 'phrin las nyi 'od kun du gsal
bar gyur cig rigs kun khyab bdag zung 'jug rdo rje 'chang / /stobs kyi mgon po dpal ldan birWa'i zhabs/ /de dang dbyer med sa skya'i bla chen rje/ /yab sras khu dbon rim
par byon la 'dud/ /'gro mgon bla ma'i gsung ngag bang mdzod la/ /dbang bsgyur dpal ldan rje dang gzungs kyi dpal/ /slob mar bcas te lugs zung chos kyi sgo/ /dang por 'byed
mdzad de dag ngo mtshar rmad/ /zas gtsang sras po'i zhal gyi bum bzang las/ /lung bstan

bdud rtsi rnyed pa'i skyes bu'i mchog /gang gi 'phrin las nyi 'od ltar gsal ba'i/ /kun mkhyen kun dga' bzang pos bdag skyongs shig /mgon de'i thugs sras nges don bstan pa'i
bdag /sems dpa' chen por grags pa'i mus chen rje/ /gzhan yang kun mkhyen smra ba'i seng ge dang / /paN chen shAkya'i mtshan rnams phyag gi gnas/ /gang gi mkhyen rab gzhol
med rdo rje yis/ /gzhan gzhung sra brtan brag ri gzhom pa la/ /rgyal srid chen po'i dpung ltar ches dpa' ba'i/ /mtshan gyi grags dkar gsal de'ang bsngags par 'os/ /de yi
bzhed gzhung la dgyes 'gro ba kun/ /dga' mdzad rnam par rgyal ba'i mtshan can dang / /e waM mi nub bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan che/ /bsgrengs mkhas legs pa'i 'byung gnas spyi
bos mchod/ /rgyud dang man ngag shes bya'i gnas kun

la/ /mkhas pa'i phul phyin dkon mchog lhun grub dang / /byang chub sgrub pa'i rnam dpyod blo'i nor bu/ /dbang gi rgyal po gang la mnga' de rgyal/ /yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i bdag
po'i chos srid dpal/ /srid mthar rgyun chad med par spel mdzad pa'i/ /sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po yab sras la/ /bka' drin dran pas lan brgyar phyag bgyi 'o/ /gang
thugs dus gsum rgyal bar ro gcig kyang / /gdul bya'i snang ngor bshes gnyen mchog gi sku/ /gcig chog rgyal po rje btsun buddha'i mtshan/ /bdag gi snying dbus 'bral med rtag
bzhugs mdzod/ /sa skya'i bstan 'dzin ngor rdzong rnam gnyis kyi/ /bzhed srol kun la phyogs med bdag dad pas/ /mkhas dbang so so'i legs bshad snying po'i don/ /bsdus te
spel la bdag yid spro ba skyes/ /'dir dpal ldan sa skya pa'i bstan 'dzin ngor rdzong rnam gnyis kyi

gsung ngag rin po che'i phyag len gyi rim pa 'ga' zhig las brtsams te so so'i bzhed srol rnams legs par bshad pa/ lugs gnyis zab don gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba 'di 'chad
pa la/ spyir rje btsun sa skya pa'i bstan 'dzin la mdo phyogs kyi bstan 'dzin g.yag rong rnam gnyis dang / zab mo rdo rje theg pa gtso bor gyur pa la ngor rdzong rnam gnyis
zhes yongs su grags pa'i ngor rdzong gnyis ni dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyan mtshan gyi slob ma dag nas gyes pa yin te/ de'ang chos rje de la spyir slob ma'i
mchog sngags kyi rgyal tshab gnyis/ gsung ngag 'dzin pa'i thugs kyi sras mchog brgyad/ bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bu chen po bzhi/ yongs su grags pa'i mkhas mchog bcu la sogs
pa mang du byon pa'i gsung ngag 'dzin pa brgyad kyi nang tshan rdzong chung pa sngags 'chang

gzungs kyi dpal ba dang / ngor lugs kyi brgyud pa'i rtsa ba bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims pa gnyis las gsung ngag gi bka' 'dzin pa'i brgyud pa so sor 'phel te/ dang po las
chos rje bzang po rgyal mtshan/ de las rgyal mtshan dkon mchog dang / dge ba rgyal mtshan sogs/ rgyal mtshan dkon mchog las mkhas grub chen po gtsang gi rigs su 'khrungs
pa mus srad pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan la sogs pa mang du 'phel/ de rnams las brgyud de dar ba'i lam 'bras la rdzong lugs dang / bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims pa las/ grub chen
buddha shrI/ de las rgyal bas lung bstan pa'i skyes bu chen po thams cad mkhyen pa kun dga' bzang po sogs 'phel te/ ngor chen 'dis gsung ngag rin po che tshar brgyad
cu gya gsum tsam gnang zhing / gsung ngag 'chad thabs kyi man ngag gsang ba'i sgo 'byed sogs lugs 'di la mkho ba'i yig cha mang du mdzad de gdams pa 'di nyid sgo du ma'i
sgo nas ches cher dar rgyas su spel zhing / de nas brgyud pa la gsung ngag ngor lugs zhes grags pa 'di byung ba yin no/ /gzhan yang chos rje bla ma'i slob ma yongs grags
mkhas pa bcu'i nang tshan theg chen chos rje kun dga' bkra shis las nyi lde ba kun dga' rgyal mtshan dang / brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po sogs mang du 'phel ba'i/ brag
thog pa'i thugs sras rdo rje gdan pa chen po kun dga' rnam rgyal te/ de ltar mang du byon pa'i mkhas mchog rdo rje rgyal mtshan sogs la rdzong pa snga rabs pa dang / rdo
rje gdan pa sogs la rdzong pa phyi rabs pa zhes kyang grags so/

/de las rdzong lugs kyi bstan 'dzin gyi gtso bo ni nyi lde ba kun dga' rgyal mtshan nam mtshan gzhan 'jam dbyangs grags pa'i dpal zhes pa de nyid dang / brang mo che pa rdo
rje rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal sogs mang du byon zhing / ngor lugs kyi bstan 'dzin gyi gtso bo ni rgyal bas lung bstan pa'i skyes bu chen po rdo rje
'chang kun dga' bzang po/ sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge paN chen shAkya mchog ldan/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ mkhas pa'i
dbang po dkon mchog lhun grub la sogs pa grangs dang tshad med pa zhig byon pa las/ de ltar lugs gnyis kyi mkhas pa de dag don dam lta ba'i gnad la bzhed tshul mi 'dra
ba'i khyad par cung zad kyang med mod/ 'on kyang kun rdzob cho ga'i rnam gzhag sogs la phyag len mi mthun pa 'ga' re byung ba'i dbang gis dgag sgrub kyi rnam par gzhag pa'ang
ci rigs pa snang te/ de'ang gtsang byams pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis chu rgyun rnam pa bzhi dang / sgrub pa bzhi la sogs pa gsung rab kyi tshogs mang po zhig mdzad
pa las rnam par bshad pa'i chu rgyun dang po ni/ bo gdong paN chen sogs gzhan lugs kyi mkhas pa 'ga' zhig gis rje btsun gong ma'i gsung la brgal brtags kyi rnam grangs mang
po zhig gsungs pa dag lung rigs kyi sgo nas sun phyung ste chos dang mthun pa'i lan med par mdzad cing / gong ma'i dgongs don phyin ci ma log par sgrub pa'i legs bshad
kyi dga' ston du snang ste skabs drug gi bdag nyid can no/ /chu

rgyun gnyis pa ni kyai rdo rje'i rgyud kyi mtshan dang / 'gyur dang bla ma brgyud pa sogs ngor lugs dang mi mthun pa dag la mtha' dpyod mdzad pa zhig ste/ rgyud dang man ngag
gnyis kyi nang nas gtso bor rgyud 'grel gyi phyogs so/ /chu rgyun gsum pa ni theg chen chos rje'i Dombi lugs kyi kye rdor gyi sgrub dkyil gnyis kyi rtsod spong du snang
la/ chu rgyun bzhi pa ni gtso bor gsung ngag lam 'bras kyi phyag len 'ga' zhig las brtsams te ngor lugs la brgal zhing brtags pa'o/ /bsgrub pa bzhi'i dang po ni gong ma'i
bka' bsgrub pa/ gnyis pa ni 'phags pa'i bzhed pa bsgrub pa/ gsum pa ni chos rje bla ma'i bzhed pa bsgrub pa/ bzhi pa ni phyag len bsgrub pa yin cing / de bzhi dang chu
rgyun phyi ma gsum ngor lugs la ched du brgal ba gtso che'ang / gzhan rnams la ngor lugs kyi brgyud 'dzin rnams kyis lan mdzad pa ni ma mthong la/ chu rgyun bzhi pa dang
bsgrub pa dang po la/ ngor pa'i mkhas pa dag gis lan gyi rim pa mang du snang ngo / de'ang chu rgyun bzhi par/ sems bskyed brgyud pa med pa dang / /rjes bzung grangs nges
med pa dang / /sta gon 'brel pa med pa dang / /slob dpon grangs nges med pa dang / /lus dkyil 'byung khungs med pa dang / /dbang rdzas yongs dag med pa dang / /rgyas gdab
rigs mtshon med pa dang / /bza' ba'i dam tshig med pa yis/ /'di na thabs mchog thabs min byed/ /smin byed byas kyang smin min la/ /grol byed bsgom yang grol min pas/ /de
phyir 'di dag dgag par bya/ /zhes ngor lugs kyi bzhed pa mi 'thad pa'i phyogs

brgyad thog mar mdor bstan nam rtsa tshig gi tshul du smos te/ slar de dag rgyas bshad dam rang 'grel gyi tshul du zhib par gsungs pa la brten nas/ ngor lugs kyi bstan 'dzin
dag gis de nyid kyi brgal lan du ma dang / slad nas rdzong lugs kyi mkhas pa rnams kyis kyang lan gyi rim pa dag mdzad de/ /'bel ba'i gtam gyis bstan pa rin po che nyid
gsal bar mdzad pa yin no/ /gong gi tshigs bcad 'di dag la paN chen gyi rnam thar sgo brgyad pa dang / dkon mchog lhun grub kyi tshangs pa'i rigs sngags su mi 'dra ba re
'byung yang 'dir ni chu rgyun bzhi pa nas ji skad 'byung ba bzhin bkod pa'o/ /brgal lan gyi rnam gzhag de dag las 'dir so so'i bzhed don gyi snying po dag blangs te bshad
na/ 'di la don tshan dgu ste/ sems bskyed la brgyud pa yod med kyi rnam gzhag rjes 'dzin la grangs nges yod med kyi rnam gzhag sta gon la 'brel pa yod med kyi rnam gzhag
slob dpon gyi dbang la grangs nges yod med kyi rnam gzhag brtul zhugs dang slob dpon gyi dbang la yangs dag yod med kyi rnam gzhag lus dkyil la 'byung khungs kyi tshig yod
med kyi rnam gzhag lus dkyil lha la rgyas gdab rigs mtshon yod med kyi rnam gzhag bza' ba'i dam tshig yod med kyi rnam gzhag gdan gyi dag pa sogs gong ma'i bka' yin min
gyi rnam gzhag bstan pa'o/ /dang po ni/ chos rje rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis rnam bshad chu rgyun bzhi par/ sems bskyed brgyud pa med pa dang / /zhes pa'i rgyas bshad du
ji ltar

'byung ba'i don bsdus te bkod na/ rje btsun chen po'i mdzad byang yod pa'i sems bskyed kyi yi ge ngor pas sgo rum dpe khang nas rnyed zer ba de'i steng nas sems bskyed byed
pa la brgyud pa chad pa ni tshig de nyid kyis shes shing / lam 'bras pa phyi ma rnams kyis brgyud rim mang po'i grangs bgrangs nas/ yi ge de'i steng nas lam 'bras pa sus
kyang byas pa med do/ /gzhan yang mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje bas bla ma bcu phrag lhag tsam bsten nas gsan par mdzad pa'i rje btsun gyi bka' 'bum gyi nang na yi ge de med
ces rgol bar mdzad do/ /de la paN chen shAkya mchog ldan gyis brang mo che ba'i brgal lan rnam thar sgo brgyad pa zhes bya ba mdzad pa de'i nang du gong gi de'i lan la/
spyir bshad pa dang / dngos kyi lan gnyis su mdzad nas/ dang po la so thar gyi mkhan brgyud dang / sngags kyi sdom pa'i bla ma brgyud pa dang 'dra ba zhig sems bskyed kyi
sdom pa la nges pa nyid du mi dgos te/ bslab btus dang spyod 'jug gi dgongs pas sems bskyed kyi sdom pa len gso gnyis ka la bla ma nges par mi dgos pa dang / byang sa
ltar na len pa la dgos kyang gso ba la nges par mi dgos pas so/ /spyir rnal 'byor dbang phyug nas brgyud pa bar ma chad pa'i smon 'jug gi sdom pa zhig mi 'dod na ni shin
tu tha chad la/ 'dod na ni de brgyud ldan gyi rdo rje slob dpon zhig gis phyis byung gi byang sems kyi sdom pa 'bogs chog ma nor ba ci yin zhig gi steng nas sdom pa de phog
chog ste/ 'bogs rgyu'i sdom pa rang gi ngo bo la khyad par med pa yin pas so/ /dper na chos kyi rje sa skya paNDi tas hor yul

du thub pa'i dgongs pa gsal ba mdzad nas rjes su bod du bskur ba de'i tshe tshig don rnams slob ma dag gis bod du bshad chog pa bzhin no zhes pa dang / dngos lan la sa skya
pa chen po las dbang bskur thob pa'i slob dpon zhig gis slob dpon rtse mos mdzad pa'i dbang chu chen mo'i steng nas dbang ma zhus kyang / rang gi slob ma dag la dbang chu
chen mo'i steng nas dbang bskur byed du rung ba bzhin du/ rje btsun rin po che nas brgyud pa'i byang sdom thob la ma nyams pa'i rdo rje slob dpon zhig gis/ rje btsun gyis
mdzad pa'i sems bskyed kyi yi ge'i steng nas rang gis thob pa ma yin kyang gzhan la 'bog tu rung ste/ rje btsun chen po nas brgyud pa'i sems bskyed kyi sdom pa thob la
ma nyams pa'i gang zag yin pas so/ /de ni snyan brgyud yi ger bris pa rnams la mtshungs zhes gsungs so/ /yang gong gi mus srad pa chen po'i gsung de'i lan du/ thams cad
mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis brgal lan tshangs pa'i rigs sngags zhes bya ba mdzad de/ de nyid las/ dngos bstan gyi rgol tshul la skyon chags pa dang / zhe 'dod kyi
lan dpe dang bcas te bshad pa/ rgol ba po rang nyid nyes pa can du bstan pa dang gsum du mdzad nas/ dang po la sems bskyed kyi yi ge de sngar med pa phyis gsar du rnyed
pa dang / yi ge de'i steng nas sngon byon pa'i chen po sus kyang byas pa med do zhes pa de'ang ngor chen gyi gsung gang na'ang med cing / khungs thub kyi gsung bgros na'ang
med pas rang gi zhe 'dod kyis smras par snang bas/ dngos bstan gyi rgol tshul

yang mi 'thad par gsungs/ zhe 'dod kyi lan la sems bskyed kyi yi ge de gsar du rnyed pa dang / de la lung gi rgyun tsam med du chug kyang / de tsam gyis sems bskyed kyi brgyud
pa med par mi 'gro/ de bas khyed rang rgyud sde nas bshad pa'i dbang gi sngon 'gro'i sems bskyed cig mi 'dod na shin tu skal ba dman/ 'dod na sangs rgyas nas rje btsun
rtse mo yan chad du sems bskyed kyi yi ge de med kyang / de'i brjod bya dang mthun pa'i sems bskyed kyi sdom pa'i rgyun yod pa dang / rje btsun nas ngor chen rdo rje 'chang
gi bar du'ang bde kye gnyis kyi dbang gi sngon du yi ge de dang mthun pa'i sems bskyed kyi sdom pa'i phyag len ma nor ba yod pas/ phyag len de dang mthun pa'i yi ge
su zhig gis byas kyang de'i steng nas sems bskyed bya rung ste/ dper na dbang chu chen mo'i lung ma thob kyang / kye rdor man ngag lugs kyi dbang thob la ma nyams pa'i rdo
rje slob dpon zhig gis de'i steng nas dbang byar rung ba dang / karma sha taM lta bu'i steng nas sdom pa thob la ma nyams pa'i mkhan po zhig gis las chog tshad ma gang
rung zhig gi steng nas sdom pa 'bogs rung ba bzhin dang / snyan brgyud yi ger bris pa thams cad la des mtshon zhing / des na rje btsun chen pos mdzad pa'i yi ge de ni rgyud
sde nas bshad pa'i sems bskyed kyi cho ga thun mong ma yin pa yin/ dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed kyi cho ga ma yin pas/ dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed lam 'bras pa la yod med
ci ltar yang lugs 'di'i sems bskyed byed pa la phan gnod gang yang med gsung pa'i lan mdzad do/ /rgol

ba po nyes pa can du bstan pa la/ dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed ni lam 'bras pa la med par rgol ba po rang gi khas blangs/ rgyud sde nas bshad pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i theg
chen sems bskyed kyi cho ga ni khyed kyi dgag bya'i gtso bo yin/ sems tsam lugs kyi sems bskyed kyi cho ga ni lam 'bras pa gong ma rnams la med/ de dag tu ma 'dus pa'i theg
chen sems bskyed rang 'bogs byed kyi cho ga sbyor dngos rjes gsum tshang ba med cing / yod kyang de la brgyud pa yod pa dka' bas na rgol ba po rang nyid brgyud pa dang
bcas pa la sbyor dngos rjes gsum tshang pa'i cho ga las thob pa'i theg chen sems skyed med par khas blangs/ de ni shin tu mi rigs te/ rigs dang dam tshig ma thob snying
rje med/ /de bzhin byang chub sems kyang ma bskyed cing / /sangs rgyas ma dad lha gzhan bsten pa la/ /nga yi gsang sngags bstan na phung bar 'gyur/ /zhes dang / phyag rdor
dbang bskur ba las/ 'jam dpal gang dag byang chub kyi sems bsgom pa la zhugs pa dang / gang gi tshe de dag gi byang chub kyi sems bsgrub par gyur pa de'i tshe/ 'jam dpal
byang chub sems dpa'i gsang sngags kyi sgo dpyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' de dag ye shes chen por dbang bskur ba'i gzungs sngags kyi dkyil 'khor 'dir gzhug par bya yi/
gang de dag gis byang chub kyi sems rdzogs par ma gyur pa de dag ni mi gzhug go /de dag la ni phyag rgya dang sngags bstan par mi bya'o/ /'jam dpal mtshams med pa lnga
byas pa ni sla'i/ dam tshig mi shes pa

dang / lus yongs su ma sbyangs pa dang / byang chub kyi sems bsgom pa ma grub pa la ston pa ni de lta ma yin te/ 'jam dpal sems can de dag gi mdun du ni nam yang tshig tsam
brjod par mi bya'o/ /zhes sogs dang / slob dpon rin po che'i dbang chu las/ gang zag rim gyis pa dang / cig car ba'i rigs can gnyis ka la'ang sems bskyed la gzung bar bya'o
zhes 'byung ba dang / ljon shing las/ de ltar cig car du 'jug pa zhes bya ba yin mod kyang / bla ma gong ma rnams kyi phyag len gyi brgyud pas thun mong ma yin pa'i skyabs
su 'gro ba dang sems bskyed pa tsam sngon du mdzad pas zhes gsungs nas/ 'di nyid kyi cho ga dang bslab bya sogs rgyas par bshad pa dang 'gal zhes gsung zhing / rje
dkon mchog lhun grub nyid kyis mdzad pa'i tshangs pa'i rig sngags kyi don bsdus don brgyad pa las/ rje btsun mched kyi dbang chu dang / /mngon par rtogs pa ljon shing las/
/dbang bskur sngon du skyabs 'gro dang / /sems bskyed sdom pa 'bogs so zhes/ /gsungs pa de la lag len zhig /sa skya'i chos na yod dam med/ /yod na de yi brgyud pa gang
/ /med na khungs nas med pa 'am/ gsar du chad pa gang yin brtag /dang po ltar na sku mched kyis/ /de ltar bshad pa ming tsam las/ /nyams len rim par ma byung phyir/ /byang
chub sems mchog ma bskyed la/ /gsang sngags bstan na phung ngo zhes/ /rdo rje 'chang gis bkag pa de/ /rje btsun gong mas bsgrub mdzad dam/ /phyi ma ltar na dbang yod kyang
/ /sngon 'gro'i sems bskyed chad do zhes/ /chos

dang mthun par smra nus sam/ /rang la khyab pa bsgrub byas nas/ /phyogs chos gzhan la sbyor ram ci/ /gang ltar byas kyang byang chub sems/ /ma bskyed pa la dbang bskur ba'i/
/nyes pa khyod kyi thog tu babs/ /byed na de yis nyes pa ci/ /brgyud pa med pa'i sems bskyed cig /mi 'dod bzhin du khas len nam/ /thun mong min pa'i skyabs 'gro dang /
/sems bskyed cho ga byed pa la/ /dbu ma'i lugs kyi sems bskyed pa/ /lam 'bras pa la med do zhes/ /rnam par dpyod la 'brel ci zhig /ces gsungs pa yin no/ /don tshan dang po
'di la paN chen dang / thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis/ spyir dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed lam 'bras brgyud pa la med ces pa phyogs sngar bkod nas de'i lan
'debs kyang mdzad mod/ mus srad pa'i chu rgyun bzhi par ni de 'dra dngos shugs gang la'ang bshad pa mi snang la/ gzhan yang dkon mchog lhun grub kyis yi ge de'i steng nas
chen po sus kyang byas pa med ces pa ngor chen gyi gsung gang na'ang med ces sogs kyi lan mdzad pa ni yi ge ma dag pa zhig gzigs pa'i gsung du snang ste/ mus srad pa'i
chu rgyun bzhi par lan de ltar mdzad dgos pa'i rtsod pa mi snang bas so snyam du sems te dpyad par bya'o/ /yang gong gi de'i lan du tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po blo gsal
rgya mtshos gsung ngag rin po che'i skabs brgyad la 'khrul pa spong ba rdo rje'i 'khrul 'khor gyi zegs ma zhes bya ba mdzad pa'i nang du/ byang chub sems bskyed med pa dang
/ /rjes 'dzin mang po med pa dang /

/sta gon gcig las med pa dang / /lus dkyil bskyed gzhi med pa dang / /slob dpon gcig tu nges pa dang / /dbang chog lung khungs med pa dang / /rigs gtso'i rgyas 'debs med pa
dang / /dpa' bo'i ston mo med pa rnams/ /rdo rje theg pa spyi dang ni/ /khyad par dpal ldan sa skya pa'i/ /bstan la gnad bcos bdud kyi tshig /yin phyir thos kyang rna ba
dgab/ /ces rtsa tshig gi tshul gyis mus srad pa chen po'i brgal ba brgyad kyi lan phyogs gcig tu bkod de 'grel pa'i tshul du lan dang po la/ de ltar na rje btsun bsod nams
rtse mo'i dbang chu'i steng nas kye rdor gyi dbang byed pa mi 'thad cing brgyud pa med par 'gyur te/ 'phags pa rin po che'i zhal slob dam pa kun dga' grags/ dga' ldan
pa kun bsod/ zhang dkon mchog dpal ba sogs kyis yi ge de'i steng nas ma thob cing / phyag len yang de la mi byed par 'phags pa'i mngon dkyil gyi steng nas mdzad pas so/ /yi
ge de gnyis la nang sel gyi khyad par cung zad tsam las med pas rung zer na/ sems bskyed kyi yi ge sgo rum nas ngor chen gyi gsar du rnyed pa de'i steng nas sems bskyed
byed pa dang / dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed kyi cho ga gnyis la'ang nang sel gyi khyad par phra mo tsam las med pas 'di la'ang mtshungs/ yi ge 'di'i lung mkhan chen shes
rdor bas ma thob pa sogs thal ror snang ste/ ngor pa'ang 'di'i lung mi byed pa'i phyir/ des na spyir birWa pa dang / khyad par rje btsun chen po nas brgyud pa'i sems bskyed
thob la ma nyams pa dag gis 'di'i steng nas gzhan la sems bskyed phog pa la skyon ci

yang med cing / phyag len gyi khyad par ches khungs btsun zhing rnam par dag par 'gyur ba yin no zhes gsungs so/ /de ltar ngor lugs kyi bstan 'dzin dag gis mus srad pa chen
po'i sems bskyed brgyud pa med pa dang zhes pa'i lan 'debs mdzad pa de rnams dang / khyad par mkhas pa'i dbang po dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i brgal lan tshangs
pa'i rigs sngags kyi yang lan du/ ngam ring mkhan chen chos rje bzang po bkra shis pas snyan brgyud 'khrul sel zhes bya ba tshigs bcad ma zhig mdzad pa de nyid las/ sgo rum
rnyed dam min yang rung / /mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje bas/ /bla ma bcu phrag lhag pa las/ /rje yi bka' 'bum kun gyi lung / /gsan pa gang na'ang de 'dra med/ /sdom rgyun
yod pa'ang bsgrub bya yin/ /gzhan yang mtha' gzhan bkag pas shes/ /des na de 'dra'i cho ga ni/ gsar du gzhan gyi byas par nges/ dbang gi sngon du ljon shing las/ /sems
bskyed cho ga bshad na yang / /phyag len nub par mkhas rnams bzhed/ /ces pa dang / lam 'bras 'chad las gzhan pa'i dus/ /sngon du de 'dra'i sems bskyed kyi/ /cho ga med par
dbang bskur ba/ /khyed rang 'dod pa dran par gyis/ /sta gon 'jug pa'i gnas skabs su/ /sems bskyed gsung phyir dogs 'di med/ /gsum la skyabs 'gro la sogs pa/ /'khrul spong
nyid las ji skad du/ /smon 'jug sems bskyed blangs bar bya/ /de ni gud du blangs kyang rung / /ma blangs kyang ni sta gon gyi/ /skabs su 'byung zhes gsungs pa 'dis/

/dogs gnas kun grol dngos lan no/ /zhes gsungs/ yang sgyi chu ba buddha shrI bas thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyi tshangs pa'i rigs sngags kyi yang lan nor bu'i
phreng ba zhes bya ba mdzad de/ de nyid las/ sngar tshangs pa'i rigs sngags kyi lan de dag gi yang lan du/ sus byas ma nges pa'i chog bsgrigs kyi yi ge de chos rje khu dbon
tsam gyi rjes su byung na de'i steng nas cho ga byas pas na gsung sgros dang bcas pa'i nges pa yongs rigs pa las med pa dang / phyi mo nas byung ba yin na ni rtsa ba
med pa'i yan lag mi rigs pa dang / bar skabs der phyag dpe 'di la rten bya ba'ang med pas na tshangs pa'i rigs sngags kyi de dag ma brtags pa'i lan yin cing / nA ro pa'i
lugs kyi sems bskyed kyi cho ga birWa pa'i lugs kyi snyan brgyud du mi rung bas/ brgyud pa gnyis ldan gyi sems bskyed kyi cho ga de snyan brgyud yin zhes pa'ang gyi nar song
/ bde kye'i dbang gi sngon du yi ge de dang mthun pa'i sems bskyed byed ces pa'ang bstan pa spyi'i babs 'gros la brten nas bsgrigs pa ste/ de ltar na byang sdom gyi sngon
du so thar dgos pas/ skabs der gsol bzhi'i cho gas bsnyen rdzogs re yang 'bogs rigs/ des na sambu Ta las/ skyabs su 'gro ba'i rim pa yis/ /shin tu legs par sbyangs nas
ni/ /sngags dang rgyud kyi rim pa yi/ /gsang ba'i de kho na nyid bsgrags/ /zhes dkyil 'khor du 'jug pa'i sngon du skyabs 'gro dang sems bskyed bya dgos par gsungs kyang
phyag len gyi rim par mi snang / 'on kyang 'gal ba med de/ sta gon gyi skabs

su 'byung bas so/ /des mi rung ba yang min te/ khrid kyi tshe ma gtogs phyag len tal ma la khyed rang kyang mi byed pas so zhes gsungs so/ /de ltar rtsod pa dang rtsod lan
de dag gis so so'i dgongs bzhed kyi snying po blangs na mkhas mchog rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyi dgongs don gyi snying po ni/ rje btsun gyis mdzad par grags pa'i sems bskyed
kyi yi ge'i steng nas sems bskyed 'bogs pa 'di la brgyud pa med pas 'di mi rigs te/ brgyud pa med pa'i rgyu mtshan ngor chen gyis yi ge de gsar du rnyed pas so gsungs par
snang la/ de'i brgal lan dag bshad tshul cung zad mi 'dra yang don gyi snying po kun mthun par/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gis gsar du rnyed pa'i rje btsun gyis mdzad pa'i
sems bskyed kyi yi ge de la lung rgyun med kyang / de'i steng nas sems bskyed phog chog ste gong ma'i gsung dag las dbang gi sngon du sems bskyed byed par bshad cing / bshad
pa bzhin rje btsun nas ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gi bar du rgyun ma chad pa'i sems bskyed kyi phyag len rnam par dag pa yod cing / phyag len de dang mthun pa'i sems bskyed
kyi yi ge su zhig gis byas kyang de'i steng nas sems bskyed 'bogs rung zhing / yi ge de'i brjod bya dang mthun pa'i sems bskyed kyi sdom pa'i brgyud pa med par yang
mi 'gyur la/ dper na rje btsun nas brgyud pa'i kye rdor man ngag lugs kyi dbang thob la ma nyams pa'i rdo rje slob dpon zhig gis dbang chu'i lung ma thob kyang / de'i steng
nas gzhan la dbang de byar rung ba bzhin no/ /de ltar phyag len mdzad pa'i dbang gi

sngon 'gro'i sems bskyed 'di dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed ma yin pas/ dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed ni lam 'bras pa la med ces pa'i dpyad pa la 'brel nus ma byung / yang dbang
gi sngon du sems bskyed zhig mi 'dod na ni shin tu skal ba dman zhing / gong ma'i gsung sogs dang 'gal lo zhes gsungs par rtogs so/ /yang de dag gi yang lan mkhan chen bzang
bkras pa'i bzhed don snying po ni/ sems bskyed kyi yi ge de mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje bas bla ma bcu phrag lhag pa bsten nas gsan pa'i rje btsun gyi bka' 'bum gyi
nang na med pas gsar du gzhan zhig gis byas kyis rje btsun gyi gsung min/ des na yi ge de steng nas sems bskyed byed pa 'di la sdom rgyun yod pa'ang sgrub dgos/ ljon shing
las dbang gi sngon du sems bskyed kyi cho ga bshad na'ang de'i phyag len nub/ gzhan dbang gi sngon 'gro'i sems bskyed gud du blangs kyang rung / ma blangs kyang sta gon
gyi skabs su 'byung ba des chog par 'khrul spong las bshad pas skal ba dman pa'ang ma yin zhing / khrid kyi tshe ma gtogs gzhan du dbang gi sngon du de 'dra'i sems bskyed
khyed rang yang mi byed pa dran par gyis zhes par mngon zhing / yang sgyi chu ba buddha shrI'i gsung de dag gi snying po ni/ brgyud pa gnyis ldan gyi sems bskyed kyi chog
bsgrigs 'di chos rje khu dbon gyi rjes tsam na byung ba yin na gsung sgros tsam 'byung rigs pa las de med/ rjes phyi mo nas byung na rtsa ba med pa'i yan lag mi rigs/
nA ro pa'i lugs birWa pa'i snyan brgyud du mi rung bas snyan brgyud yin zhes pa'ang gyi na

yin/ spyir bde kye'i dbang gi sngon du sems bskyed byed ces pa'ang bstan pa spyi'i babs 'gros la brten nas bsgrigs par snang bas/ de ltar na byang sdom gyi sngon du so thar
dgos pas gsol bzhi'i cho gas bsnyen rdzogs zhig kyang skabs der bya rigs/ des na sambu Ta las/ dkyil 'khor du 'jug gong sems bskyed mdzad par bshad kyang phyag len mi snang
/ 'on kyang skyon med de sta gon gyi skabs su 'byung zhing / des mi rung ba'ang ma yin te/ phyag len tal ma la ngor pa rang yang mi byed pas so zhes par snang ngo / /de
dag la rang gi go tshod kyis rnam dbye cung zad phye na/ ngor lugs la dbang gi sngon du mdzad pa'i sems bskyed kyi sdom pa 'bogs pa'i phyag len 'di sngon nas med cing
sems skyed kyi sdom rgyun yang med par rje rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang pos sgo rum dpe khang nas rnyed pa de nas bzung yi ge de la brten nas gsar du mdzad pa yin na/ mkhas
mchog rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis sems bskyed brgyud pa med pa dang zhes pa'i dpyad pa de 'jug tu rung na'ang / ngor lugs la sems bskyed kyi sdom rgyun yod pa gzhir bcas
shing / dbang gi sngon du sems bskyed 'bogs pa'i phyag len zhig kyang snga mo nas yod 'dug pas/ slar phyag len de dang mthun pa'i yi ge de rnyed pa na yi ge de steng nas
sems bskyed mdzad pas na yi ge de'i lung rgyun med kyang sdom pa'i rgyun med par ma nges te/ dbu ma lugs lta bu'i sems bskyed kyi ngo bo dang / yi ge de'i brjod bya'i sems
bskyed kyi ngo bo la khyad par med pas so/ /de tsam du ma zad rje rdo

rje 'chang gis bstan pa'i rgyun la dgongs pa'i thugs kyi lhag bsam 'di la rang gzhan kun gyis rjes su yi rang dang gus pa'i thal mo snying nas sbyor rigs te/ de'i rgyun mtshan
gyis rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud gong ma phal cher yang phyag len gtso bor de bzhin du mdzad pa'i dgongs bzhed kyang de yin no/ /mkhan chen bzang bkras pas yi
ge de rje btsun gyi gsung min pa'i shes byed du/ mkhan chen shes rdor bas gsan pa'i rje btsun gyi bka' 'bum gyi nang na med pa bkod kyang / ngor lugs la'ang yi ge de la
lung rgyun med par bzhed pas shes byed rnam dag tu 'gro ba dka' zhing / sgyi chu ba buddha shrI'i de ltar na byang sdom gyi sngon du so thar dgos pas skabs der gsol bzhi'i
cho gas bsnyen rdzogs zhig kyang byed rigs zhes dbang gi sngon du byang sdom dang / de'i sngon du so thar dgos pa tsam la dgongs nas byang sdom dang bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom
pa gnyis mtshungs pa bsgre bar mdzad kyang de gnyis mi mtshungs te/ byang chub tu sems bskyed pa sngon du ma song bar dkyil 'khor du 'jug tu mi rung ba ni/ rigs dang
dam tshig ma thob snying rje med/ /de bzhin byang chub sems kyang ma bskyed cing / /sangs rgyas ma dad lha gzhan bsten pa la/ /nga yi gsang sngags bstan na phung bar 'gyur/
/zhes pa la sogs pa rgyud sde phal cher las gsungs shing / byang sdom gyi rten du so thar gyi sdom pa tsam dgos kyang / bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa nges par dgos pa'i bshad
tshod mi snang bas so/ /gnyis pa rjes bzung la grangs nges yod med kyi rnam gzhag ni/ ngor lugs la lam

'bras 'chad pa'i tshe/ slob ma mang po cig car du rjes bzung mdzad pa'i phyag len 'di la dgongs nas/ mus srad pa chen pos/ rjes bzung grangs nges med pa dang / /zhes pa'i rgyas
bshad du/ slob ma brgya phrag mang po la grangs nges med par rjes 'dzin gyi cho ga byed pa ni/ gsang ba spyi rgyud las/ mkhas pas slob ma gcig gam gsum/ /zhes sogs kyi
lung dang 'gal/ dbang gi chu bo las/ dkyil 'khor gcig tu slob ma nyi shu rtsa lnga las lhag pa gzung bar mi bya zhes sogs gong ma'i gzhung dang 'gal/ rjes bzung la grangs
nges med na sta gon la yod pa'i khas len dang 'gal te/ sta gon gyi grangs nges rjes bzung gi grangs nges la ltos/ dbang dus kyi grangs nges sta gon gyi grangs nges la
ltos par spyi rgyud las gsungs pa'i phyir ro zhes rgol bar mdzad do/ /de'i lan la paN chen rin po che'i rnam thar sgo brgyad par/ spyi rgyud kyi rjes 'dzin dang lam 'bras
gzhung ji lta ba'i rjes 'dzin mi mtshungs par bstan pa dang / 'dir spyi rgyud kyi rjes 'dzin khas mi len kyang rjes 'dzin med pa'i nyes pa mi 'byung bar bstan pa dang /
sta gon spyi rgyud kyi rjes 'dzin la ltos na ha cang thal ba dang gsum du mdzad nas rgyas par 'byung ba'i rkang grangs rags pa tsam zhig bkod na/ dang po la slob dpon 'ga'
zhig gi drung du gang zag kha cig dbang zhu 'dod zer na/ gang zag de spyir chos la zhugs ma zhugs/ zhugs kyang nges legs la zhugs ma zhugs/ der zhugs kyang theg chen la
zhugs sam dang / lta ba la yid ches sam/ de ches na

rdo rje theg pa'i snod du rung mi rung rnams brtags nas rim gyis bkri/ de zin pa'i tshe slob dpon gyis rjes su bzung / lhag pa'i lhas bsrung ba byas/ slob dpon la mkho ba'i
yo byad bstab tu gzhug pa de tsam la slob ma rjes 'dzin gyi cho gar spyi rgyud las bshad la/ tshul de lta bu ni deng sang lam 'bras 'chad pa'i slob ma rjes 'dzin gyi ming
can skabs su babs pa de la mi dgos te/ de ni sems bskyed kyi sdom pa phog pa yan chad la grub cing / de'i rjes su rjes 'dzin gyi ming can sngags lam gyi sa mtshams thog
mar 'dzin pa de'i tshe rjes 'dzin gyi rtogs pa skyes zin pa'i slob ma mang po las nyer lnga rjes su bzung / gzhan dag dor te yid chad du 'jug na spyi rgyud kyi dngos bstan
dang 'gal ba las/ bshad ma thag pa de nyes pa che ba rje bla mas ma dgongs pa min/ ci ste 'gal bar dogs na slar yang rjes 'dzin gyi skabs 'dir snang gsum gyi khrid tshar
gcig phog dgos par 'gyur ro/ /de ltar grangs nges ma byas par rjes 'dzin byas pa la rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor la dgos pa'i yo byad rnams kun gyi thun mong du bsgrubs
pas tshogs rdzogs pa dang bsag sbyong 'phel ba/ slob ma kha cig gzhan du mi 'khyar ba sogs kyi dgos pa shin tu mang ngo / /de'i phyir spyi rgyud nas bshad pa'i rjes 'dzin
dang / ngor lugs kyi rjes 'dzin gyi khyad par ni rjes 'dzin gyi rtogs pa ma skyes pa skyed par byed pa la grangs nges dgos pa dang / skyes zin brtan par byed pa la grangs
nges mi dgos pa gnyis kyis phye ba yin/ de lta na'ang dbang chu chen mo dang mi 'gal te/ dbang chur bshad pa de gzhung ji

lta ba bzhin khrid pa'i tshe kho na dang sbyor rgyu min pas so zhes gsungs/ gnyis pa la/ 'o na de gnyis gang yang ma yin pa'i rjes 'dzin khyod la yod dam med snyam na/ sems
bskyed chen mo byas pa'i phyi nyin de rjes 'dzin gyi phyag len byed pa de sngags kyi thar pa cha mthun/ de nas sngags lam du 'jug pa ni rjes 'dzin dngos te slob ma sta gon
yin cing / chos rje pa yan gyis kyang spyi rgyud kyi slob ma rjes 'dzin gyi dngos gzhi slob ma sta gon nyid la dgongs par gsal te/ nyer lnga las lhag pa rjes su mi bzung
ba'i shes byed du/ de bas lhag pa'i slob ma la/ /cho ga yongs su rdzogs pa ni/ /mtshan mo gcig la tshar mi nus/ /zhes gsungs pa'i phyir/ de dngos gzhi la dgongs pa min
te dngos gzhi nyin mo byas pas cho ga nyams par mi 'gyur ba'i phyir dang / sta gon gcig gis chog pa'i dbang mang po pa dag sngon 'gro dang rjes thun mong bas bsdus pas na
cho ga yongs su rdzogs pa gcig tu 'jog pas de lta bu mtshan thog thag slob ma nyung shas la byas kyang mi tshar ba'i phyir/ slob ma sta gon la mi mtshungs ste slob ma sta
gon gyi cho ga'i mgo nyi ma nub pa nas bzung sang nyi ma ma shar gong du zin pa dgos pa'i phyir te/ de phyir khyed rnams theg chen du/ /sang ni rab tu skye bar 'gyur/
/zhes gsungs dgos pa dang / rmi lam brtag dgos pas so/ /des na snang gsum gyi khrid zin pa dag la spyi rgyud nas bshad pa'i rjes 'dzin mi dgos pa dang / las dang po pa gzhan
la dgos pa'i khyad par yod/ de'i tshe so skye'i rdo rje slob dpon gyis nyer lnga las lhag pa

rjes su 'dzin nus kyang / skabs der mi 'dzin pa ni gong ma'i dgongs pa'o zhes gsungs/gsum pa dbang dang sta gon rjes bzung la ltos na ha cang thal ba la spyi rgyud pa la ha
cang thal ba dang / lam 'bras pa la ha cang thal ba gnyis su mdzad nas/ dang po la khyed kyis drangs pa'i/ gal te rjes bzung byas gyur pa/ /'ga' zhig der ni ma 'ong na/
/de yis gzugs brnyan skyin por gzhug /ces dang / sta gon gnas su ma 'ong na/ /gzhan dag de yi skyin por gzhug /ces dang / sta gon gnas pa 'ga' zhig ni/ /dbang gi dus su med
gyur na/ /gzhan la dbang bskur bya ba min/ /zhes pa'i lung sgra ji bzhin par bshad pa'i tshe nang 'gal 'byung ste/ rjes bzung gi dus kyi slob ma sta gon gyi tshe ma tshang
yang skyin po bcug pas chog na sta gon gyi grangs nges rjes bzung la ltos pa 'gal/ dbang dus su sta gon gyi slob ma gcig nas nyer gsum gyi bar du ma tshang na'ang lhag
ma zung du ma gyur pa la dbang bskur bas chog na dbang gi grangs nges sta gon la ltos pa 'gal/ dgag dgos kyi tshe nyer bzhi la bskur bas chog na de'i tshe nyi shu rtsa
bzhi la sta gon byas pas chog par 'gyur ro/ /gzhan yang sta gon dus su gzugs brnyan dang skyin po gnyis la dbang bskur byed rung ma yin na ni sta gon thob par 'gal/ de'ang
ma thob na ni skyin por bcug pa la dgos pa med/ nyer lnga'i grangs tshang ba tsam dang / sta gon byed pa'i nyes pa khegs zer na/ 'o na dbang dus su'ang sta gon ma byas
pa gzhan zhig gis kha bskangs rigs te grangs de tshang ba la phan

pas so/ /yang rjes bzung gi slob ma zhig rkyen gyis ma slebs par gzugs brnyan bcug pa des dngos de'i go chod dam mi chod/ mi chod na bcug pa'i dgos pa ci/ go chod na gzugs
brnyan de la sta gon byas pas thob bam mi thob/ mi thob na go chod pa 'gal/ thob na de dngos su 'gyur ro gsungs nas/ rang gis lung de dag gi don rkyen dgos kyi tshe kha 'chams
la dbang bskur byas chog pa dang / rjes bzung gi skabs su med kyang rjes 'dzin gyi yon tan dang ldan pa gzhan dag kyang sta gon byas nas dbang bskur chog pa'i don dang
/ bye brag tu gzugs brnyan la sta gon byas pa ni/ slob ma 'ga' zhig tshe'i dus byas pa la dgongs te/ slob dpon snying rje chen po dang ldan pas gzugs brnyan de la'ang
dbang bskur bas sdig pa 'dag pa sogs kyis dgos pa yod cing / 'di la bsams nas bod du rjes bzung gi slob ma yul gzhan du song ba sogs lus srog dang tshangs spyod kyi bar
chad byung dogs pa'i tshe gzugs brnyan la shes pa bkug nas dbang bskur byed pa sogs kyi lag len byung bar snang ngo gsungs/ lam 'bras pa la ha cang thal ba la khyed kyis
bla ma dam pa'i dgongs par byas nas snang gsum gyi sngon du dbang byed pa/ de'i sngon du rjes bzung dang sta gon byed pa gzhir bcas/ rjes bzung yang dbang chu chen mo nas
bshad pa de las gzhan khyed la med pas/ de ltar na thog mar dal 'byor rnyed dka' nas don dam sems bskyed la thug gi bar ji lta ba bzhin bskyed du bcug nas/ de la rjes 'dzin
gyi cho ga phyag len bzhin byed

dgos/ de byas na ni snang gsum gyi khrid tshar gnyis zlos pa can du 'bogs dgos par 'gyur ro zhes gsungs/ yang gong gi mus srad pa chen po'i gsung de'i lan du thams cad mkhyen
pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis tshangs pa'i rigs sngags su rjes 'dzin gyi rnam gzhag spyir bstan pa dang / skabs don gyi dngos lan 'phros dang bcas pa gnyis su mdzad/ dang
po la spyi rgyud kyi rjes 'dzin gyi rnam gzhag dang / lam 'bras pa'i rjes 'dzin bshad pa/ gnyis ka ltar yang rgol ba la 'gal ba ste gsum du mdzad nas shin tu rgyas par
'byung ba rnams cung zad bsdus te bkod na/ dang po la spyi rgyud las/ las kun byed pa'i gsang sngags kyi/ de las slob ma yongs su bzung / /bu mo gzhon nus bkal ba'i skud/
/blangs nas bzhi bcu rtsa dgur bzlas/ /slob ma rnams ni blos bsam nas/ /mnyam par bzhag pas mdud pa bor/ /de ltar slob ma yongs bzung nas/ /las la bgegs ni med par 'gyur/
/zhes pas slob ma rjes bzung dngos dang / sang ni dkyil 'khor bri ba yi/ /zhes sogs kyis sta gon gyi sbyor ba dang lha sta gon sogs/ de nas slob ma legs brtags te/ /zhes
sogs kyis slob ma'i mtshan nyid dang kun slong gi bsam pa/ mkhas pas slob ma gcig gam gsum/ /zhes pa nas/ sta gon gnas par brtsam par bya/ /zhes pa'i bar gyis slob ma'i
grangs dang lus kyi spyod lam/ dang po gsum la skyabs su btang / /zhes sogs kyis slob ma sta gon gyi cho ga dngos bstan pa yin no gsungs/ gnyis pa la dbang chu las dbang
bskur don du

gnyer ba'i slob ma la/ sngar gsang sngags la zhugs pa dang / theg chen la zhugs pa dang / nyan thos la sogs pa'i lam la zhugs pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la ma zhugs
pa dang bzhi las/ dang po gnyis la de ma thag rjes bzung byar rung ba dang / gsum pa la bzhi pa'i nang tshan gzhan du rdzogs byang 'dod pa dang / nges legs tsam 'dod pa
rnams la dpon slob 'brel brtags te sems bskyed nas rjes su bzung bar bshad cing / gang zag tha ma mngon mtho tsam don du gnyer ba yin na de ma thag rjes bzung mi bya bar
thun mong ba'i lam gyis blo rim gyis sbyangs te sems bskyed la/ gzod rjes bzung gi ming can slob mas gsol ba gdab pa dang / slob dpon gyis ting nge 'dzin gyis bsrung ba dang
/ bsnyen pa'i stabs su gzhug pa rnams bya bar bshad zhes gsungs/ gsum pa la rgol ba khyod kyi rjes bzung la spyi rgyud las bshad pa'i slob ma la sngags dang ting nge
'dzin dang / srung skud btags te srung ba byed pa sogs tshang bar byed pa'i srol med pa dang / der grangs nges dgos pa'i dmigs bsal ma bshad pa la grangs nges 'dod pas khyed
kyi de spyi rgyud lugs kyi rjes 'dzin yang ma yin/ slob ma'i rigs brtags pa'i sgo nas thun mong ba'i lam gyis rgyud sbyangs dgos pa'i gang zag tha ma rnams rim can pa'i
lam gyis rgyud sbyang ba sogs byas nas/ gzod dbang bskur ba de khyed kyi rjes bzung gi lag len la med pas lam 'bras kyi lugs kyi rjes bzung yang min gsungs/ don tshan
gnyis pa skabs don gyi dngos lan

'phros don dang bcas pa la/ phyogs snga ma'i 'dod pa skyon med du bstan pa dang / rgol ba'i grub mtha' rtsa ba nas mi rung bar bstan pa dang gnyis su mdzad nas/ dang po la/
'o na khyed rang gi rjes bzung lugs gnyis po de gang gi rjes su 'brang / dang po ltar na ni skyon de dag khyed la'ang mtshungs/ gnyis pa ltar na grangs nges med pa'i skyon
de so na gnas so zhe na/ kho bo cag rje btsun gong mas bshad pa ltar 'dod la/ de'i khungs kyang sambu Ta las/ slob mas pus mo'i lha nga ni/ /zhes sogs kyis bstan par ljon
shing las bshad pas/ spyi rgyud kyi dngos bstan dang cung zad ma mthun yang nyes pa chen po med cing / dbang chur grangs nges su bshad pa de spyi khyab tu mi sbyor bas
lung rigs gnyis kyi sgo nas dbang chu dang 'gal ba'i nyes pa spangs sla ste/ lung ni rnam snang mngon bya las/ gcig gnyis bzhi las lhag kyang rung / dpyad mi dgos par gzung
bar bya/ /zhes dang / slob dpon snying rje chen po dang ldan pa sems can gyi khams ma lus pa bsgral ba'i dbang du byas te/ des byang chub kyi sems kyi rgyur 'gyur bar
bya ba'i phyir slob ma tshad med pa bzung bar bya'o zhes gsungs pa dang mthun par/ slob ma dbang bskur la grangs nges dgos pa'i dmigs bsal du sbyor bas dbang chu dang yang
mi 'gal/ gal te lung de dag dbang chur rjes bzung gi skabs su drangs pas dbang gi grangs nges kyi dmigs bsal min zer na/ lung phyi ma de'ang 'phags pa rin po che'i brtag
gnyis kyi TIkka snying po gsal bar rjes 'dzin gyi skabs su drangs pas

kun du mtshungs/ yang grangs nges yod pa'i khas len dang 'gal zer ba de ci/ dbang la grangs nges yod na rjes bzung la grangs nges yod par su zhig gis khas blangs/ sems rnal
du 'dug la smros shig gzhan yang spyi rgyud las/ slob ma yongs su bzung ba gang / /sta gon gnas tshe med na ni/ /de yi gzugs brnyan bris nas ni/ /ji skad bshad pa thams
cad bya/ /zhes dang / slob ma yongs su bzung ba gang / /der ni 'ong bar ma gyur na/ /gzhan dag de yi skyin por gzhug /ces gsungs pa'i don ji ltar 'chad/ gzugs brnyan nam
skyin po gang rung ba de la rjes bzung byed dam mi byed/ byed na de la dbang yang logs su bya dgos par 'gyur te/ dbang gi grangs nges sta gon dang / sta gon gyi grangs nges
rjes bzung la ltos shing / rjes gzung gi tshe gzugs brnyan nam skyin po de las med pas so/ gal te snga ma rnams kyi grangs tshang ba'i phyir bsnan pa yin no zhe na/ kho
bo cag la rung yang khyed la 'gal te/ rjes bzung gi grangs dang sta gon gyi grangs ma mthun pa'i skyon 'dug pas so/ /de la rjes bzung mi byed na sta gon gyi grangs nges
rjes bzung la ltos pa 'gal te/ rjes bzung la med pa'i slob ma zhig sta gon la 'dug pas so gsungs nas/ rang gi bzhed pa spyi rgyud kyi tshigs bcad dang po'i don slob ma 'ga'
zhig tshe'i dus byas nas med pa lta bu la/ de'i gzugs brnyan byas nas rnam shes bkug ste sta gon sogs bya ba dang / tshigs bcad phyi mas slob ma kha cig rkyen dgos kyi
ma slebs pa lta bu la dbang gi snod

rung gzhan skyin por bcug pa la sta gon dang dbang bskur sogs byas chog pa'i don yin pas/ slob ma rjes 'dzin ma byas kyang dbang bskur byas chog pa'i dmigs bsal gyi lung yin/
spyir yang gzugs brnyan de la rjes 'dzin nges par dgos na/ rje btsun gyi gzhan phan bdud rtsi las/ dbang bskur te sdig pa sbyong tshul rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum gsungs pa'i
gsum ka la gshin po la rjes 'dzin bya dgos pa ma bshad pa mi 'thad par 'gyur/ yang gong du lung rigs gnyis kyi sgo nas skyon spong gsungs pa'i rigs pa la slob dpon gyi
dbang slob ma re re nas byed pa'i maNDal dang gsol gdab sogs slob ma thams cad kyis cig car bya rung bar bshad pa'i rigs pas/ dbang la grangs nges yod kyang rjes bzung
la grangs nges ma byas pa la nyes pa med pa shes te/ rjes bzung gi don slob mas gsol ba gdab pa dang / bla mas dbang skur ba la gtso bor 'dod par sambu Ta'i lung des shes
pas so/ /gzhan du na khyed rang la slob ma re re nas rjes bzung dang sta gon bya dgos par 'gyur te/ dbang gi gtso bo rdo rje slob dpon gyi dbang re re nas skur dgos pa gang
zhig dbang gi grangs nges sta gon dang / sta gon gyi de rjes bzung la ltos dgos pa'i phyir zhes gsungs/ spyi rgyud las grangs nges su bshad pa ni slob ma sta gon nyid
la dgongs par mngon te/ gzhung gi sa mtshams slob ma sta gon gyi skabs su 'byung ba dang / nyer lnga las lhag pa cig car bzung na mtshan mo gcig la tshar mi nub par bshad
pa'i rigs pas so/ /rjes 'dzin ni mtshan mo dgos pa'i dmigs bsal

med la/ yod kyang mi tshar ba'i dogs pa skye don med pa'i phyir ro/ /sta gon la ni mi mtshungs te slob ma sta gon gyi cho ga'i 'go nyi ma nub pa nas brtsams mtshan phyed tshun
la tshar dgos pas so/ /de phyir khyed rnams theg chen du/ /sang ni rab tu skye bar 'gyur/ /zhes pa'i tshig bshad du yod pa dang / rmi lam brtag dgos pa'i phyir ro zhes
sogs dang / kho bo cag gi rang lugs ni 'phags pa rin po che'i rtsa rgyud kyi TIkkar spyi rgyud kyi dgongs pas grangs nges yod pa dang / rnam snang mngon byang gi dgongs

chu ba buddha shrI ba'i nor bu'i phreng ba las tshangs pa'i rigs sngags kyi bzhed pa rags pa tsam zhig bkod pa'i rjes su/ yang lan dngos la legs par rna ba blags te gsan

te/ dbang bskur gyi grangs ka tshang ba'i phyir rjes bzung byas pa tshe'i dus byas pa de nyid kyi rten la cho ga bya dgos pa byung ba yin pas so/ /gzu bor gnas pa'i blo

/ skyes zin brtan par byed pa gnyis kyi sgo nas phye ba yin zhing / de'i tshe snga ma la grangs nges dgos pa dang / phyi ma la mi dgos pas spyi rgyud dang ni bshad tshul

med/ gzhan yang tshangs pa'i rig sngags su spyi rgyud las rjes 'dzin la grangs nges dgos pa'i dmigs bsal med gsungs pa dang / 'phags pa'i rtsa rgyud kyi TIkkar spyi rgyud
kyi dgongs pas grangs nges yod pa dang / rnam snang mngon byang gi dgongs pas grangs med pa gnyis char rjes 'dzin gyi skabs su bshad pas 'gal med du khas len gsungs
pa gnyis khas blang nang 'gal gsung bar snang la/ sgyi chu ba buddha shrI'i gsung de dag gi snying po ni phal cher bzang bkras pa'i de dang mtshungs la/ gnod byed kyi rigs
pa la ngor lugs la spyi rgyud kyi rjes 'dzin gyi lag len de med

cing / lam 'bras kyi rjes 'dzin gyi grangs nges de med pas/ rjes 'dzin de gnyis char ngor lugs la med par song / rnam snang mngon byang gi lung de ne spyod rgyud la grangs
nges mi dgos pa dang / rgyud sde gzhan gsum la grangs nges dgos pa'i lung dang / slob ma rjes su bzung ba gang / /zhes sogs kyis kyang rjes 'dzin grangs med la byed pa bkag
gsung bar snang ngo / /yang paN chen rin po che'i legs bshad gser thur gyi dri bar/ gsang ba spyi rgyud dag las ni/ /dkyil 'khor dag tu dbang bskur ba'i/ /slob ma gnyis
dang bzhi la sogs/ /zung du bshad pa 'ga' zhig yod/ /ces pa dang / spyod pa'i rgyud kyi dbang skur la/ /slob ma grangs nges med gyur na/ /gcig nas bcu yi bar dag gi /grangs
nges mdzad pa ji ltar yin/ /gsang ba spyi rgyud lung gis ni/ /rjes bzung cho gas slob ma rnams/ /rjes 'dzin dus kyi slob ma yi/ /grangs nges bstan pa ma yin nam/ /zhes
gsungs nas/ dri ba dang po'i rang lan du/ spyi rgyud kyi dgongs pa ni rjes 'dzin dang sta gon gyi dus su nyer lnga man chad kyis grangs kha yar ba ci yod thabs gcig tu
tshogs pa la rjes 'dzin dang sta gon yongs su rdzogs par byas nas/ dbang dngos gzhi slob ma re re nas byed pa yin/ sta gon gyi tshe ni thams cad cig car 'tshogs dgos te
ma tshang na skyin po dang / de'ang ma 'byor na gzugs brnyan byas nas sta gon byed dgos te/ spyi rgyud las/ slob ma yongs su bzung ba gang / /sta gon gnas tshe med na ni/
/de yi gzugs brnyan byas nas su/ /ji skad bshad pa'i las

rnams bya/ /slob ma yongs su bzung ba gang / /gal te rkyen 'ga' zhig gis ni/ /der ni 'ong bar ma gyur na/ /gzhan dag de yi skyin por gzhug /ces gsungs so/ /'di'ang rjes bzung
gi slob ma dngos gzhi'i dus gtan mi sleb pa'i dbang du byas pa ni min pa 'dra ste/ yin na de dag la sta gon byas pa la dgos pa med pa'i phyir/ grangs tshang ba kho na'i
ched yin na ni rjes bzung gi dus las gnyis dang / bzhi dang / drug dang / brgyad la sogs pa ma tshang na skyin po gzhug mi dgos par 'gyur ro/ /'o na skyin po la sta gon
byas pa'i dgos pa ci zhe na/ sta gon gyi tshe skyin po bcug nas/ dngos gzhi'i dus su rang nyid kyis dbang blang chog pa'i rgyu mtshan gyis yin te/ de las gzhan du skyin
po de la dbang bskur ba yin na ni/ gzugs brnyan de la'ang dbang skur bar thal ba'i phyir dang / rjes su ma bzung ba zhig la dbang bskur bar thal ba'i phyir ro/ 'di'ang bya
ba'i rgyud du sta gon gyi chos nyung ngu zhig gis chog pa'i dbang du byas sam snyam ste dpyad par bya'o zhes dang / gnyis pa'i rang lan du/ spyod pa'i rgyud kyi dbang bskur
la/ /slob ma kha 'chams kha yar gyi/ /nges pa med mod grangs med min/ /bcu las lhag pa bkag phyir ro/ /de lta na yang rjes bzung gi /slob ma'i grangs la nges pa med/
slob dpon snying rje chen po yis/ /tshad med bzung zhes gsungs phyir ro/ /zhes lan 'debs te/ rnam snang mngon byang las/ 'on kyang slob dpon snying rje chen po dang ldan
pas zhes sogs drangs nas/ de ltar na gzhung 'di ltar

du/ spyod pa'i rgyud kyi dbang bskur la/ /slob ma rjes bzung grangs nges med/ /lhag ma dmigs bsal mdzad pa yin/ /zhes sbyar na bde gsungs/ spyi rgyud dang mngon byang gi rjes
'dzin la grangs nges yod med ni brtags nas rjes su 'dzin pa dang / rjes su bzung nas brtag pa'i khyad par du snang ngo / /dkyil 'khor du 'jug pa la ni brtag mi dgos par
grangs med rjes su bzung bas chog ste/ de nyid 'dus pa las/ dkyil 'khor chen po 'dir 'jug pa la snod du gyur ma gyur brtag mi 'tshal lo zhes gsungs pas so zhes pa dang
/ dri ba gsum pa'i rang lan du spyi rgyud las/ rjes 'dzin la nyer lnga man chad kyi grangs nges mdzad pa de dbang chu'i dgongs par gdon mi za'o/ bla ma rnams kyi phyag len
du mdzad pa ni mngon byang las gsungs pa ltar byang chub sems kyi rgyur 'gyur ba'i dgos pa khyad par can la dgongs nas grangs nges ma mdzad pa'am/ yang na rdul tshon gyi
dkyil 'khor gcig tu bsgrub cing mchod pa dang / bdag nyid 'jug cing dbang blang ba'i cho ga tshar gcig las mi mdzad pa'i dbang du byas nas rjes bzung gi grangs nyer lnga
las lhag pa ma bshad do zhes kyang bsam par bya'o zhes gsungs/ glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub kyis rjes 'dzin byas pa'i slob ma ji tsam tshang yang lhag ma rnams
la dbang bskur ba'i tshe sta gon gyi skabs su grangs nges yod pa re byas nas de dag la dbang gi dngos gzhi bskur ba shin tu'ang rung zhing slob ma rjes 'dzin gzhan 'os pa
ci rigs pa la byed pa'am/ slob ma rjes 'dzin ma byas pa la'ang sta gon gyi cho ga byas nas

dbang bskur ba bya rung zhing / rjes 'dzin byas pa'i slob ma sta gon gyi dus su med pa la'ang yod bzhin du ma 'dzom pa dang / shi nas med pa sogs du ma 'byung bas lhag ma rnams
la dbang ma bskur bar lam bstan du rung ba ni ma yin no/ /kha 'chams la dbang bskur byas na skye la nyes byas yin zer ba ni skye la nyes byas dang nyes med kyi tha snyad
rnams 'dul ba la grags kyi/ gsang sngags la sbyar na lham dpe zhwa la bkab pa las ma 'das lags zhes rab 'byams pa blo gros rab gsal gyi dris lan las gsungs so/ /yang
bdag gi bla ma mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags kyis sdom gsum rnam bshad kyi 'phros don las/ kun mkhyen dang paN chen gyi bzhed pa bkod pa'i rjes su/
zung du ma gyur slob ma gang / /zhes pa slob ma rjes bzung yin pa thugs mad de/ /de ltar slob ma rjes bzung tshar ba rnams sta gon bya ran pa'i tshe 'ga' zhig med zin pa'am
ma slebs pa la gzugs brnyan 'dri ba dang tshab bcug nas kha skong bar gsungs pas kyang shes nus pa'i phyir/ de'ang rgyud las/ slob ma yongs su bzung ba gang / sta gon
gnas tshe med na ni/ /de yi gzugs brnyan byas nas su/ /ji skad bshad pa'i las rnams bya/ /slob ma yongs su bzung ba gang / /gal te rkyen 'ga' zhig gis ni/ /der ni 'ong
bar ma gyur na/ /gzhan dag de yi skyin por gzhug /ces gsungs te/ rjes 'dzin tshar ba'i slob ma sta gon gyi gong du tshe phyi mar 'phos tshar na de'i byang bu lta bu la dgug
zhugs byas te dbang gral der bzhag nas sta gon

dang dngos gzhi'i dbang bskur bas kha skong zhing kho'i sdig sbyong du 'gyur ba dang / gal te na ba'am phyogs che ge mor 'gro dgos byung ba'i rkyen gyis ma sleb pa la na rjes
'dzin ma byas kyang tshab gzhan bos nas sta gon bya ba yin no/ /dgos pa ni kha skong ba'i ched dang / dngos gzhi'ang tshab de nyid la bskur bas de nyid kyis dbang thob
par 'gyur la/ sta gon la ma sleb pa la de'i dngos gzhi bya mi rung ngo / /yang sta gon byas pa dngos gzhi la med pa'am ma sleb na ji tsam tshogs pa de la dngos gzhi bskur
gyi/ gzugs brnyan dang tshab ni mi bya ste/ spyi rgyud kyi lung sngar drangs pa'i 'phros las/ sta gon gnas pa byas pa la/ /gal te der ni ma 'ongs na/ /bla ma blo ldan mkhas
pa yis/ /der ni slob ma gzhan mi bzung / /zhes gsungs pa'i phyir/ paN chen gyis rjes 'dzin gyi slob ma dngos gzhi la sleb nges pa'i dbang du byas nas gzugs brnyan dang
skyin po bcug pa yin gyi/ gzhan du na gzugs brnyan dang skyin po la sta gon byas pa la dgos pa med gsung ba ni rgyud tshig de dag gi don la thugs g.yel bar zad do/ /de
ltar spyi rgyud kyi lung des slob ma rjes bzung bstan yang / rjes 'dzin gyi grangs kyis dbang dus kyi grangs kyang 'grub pa yin te/ rjes bzung grangs ji tsam dang mthun
par phyis dbang yang grangs de dag la bskur ba yin pa'i phyir/ deng sang lam 'bras pa phal cher slob ma rjes 'dzin la grangs nges mi mdzad pa ni phyag len zor bde ba tsam
ste/ phyag len dog par byas na lam 'bras dang ma 'brel yang slob ma rjes 'dzin dang bsnyen pa kha gso dgos so

zhes gsungs la/ de ltar mkhas pa'i bzhed srol rnam grangs mang po zhig bshad pa de dag la rang gis go tshod kyis rnam dbye cung zad phye na/ mkhas mchog rdo rje rgyal mtshan
gyis dbang gi sta gon dang dngos gzhi'i slob ma la grangs nges yod na slob ma rjes 'dzin la yang grangs nges dgos gsung pa 'di spyir btang la rgyud sde'i dgongs par gnas
te/ spyi rgyud las/ mkhas pas slob ma gcig gam gsum/ /lnga 'am yang na bdun dag gam/ /nyi shu rtsa ni lnga yi bar/ /zung du ma gyur slob ma bzung / /de bas lhag pa'i slob
ma ni/ /yongs su bzung ba mi shes so/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / dbang chu chen mor/ de ltar 'brel pa brtags nas mtshan nyid dang ldan pa'i slob ma gcig nas nyi shu rtsa lnga'i
bar grangs kha yar ba gzung bar bya'i/ de bas lhag pa dkyil 'khor gcig tu gzung bar mi bya ste zhes gsungs nas/ spyi rgyud kyi lung de 'dren par mdzad pa dang / khyad
par chos rje sa skya paNTi ta chen po'i sdom gsum rab dbyer/ sngags kyi dbang bskur byed pa na/ /grangs nges med par dbang bskur byed/ /'di ni rdo rje 'chang gis bkag
/spyod pa'i rgyud kyi dbang skur la/ /slob ma grangs nges med par gsungs/ /lhag ma dmigs bsal mdzad pa yi/ /slob ma la ni grangs nges yod/ /ces spyod rgyud kyi dbang la grangs
nges med pa dmigs bsal dang / lhag ma rgyud sde gzhan gsum gyi dbang la grangs nges yod pas/ grangs nges med par dbang bskur byed pa bkag pa'i shes byed du/ mkhas pas
slob ma gcig gam

gsum/ /zhes sogs gcig nas nyer lnga'i bar grangs kha 'chams dang / de bas lhag pa la rjes bzung mi byed par ston pa'i spyi rgyud kyi lung de 'dren par mdzad pas so/ /yang rjes
bzung gi grangs nges des sta gon gyi grangs nges kyang 'grub pa la dgongs nas rjes bzung nyer lnga las lhag pa mi rung ba'i shes byed du/ de bas lhag pa'i slob ma la/
/zhes sogs nyer lnga las lhag pa la byas na cho ga yongs rdzogs mtshan mo gcig la tshar mi nus pa sogs dbang la sbyar nas gsungs pas so/ /de las gzhan du rjes bzung gi grangs
kyis sta gon dang dbang gi grangs mi 'grub na dbang bskur nyer lnga las lhag pa mi rung ba'i sgrub byed du nyer lnga las lhag pa rjes su mi bzung ba'i spyi rgyud kyi
lung dang / rjes bzung de las lhag pa la mi rung ba'i shes byed du dbang gi cho ga mtshan mo gcig la mi tshar ba rnams 'brel mar gsung ba la rnam dpyad med par 'gyur bas
so/ /paN chen rin po che dang thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis nyer lnga las lhag pa la cho ga mtshan mo gcig la tshar mi nus pa 'di slob ma sta gon gyi dbang
du byas pa yin te/ rjes bzung ni mtshan phyed tshun la mi tshar ba'i dogs pa skye don med la/ slob ma sta gon gyi cho ga'i mgo nyi ma nub pa nas brtsam mtshan phyed tshun
la tshar dgos shing / de'ang rmi lam brtag dgos pa sogs kyi gnad kyis yin pas so zhes bzhed la/ glo bo mkhan chen rin po che la rab 'byams pa blo gros rab gsal gyis
dbang nyi ma nub pa nas nyi ma ma shar gyi bar la mdzad par gsungs pa la/ deng sang nyin bar mdzad pa la lung rigs

gnang dgos zhus pa'i lan du/ rgyud sde nas gsungs pa'i dngos bstan la ji ltar yod pa'i phyag len de rnams da lta dus kyi stobs kyis ji lta ba bzhin du mdzad pa rgya bod kyi
bla ma phyi ma phal cher ba gcig la'ang ma byung 'dug cing / de la lung rigs kyi shes byed gzhan 'god rgyu med kyang / bstan pa dar nub kyi babs la song nas sdom pa gsum
char gyi phyag len gyi rim pa deng sang gi dus su cha mtshungs pa tsam la gtso bor byed dgos pa yin nam snyam pa byung lags/ 'di tsam du ma zad dbang bskur yul dang / bskur
ba po slob dpon dang / ji ltar bskur ba'i cho ga'i gnad che ba kun du yang legs par dpyad na ji ltar yod dgongs par bzhugs shing / dus skabs 'di 'dra ba la dgongs nas/
sdom gsum rab dbye las/ des na nyan thos bstan pa ni/ /nub kyang gzugs brnyan tsam zhig snang / /rdo rje theg pa'i bstan pa la/ /gzugs brnyan tsam yang mi snang ngo / /zhes
gsungs par go lags zhes bshad do/ /yang ngor lugs kyi bla ma dag slob ma mang po dus gcig la rjes 'dzin gyi phyag len mdzad pa'i dgongs don ni/ de ltar byas pa la nyes
pa med cing phyag len zor bde ba dang / rnam snang mngon byang du rjes 'dzin grangs med bshad pa de dmigs bsal du bzhed pa yin pas rjes 'dzin la grangs nges med kyang
slob ma sta gon dang dngos gzhi gnyis la grangs nges mdzad pa 'di ni rgyud sde zab mo'i dgongs don tshul bzhin du dgongs pa'i phyag len du snang la/ ci ste rgyud kyi spyir
btang gi bshad tshod kun nges par dgos na rgyud sde

gong ma gnyis dang bya rgyud kyi dbang la spyir btang nyer lnga man chad kyi grangs nges dgos pa kun mthun mod/ 'on kyang dmigs bsal la spyi rgyud las/ sta gon gnas par byas
pa la/ /gal te rkyen gyis ma 'ongs na/ /bla ma blo ldan mkhas pa yis/ /der ni slob ma gzhan mi bzung / /zhes slob ma nyer lnga la sta gon byas pa'i gcig lta bu ma tshang
na gzhan mi 'jug par nyer bzhi la dbang bskur bas chog par bshad pa'i phyir ro/ /thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis brgal lan tshangs pa'i rig sngags las rjes
'dzin gyi slob ma'i grangs nges rnam snang mngon byang dang mthun par khas len pa de'i tshe'ang / dbang bskur gyi slob ma'i grangs nges spyi rgyud nas bshad pa ltar 'dod
pas zhes 'byung bas/ ngor lugs kyi rjes 'dzin la grangs nges med pa 'di rnam snang mngon byang gi dgongs pa bzhin mdzad par rtogs so/ /rgyu mtshan des na rdzong lugs kyi
bzhed pa 'di rgyud sde spyir btang gi bshad tshul phyag len dog phyogs nas bstan pa la dgongs shing / ngor lugs kyi bzhed pa 'di rgyud sde'i dmigs bsal gyi bshad tshul
phyag len yang phyogs la dgongs par snang bas phyogs gnyis char rgyud sde'i dgongs pa dang mi 'gal zhing 'thad ldan du kho bos legs par rtogs so/ /paN chen rin po che'i dri
ba de dag la kun mkhyen chen pos sdom gsum 'khrul spong du dri ba phyi ma gnyis la lan ma mdzad la/ dang po'i lan du spyi rgyud las/ bla mas slob ma gcig pu ni/ /dkyil
'khor dag tu dbang bskur bya/ /mkhas pas cig car slob ma gnyis/ /dbang bskur ba ni

yongs mi bya/ /gsum mam gnyis sam bzhi yang rung / /bla mas dbang bskur byas na ni/ /yo byad gsar pa gzhan rnams kyis/ /thams cad so so so sor bya/ /rigs lnga'i dbang ni thob
pa la/ /bsgrub pa'i dkyil 'khor dbang bskur bya/ /dbang bskur pa yi cho ga dang / /bsgrub pa'i cho ga de bzhin bya/ /zhes gsungs pa la 'khrul pa 'dra/ gzhan slob ma gnyis
dang bzhi dkyil 'khor du 'jug pa ston pa'i tshig rgyud der med/ lung de'i don ni sta gon dang 'jug pa dang / chu dang cod paN gyi dbang rnams gcig nas nyi shu rtsa lnga'i
bar zung du ma gyur pa la cig car byas nas bsgrub pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi dbang bskur bya ba'i tshe slob ma gcig kho na la bya ba yin gyis/ gnyis dang gsum dang bzhi la
sogs pa cig car mi rung bar rgyud der gsal bar gsungs la/ gal te du ma la bya dgos na yo byad gsar pa sbyar nas re re bzhin so sor bya bar gsungs bzhin du/ de'i don gnyis
dang bzhi la sogs pa slob ma zung du gyur pa cig car 'jug pa la 'chad pa ni blo gros rtsing pa yin zhes gsung ba tsam mdzad/ drangs ma thag pa'i spyi rgyud kyi lung de'i
don la mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa'i gsung las/ bla mas slob ma gcig pu ni/ /dkyil 'khor dag tu dbang bskur bya/ /zhes pa nas/ thams cad so so so sor bya/ /zhes pa'i
bar gyis bstan pa'i dbang dang / bsgrub pa'i dkyil 'khor dbang bskur bya/ /zhes pa'i dbang gnyis mi gcig ste bsgrub pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi dbang ni/ thams cad so so so sor
bya/ /zhes pa'i

dbang gi rjes la bya ba yin pa'i phyir/ de'i dbang bskur tshul dang dkyil 'khor bsgrub tshul rnams dbang snga ma de bzhin du bya bar gsungs pas snga phyi rim can du bstan pa'i
phyir/ gzhan du na/ bsgrub pa'i dkyil 'khor dbang bskur bya/ /zhes pa'i 'phros las/ dbang bskur ba yi cho ga dang / /bsgrub pa'i cho ga'ang de bzhin bya/ /zhes gsungs
pa'i don ji ltar 'chad de/ de bzhin snyeg mtshams dgos so zhes pa dang / bla mas slob ma gcig pu ni/ /dkyil 'khor dag tu dbang bskur bya/ /zhes pa nas/ thams cad so so so
sor bya/ /zhes pa'i don ni spyir btang dbang phal cher la de ltar du ma nges kyang / bya rgyud rang lugs kyi dbang 'ga' zhig bskur ba na slob ma gnyis sam gsum sogs su
yod pa la dkyil 'khor bsgrub pa'ang lan grangs de bzhin du bya zhing / slob ma'ang dang por gcig kho na la dbang bskur/ de nas yang mchod pa'i yo byed sogs gsar pa bshams
nas cig shos la bskur ba sogs slob ma ji tsam yod pa ma rdzogs kyi bar du de ltar bya ba'i phyag len 'ga' zhig yod pa bstan te/ spyi rgyud nyid las/ slob ma re re nas bkug
ste/ /bsang gtor snga ma bzhin byas la/ /zhes dang / slob ma gcig nas bkug nas ni/ /cho ga bzhin du yon phul te/ /cho ga shes par bsang gtor bya/ /zhes gsungs pa'i phyir
zhes 'byung ngo / /yang paN chen rin po ches rjes 'dzin gyi slob ma dngos gzhi la slebs nges pa'i dbang du byas nas gzugs brnyan bcug pa yin gsung ba ni/ rgyud tshig de
dag gi don la thugs g.yel bar zad do zhes bdag gi bla

ma mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa gsungs pa ni thugs mad de/ spyi rgyud kyis/ slob ma yongs su bzung ba gang / /sta gon gnas tshe med na ni/ /de yi gzugs brnyan byas nas su/
/ji skad bshad pa'i las rnams bya/ /zhes pa 'dis rjes bzung la yod pa'i slob ma tshe'i dus byas pa lta bu la gzugs brnyan byed par bstan pas slebs nges pa'i dbang du mdzad
pa ga la yin/ rgyud tshig des slob ma tshe 'phos pa lta bu med par song ba de bstan te/ de'i 'phros las/ slob ma yongs su bzung ba gang / /gal te rkyen 'ga' zhig gis
ni/ /der ni 'ong bar ma gyur na/ /gzhan dag de yi skyin por gzhug /ces pa des tshe 'phos pa lta bu ma yin pa/ rkyen 'ga' zhig gis der ma slebs na skyin po gzhug pa zhig bstan
pa'i phyir/ yang paN chen gyis 'o na skyin po la sta gon byas pa'i dgos pa ci zhe na/ sta gon gyi tshe skyin po bcug nas/ dngos gzhi'i dus rang nyid kyis dbang blang
chog pa'i rgyu mtshan gyis yin te/ de las gzhan du skyin po la dbang bskur ba yin na ni gzugs brnyan de la'ang dbang bskur bar thal ba'i phyir dang / rjes su ma bzung ba
zhig la dbang bskur bar thal ba'i phyir zhes pa'ang 'thad par mi snang te/ gang zag rgyud tha dad pa zhig gis sta gon zhus pa des/ cig shos kyi sta gon ma thob kyang go
chod par byas nas dngos gzhi bskur ba de 'dra rgyud sde'i dgongs pa min zhing / skyin po la sta gon byas nas slar dngos gzhi de nyid la ka bskur du rung ba dang / gzugs brnyan
de la'ang dgug gzhug byas nas sta gon dang dngos gzhi

bskur bas shi 'pho de'i sdig sbyong du 'gyur ba sogs kyi dgos pa yod pa dang / rjes bzung ma byas pa zhig la dbang bskur du rung ba ni/ rjes bzung gi slob ma sta gon gyi tshe
med pa la gzugs brnyan nam skyin po bcug nas de la sta gon byed par spyi rgyud las bshad tshul gong du bkod pa des 'grub cing / de gnyis la sta gon gyi sngon du rjes bzung
ma byas pas so/ /gzhan yang slob ma rjes bzung ma byas par dbang bskur ba ni lam 'bras dang 'brel ba'i tshe ma gtogs deng sang phal cher gyi phyag len mdzad pa mngon
sum gyis mthong bzhin du rjes su ma bzung ba zhig la dbang bskur bar thal ba'i phyir dang zhes gsungs pa ni/ mkhas pa'i gsung du mi snang zhing / rjes bzung ma byas pa la
dbang bskur mi rung bar bshad pa de dang / yang paN chen nyid kyis sta gon gyi tshe ni thams cad cig car du 'tshogs dgos pa yin te/ de las 'ga' zhig ma tshang na de'i skyin
po gzhug pa dang / de'ang ma 'byor na gang ma tshang ba de'i gzugs brnyan byed du bcug nas sta gon gyi chos rnams byed dgos par gsungs pa'i phyir zhes gsungs nas/ spyi
rgyud kyi lung / slob ma yongs su bzung ba gang / /zhes sogs tshigs bcad gnyis 'dren par mdzad pa gnyis gong 'og nang 'gal ba ltar snang ba dang / gzhan yang chos kyi
rje sa skya paNTi ta chen pos/ spyod pa'i rgyud kyi dbang bskur la/ /slob ma grangs nges med par gsungs/ /zhes spyod rgyud kyi dbang la grangs nges med par bshad pa dang
/ paN chen gyis spyir rgyud sde bzhi char gyi dbang la grangs nges yod par gsungs/ khyad par spyi

rgyud kyi dbang la grangs nges yod pa'i rgyu mtshan du/ rnam snang mngon byang las/ slob ma dad cing rigs btsun pa/ /de bzhin dkon mchog gsum la dad/ /zab mo yi ni blo dang
ldan/ /spro ba che zhing tshul khrims ldan/ /bzod dang ldan zhing ser sna med//dpa' la yid rab brtan pa ni/ /bcu 'am brgyad dam bdun nam lnga/ /gcig gnyis bzhi las lhag
kyang rung / /dpyad mi dgos par bzung bar bya/ /zhes pa dang / de dang 'brel chags su/ 'di skad ces/ gsang ba'i bdag po/ gang dag gis sngon theg pa chen po gsang sngags spyad
pa'i tshul sgo mtha' yas pa sgrub pa la goms par byas pa de dag ni rdo rje sems dpa' yin te/ de rnams nyid kyi don gyi phyir grangs kyi tshad 'di byas so zhes pa rnams
la dgongs nas/ spyod pa'i rgyud kyi dbang bskur la/ /slob ma kha 'chams kha yar gyi/ /nges pa med mod grangs med min/ /bcu las lhag pa bkag phyir ro/ /zhes gsungs pa dang
/ yang rgyud de nyid las/ 'on kyang slob dpon snying rje chen po dang ldan pas sems can gyi khams ma lus pa yid dam 'cha' ba kho nar bya ste/ des byang chub kyi sems
kyi rgyur 'gyur bar bya ba'i phyir sems can tshad med pa rnams yongs su bzung bar bya'o zhes gsungs pa la dgongs nas/ de lta na yang rjes bzung gi /slob ma grangs la nges
pa med/ /slob dpon snying rje chen po yis/ /tshad med bzung zhes gsungs phyir ro/ /zhes gsungs nas/ spyod rgyud kyi slob ma rjes 'dzin la grangs nges med par bzhed pa rgyab
'gal du song ngo / /bshad

ma thag pa'i rnam snang mngon byang gi lung tsho gnyis po de dag gi don la bdag gi yongs 'dzin dam pa mkhan chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi gsung las/ des na mngon byang las bcu
tshun chad dang / tshad med pa gnyis gsungs pa la dgongs pa 'grel tshul 'di ltar bya ste/ skal ldan rigs sad pa'i las 'phro can nyung shas shig rjes su 'dzin pa'i tshul
dang / skal dman lam gyi sbyangs ba sngon du ma song ba mtha' yas pa zhig snying rjes rjes su 'dzin pa'i tshul gnyis las dang po'i dbang du byas nas bcu tshun chad gsungs
shing / de dag rjes su bzung tshar ma thag dbang bskur bas chog pa yin te zhes gsungs nas/ rnam snang mngon byang gi lung / slob ma dad cing rigs btsun pa/ /zhes sogs 'dren
par mdzad/ rjes su 'dzin tshul gnyis pa'i dbang du byas nas sems can tshad med pa bshad cing / de'ang re zhig dbang mi bskur bar skyabs 'gro'i sgo nas so thar la sbyangs
zhing dge sdig gi blang dor bstan/ de nas me tog la sogs pas mchod pas tshogs bsag tu bcug nas sems bskyed 'bogs shing / de'i rjes su dbang bskur ba yin te zhes gsungs
nas/ 'on kyang slob dpon snying rje chen po dang ldan pas zhes sogs 'dren par mdzad pa ni mkhas pa'i legs bshad bla med du snang ngo / /yang spyir rje btsun gong mas dbang
gi slob ma la grangs nges mdzad pa dang / khyad par chos rje sa paN gyis spyi rgyud kyi lung gis bya rgyud dang rnal 'byor rgyud dang bla med gsum gyi dbang gi slob ma
la grangs nges mi byed pa dgag pa la/ 'brug pa sprul sku padma dkar pos brtag gnyis kyi

dri bar/ snod rung gang zag nyer lnga las gzhan pa/ /'jug pa bla med rgyud sde gang du bkag /bya ba'i rgyud las skabs 'dir btsan pa'i lung / /dpal ldan dus kyi 'khor lo snang
min nam/ /zhes brtsad cing dri bar mdzad pa dang / dri ba de nyid kyi lan gong dkar ba mkhyen brtse chos mdzad ces pas mdzad pa la/ slar sprul sku nyid kyis lan zhig mdzad
pa'i nang na bya ba'i rgyud 'di'i lung / mkhas pas slob ma gcig gam gsum/ /lnga 'am yang na bdun dag gam/ /nyi shu rtsa ni lnga yi bar/ /zung du ma gyur slob ma bzung
/ /de bas lhag pa'i slob ma ni/ /yongs su gzung bar mi shis so/ /zhes pa 'di kun la sbyor du btub la/ rnam snang mngon byang las/ bcu 'am brgyad dam bdun nam lnga/ /gcig
gnyis bzhi las lhag kyang rung / /dpyad mi dgos par gzung bar bya/ /zhes pa 'di kun la sbyor du mi rung ba ji ltar 'thad ldan gyi rigs pas brtags na/ bya rgyud las spyod
rgyud phul du gyur pa yin pas de dbang btsan par byed dgongs so zhes sogs gsungs so/ /de'i tshig rkang dang po gnyis la rnam dpyad cher mi snang ste/ dbang gi slob ma nyer
lnga las lhag pa dang / de las nyung yang kha 'chams la mi rung bas dang / bla med kyi rgyud sde dag tu tshig zin la med pa'i rgyu mtshan gyis rgyud sde 'og ma'i lung
'dren par mdzad pa yin la/ de ltar mdzad pa de'ang khyed kyi thugs la sa paN gyis sbyor du rung mi rung ma gzigs par rang gar sbyar 'dug dgongs nas de ltar gsungs par snang
na'ang / chos rje mkhyen rab kyi dbang phyug 'di ni

rgyud sde gong ma rnams su rang rang na gsal kha yod pa rnams de kha gtso ba dang / ci ste gong mar dbang gi gnas skabs sogs su gsal kha cher med pa na 'og ma nas blang chog
pa dang / len dgos par ston pa nyid kyis gsungs pa dag sbyar ba yin gyi/ rgyal bas ma gsungs pa zhig rang bzo mdzad nas lung sbyor du bshad pa min pa'i phyir/ 'o na ston
pas bla med sogs kyi dbang gi slob ma'i grangs nges bya rgyud las len par gang du bshad snyam na/ dogs pa 'di lta bu sngon gyi dus su'ang byung zhing / ma 'ongs pa na khyod
lta bu 'byung bar chos kyi rje'i ye shes kyi gzigs pas legs par mkhyen nas sdom gsum rab dbye las bla med sogs kyi dbang gi slob ma nyer lnga las lhag pa mi rung ba
spyi rgyud kyi lung dang sbyar ba'i rjes su/ 'di ni bya ba'i rgyud yin pas/ /gzhan gyi cho ga min snyam na/ /gzhan rnams kun la 'di 'jug pa/ /spyi rgyud nyid las 'di skad
gsungs/ /zhes bka' stsal bar snang zhing / des na ston pas/ gang du las ni yod gyur la/ /las kyi cho ga rnams med pa/ /de ni spyi yi rgyud dag las/ /gsungs pa'i cho ga mkhas
pas bsten/ /zhes spyi rgyud du gsungs pa 'dis rgyud sde gang du dbang bskur ba la sogs pa'i las ni yod la/ slob ma'i grangs sogs las kyi cho ga gsal po med pa rnams
spyi rgyud 'di nas bshad pa ltar bya'o zhes bstan pas/ chos rje sa paN gyis lung sbyor de ltar mdzad pa 'di ni rdo rje 'chang gi rgyud kyi dgongs pa bla na med pa yin la/
khyed kyis bya rgyud las dus 'khor btsan pas de ltar mi rigs zhes pa ni rdo rje 'chang la rgol

bar song bas shin tu ya nga'o/ /gzhan yang khyed kyis brtag gnyis dri ba'i yang lan du 'thad ldan gyi rigs pas brtags na zhes sogs kyang mi 'thad de/ spyi rgyud kyi lung de
rgyud sde gong ma la sbyar du rung ba ni rdo rje 'chang gis gsungs tshul bshad zin pa de yin la/ rnam snang mngon byang gi lung de gong ma la sbyor bar ston pa'i rdo rje
'chang gis gsungs pa'i lung yod na khyod kyis ston cig dang / de 'dra med pas 'di'ang ston pa la rgol bar song ngo / /yang khyed kyi dus 'khor bya rgyud las btsan zhes pa
bla med nang phan tshun yin pas zhes par snang ba 'di'ang phyogs gcig ma gzigs pa'i gsung ste/ bla med spyi la kha skong dgos pa dag rgyud sde 'og ma nas 'gang ba rgyud
nyid las/ ji ltar de nyid 'dus pa yi/ /dkyil 'khor cho ga de bzhin bya/ /zhes pa dang / gang du las ni yod gyur la/ /zhes sogs gsungs pas gsal ba yin la/ bla med spyi la
dus 'khor gyi rgyas 'gebs pa'i tshad ldan gyi lung gis zin so med pa'i phyir/ yang dus kyi 'khor lor nyer lnga las lhag pa la dbang bskur bya ba gnang ba'i rgyu mtshan la
yang lan der/ yang / sngags kyi dbang bskur byed pa na/ /grangs nges med par dbang bskur byed/ /'di ni rdo rje 'chang gis bkag /ces sgra ji bzhin pa yin na/ chos rgyal
'jam dbyangs grags pas tshangs pa'i drang srong bye ba phrag phyed dang bzhi la dbang tshar gcig gis bskur ba 'grel chen du dngos bstan du 'byung bas ston pa la ma brtsis
par song / de ltar na jo bos/ bkag pa spyad par gyur pa'i phyir/ /dka' thub

sdom pa de nyams te/ /brtul zhugs can de pham pa yi/ /ltung ba dag ni 'byung 'gyur zhing / /zhes pas rigs ldan la ltung ba phog par 'gyur ro/ /der snod dang ldan pa mang po
la bskur ba yongs su gsungs pas lung gi go mi chod na zhes sogs gsungs 'dug kyang / de ltar bshad pa ni de dus kyi dbang bskur mkhan dang dbang zhu mkhan thams cad skal
ldan las dag pa'i gang zag kho na yin pas/ rdo rje slob dpon 'phags pa'i gang zag gis mdzad pa'i sngon gyi cho ga yin gyi/ deng sang gi so so skye bos byar mi rung la/ yang
khyed kyi yang lan de nyid las/ 'phags pas mdzad pa ji lta ba slob ma la bya dgos pa rdo rje gur du/ byang chub rdo rje sangs rgyas la/ /mchod cing ji ltar stsal ba ltar/
/bdag kyang rab tu bskyab pa'i phyir/ /nam mkha'i rdo rje deng bdag stsol/ /ces pa dang / slob dpon padma manydzus/ dpal ldan bde ba'i mgon po yis/ /dpal ldan chos kyi
rdo rje la/ /gsang ba'i de nyid bstan pa ltar/ /mgon po de bzhin bka' drin stsol/ /zhes gsungs so/ zhes bshad 'dug pas sngon byung ba'i rgyu mtshan gyis da lta'i rjes 'jug
gis byar rung zhing bya dgos par yang 'dod na/ sngon grub chen te lo pas nA ro pa la 'jim ril zhig 'phangs pa dang / rnam thar 'ga' zhig las mchil lham 'phangs par bshad
de gang ltar de la brten nas nA ro pa'i thugs la mi rtog pa 'khrungs pa dang / nA ro pas dpal mchog Dombhi par bdud rtsi byin rlabs byas pa'i thod chang byin pa 'thungs
pa tsam gyis grol ba'i tshul bshad yong gi 'dug pa khyed dag de bzhin du gyis la slob ma

grol bar gyis shig gzhan yang mdo sde dkon mchog brtsegs pa las/ rgyal sras byams pa dang 'jam dbyangs kyis mkhan po mdzad/ khyim bdag dgu stong dang bdun stong khyim pa'i
rtags dang ldan bzhin du bsnyen par rdzogs par gsungs pas na da lta'ang de ltar byed rigs par 'gyur te de ltar sngon byung ba'i gang zag sngon byung ba'i rgyu mtshan gyis
de nyid da ltar bya dgos par 'dod pa'i phyir/ yang gong gi dri ba de'i 'phros las/ bya ba'i rgyud la bkag na'ang de nyid kyi/ /rigs gtad rjes gnang khrom la byed pa'ang
'gal/ /skabs 'di'i rjes gnang dbang la dgos pa'i khyad/ /ci yang ma mthong tshig la rtsod pas ci/ /zhes pa ni rdo rje 'chang la brtsad pa ste/ /gsang ba spyi rgyud las/ mkhas
pas slob ma gcig gam gsum/ /lnga 'am yang na bdun dag gam/ /nyi shu rtsa ni lnga yi bar/ /zung du ma gyur slob ma gzung / /de bas lhag pa'i slob ma ni/ /yongs su bzung
ba mi shis so/ /zhes pa 'di bla med dang rnal 'byor rgyud kyi dbang gi slob ma'i grangs nges la sbyor du mi rung zer na'ang / bya rgyud kyi dbang gi slob ma'i grangs nges
bstan pa la smyon par mi nus la/ bya rgyud kyi rigs gtad dang rjes gnang sogs la grangs nges de ltar dgos pa rgyal bas ma gsungs pa'i phyir/ dbang bskur dang rjes gnang
la don la khyad par med zer ba'ang rgyud sde spyi la dgongs na ni gsang sngags kyi lam gyi rtsa ba dbang bskur spong ba'i bdud tshig yin te/ rdo rje theg pa'i sgor zhugs
pa'i gang zag gis dbang la ma brten par mchog 'grub pa med par

rgyud sde rnams las lan gcig ma yin par yang nas yang du gsungs shing / de'ang dbang bskur rdo rje theg pa'i lam gyi rtsa ba yin pa'i rgyu mtshan kyis yin par/ sdom gsum rab
dbye las/ des na thub pas rgyud sde las/ /dbang bskur kho na bsngags pa dang / /mkhas rnams spyi nas dbang bskur la/ /gus pa'i rgyu mtshan de ltar yin/ /zhes gsungs pas
bstan la/ khyed rang gis yang lan der/ lar dbang ma thob par mchog thob pa med la zhes bshad pas dbang ma thob par mchog thob pa med pa nyid kyang bzhed cing / rjes gnang
ma thob na mchog mi 'grub par bshad pa tshad ldan gyi lung gang na'ang med pa'i phyir/ gal te bya rgyud kyi dbang dang rjes gnang la khyad par med zer rgyu yin na/ ye shes
thig le'i rgyud las/ chu yi dbang bskur cod pan dag /bya ba'i rgyud la rab tu grags/ /zhes pa'i dbang de dag gang du bskur ba'i dkyil 'khor ston pa'i rgya gzhung yang
snang na/ rjes gnang la de 'dra gang du bshad/ des na 'di ni bya rgyud la 'dris med do zhes pa'i gsung du snang ngo / /yang dri ba der/ rigs pa cho ga rdzogs par mi 'gyur
lo/ /dus 'khor 'phreng ba'i dbang nyid mang po la/ /brten bzhin de skad smras kyang mdzes pa min/ /bde kye nyung ba mngon sum nyid kyis grub/ /ces pa 'di'ang rab dbyer/
de bas lhag pa'i slob ma la/ /cho ga yongs su rdzogs pa ni/ /mtshan mo gcig la tshar mi nus/ /de yi mtshan mo ma tshar na/ /cho ga nyams par 'gyur bar gsungs/ /zhes sogs
la rgol rgyur 'dug na'ang / bdag nyid chen pos de ltar gsungs

pa'i dgongs don ni/ brtag gnyis las/ mtshan mo skye bo med khyim du/ /slob dpon la sogs rab phye nas/ /dbang ni ji ltar gsungs pa nyid/ /ces dang / rdo rje mkha' 'gro las/
yul de dag gi bu mo gang / /rtag tu mtshan mo 'phyan pa dang / /sgrub pa po la dngos grub ster/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar dkyil 'khor bsgrub cing mchod pa dang / slob dpon bdag
nyid 'jug cing dbang blangs ba dang / slob ma la dbang bskur ba sogs thams cad mtshan mo tshar na legs shing / de'ang rdo rje rtse mo ni dus 'khor las kyang dkyil chog
mang ba dang / bla med la bde kye gnyis sogs dus 'khor las nyung yang de dag gis rdo rje slob dpon gyi dbang rnams slob ma re re nas dbang stegs la bzhag nas bskur ba dang
/ dbang gong ma gsum gyi dngos gzhi'ang slob ma re re nas bskur ba dang po'i phyag len la yod pas/ de bzhin byas pas nyer lnga las lhag pa la mtshan mo de'i nang du mi
tshar ba shas che bas skya rengs shar gong mtshan mo byon pa'i dpa' bo rnal 'byor ma rnams tshogs gtor gyis mnyes par byas nas gshegs gsol thub na 'brel chags shing shis
pas na de ltar du chos rjes gdul bya rnams la brtse bas 'doms par mdzad pa yin zhing / de ni rgyud kyi dgongs pa'ang yin te spyi rgyud las/ lha yang nyi ma nub pa na/ /nges
par byin gyi rlabs kyis 'du/ /nyi ma shar bar ma gyur pa/ /mchod nas gshegs su gsol ba shis/ /zhes gsungs pas so/ /des na dbang gi cho ga yongs su rdzogs pa mtshan mo
gcig la tshar na legs pa

las/ nyer lnga las lhag pa la byas na mi tshar ba shas che bas de las lhag pa la mi bya zhes 'doms par mdzad pa yin pas/ dus 'khor dang phreng ba sogs kyang nyer lngar grangs
bcad de mdzad thub na shin du'ang legs la/ der ma zad slob ma re re nas bskur thub na'ang legs pa nyid yin pas/ dus 'khor phreng ba'i dbang nyid mang po la/ /brten bzhin
de skad smras kyang mdzes pa min/ /zhes pa'ang ma nus med du grub bo/ /'brug pa'i gsung 'di la'ang kha cig tu ston cing zhes pa dang / 'ga' zhig tu ston bzhin/ zhes 'byung
ba de ltar byas na slob ma mang po la ston bzhin zhes par 'gyur la/ de ni/ bde kye nyung ba mngon sum nyid kyis grub/ /ces pa 'di dang gzhung snga phyi'i 'brel mi 'grig
cing khong rang gi yang lan der cho ga'i tshogs mang po la brten zhing zhes pa lta bu gcig bshad yod pas snga ma ltar byas na 'brug pa'i rjes 'jug dag phyogs snga ma
longs zhes zer ba dag 'byung du dogs te da dung dpyad par rigs so/ /yang brgal lan tshangs pa'i rig sngags su 'phros don gyi tshul du 'di ltar/ gnyis pa ni rgol bas chos
rje bla ma'i dgongs pa yin par byas nas snang gsum gyi sngon du dbang nges par byed pa de la 'di 'dri ste/ khyed kyi khrid tshul de skal ldan cig car ba dang skal dman rim
'jug pa gang gi lam rim yin/ dang po ltar na lam rim de la dbang dang rim gnyis yan lag dang bcas pa'i bar du snang gsum gyi khrid mi dgos te/ de la thun mong ba'i lam
gyis rgyud sbyangs mi dgos par dang po nyid nas dbang dang rim gnyis 'brel pa can du

byas chog pa rgyud kyi dgongs pa dang / dbang gi sngon du skyabs 'gro dang sems bskyed tsam gnon pa bla ma rnams kyi phyag len yin par rje btsun gong mas bshad pa las/ khyod
kyis ni bshad pa'i dbang gi sngon 'gro'i sems bskyed bor nas/ ma bshad pa'i thun mong gi lam gyis dkri ba ni nor/ phyi ma ltar na gang zag de la thun mong ba'i lam rim
gyis bkris nas/ phyis snod rung du gyur pa na dbang bskur bar bshad kyi/ dang po nyid nas tsham tshom med par dbang bskur ba bshad pa med/ ma bshad pa tsam du'ang ma zad
slob dpon rin po che'i dbang chu dang / rje btsun gyis ljon shing sogs las lung rigs kyi sgo nas de ltar byed pa bkag go /'ga' zhig 'di'i rjes skyob par 'dod nas/ rdo rje'i
tshig rkang gi bla ma dam pa'i zhabs pad btud de zhes pas smin byed kyi dbang bstan cing / gzhung bshad rnams las snang gsum gyi skabs su thos bsam dang bslab pas rgyud
sbyangs pa dang / dbang gis sbyangs pa zhes bshad pas snang gsum gyi sngon du dbang nges par dgos par grub ces smra'o/ /de ltar na gdan sogs gsum pa bzhi'i rgyu'i dbang
zhes pas rgyu dbang bstan par gzhung bshad mtha' dag nas 'byung bas/ snang gsum khrid kyi thog mtha' gnyis char du dbang re bya dgos par 'gyur ro/ /'o na ci zhe na bla ma
dam pa'i zhabs pad btud de zhes pa ni bstan bcos lus dang mthun pa'i mchod brjod yin pas/ des de bstan par sems pa ni blo gros shin tu chung ba ste/ nyams snang gi rten
rnal 'byor pa la dbang gis smin pa sogs

gzhung bshad las bshad pa skabs 'di'i snang gsum gyi sngon du dbang dgos pa'i shes byed du 'dod pa ni rdo rje'i tshig rkang gi bzhugs tshul rags pa tsam yang thos bsam gyi
yul du ma byas pa'i 'chal gtam yin te/ gzhung de'i bzhugs tshul la snang ba gsum lam rang rkang la sbyar ba dang / lam gyi gzhi bca' la sbyar ba gnyis las/ dang po ni gzhung
de'i 'khor 'das thun mong ba'i gzhung tshom bu re res kyang 'tshang rgya ba'i cha rkyen lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa yongs rdzogs re ston pa yin la/ de'i tshe snang ba gsum
du bstan pa'i gzhung nyung ngu des kyang snang ba gsum lam rang rkang la sbyar ba zhes pa'i ming can gyi lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams ngag yongs rdzogs gcig ston
dgos pas/ de la dgongs nas gzhung bshad rnams su thos bsam dang bslab pas rgyud sbyangs pa dang / dbang gis sbyangs pa sogs kyi rnam gzhag de dag 'byung ba yin la/ snang
gsum lam gyi gzhi bca' la sbyar ba'i skabs 'dir ni 'khor 'das thun mong ba'i gzhung tshom bu bdun dang / 'khor lo 'cham pa 'jig rten pa'i lam gyi gzhung tshom bu bdun te
bcu bzhi po thams cad kyang gang zag gcig gis nyams su blang bya'i lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams ngag yongs rdzogs zhig ston pa la dgongs nas/ rje sa chen gyis/ snang
ba gsum gyis lam gyi gzhi bcas te/ nyams blangs ma lus rgyud gsum dag gis shes/ /zhes sogs gsungs/ de'i tshe snang gsum lam gyi gzhi bca' la sbyar ba'i lam ni rgyud gsum
po nyid la 'jog de'ang smin grol gnyis su

'dus/ de'i sngon du lam gyi gzhi gdan gyi tshul du snang gsum gyi khrid dgos pa drangs ma thag pa'i lung des shes/ de la dgongs nas rje btsun gyis gzhung ji lta ba'i khrid
yig gnyis char du snang gsum lam gyi gzhi bca' la sbyar ba de bshad pa yin la/ de ltar du bkris nas nyams su blangs nas nyams myong skyes pa de grub chen gyi gzhung gi dgongs
par bsgrub pa'i phyir/ phyis rdo rje'i tshig rkang las bstan pa de dag gzhung bshad dang mthun par slob dpon gyis bshad/ slob mas thos bsam gyi sgro 'dogs chod par bya
dgos pa'i don du bshad pa yin zhes gsungs nas/ chos rje bla ma dam pa'i khrid yig gi dgongs don la kho bo cag ni dngos bstan de khyab mthar mi bzung / 'phags yul lta bu
