na theg pa che chung dang / rgyud sde bzhi'i gdul bya rigs so sor nges pa yod kyang / bod na theg dman dngos su med pa dang / deng sang dbang dar ches pas lam 'bras zhu
mkhan rnams de gnyis gang rung la zhugs pa shas che bas dang por dbang byas kyang nyes pa med pa la dgongs nas snang gsum sngon du dbang bskur ba bshad la/ de lta bu la
snang gsum gyi khrid ma byas kyang rung mod/ gzhung ji lta ba'i khrid kyi kha tshang ba'i ched dang / des snang gsum gyi lam nyams su blangs kyang skyon med pa la dgongs
pa yin pas 'di ltar 'chad shes na dka' gnas su sems pa thams cad rang grol du 'gro ba yin gsungs/ de dag dang mthun par glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub kyis rab 'byams
pa blo gros rab gsal gyi dris lan du khrid yig phyi ma 'di

la brten nas snang gsum gyi sngon du dbang byed pa rnams ni gdul bya la ltos pa'i lam dkri lugs kyi babs dang ye mi mthun pas zhes dang / 'on kyang da lta snang gsum gyi sngon
du dbang bskur byed pa'ang dang po'i dus kyi lam 'bras pa rnams kyis sngar dbang gis smin pa zhig la lam 'bras kyi khrid ston pa'i tshe dbang de khrid kyi sngon 'gro'i
rgyu dus kyi dbang min yang / slob dpon rang nyid las kyai rdo rje'i dbang bskur re thob par byas nas/ de dang 'brel ba'i khrid ston pa la bla bu bsgrigs pa'i lugs su byas
nas/ de 'dra'i gang zag la rgyud gsum man chad kyis dkris pas chog kyang / khrid kyi kha tshang ba'i phyir snang ba gsum nas ston pa mang po zhig byung zhing / de 'dra'i
sgo nas khrid byed pa la 'gal ba yod pa ma yin kyang / skal dman rim gyis pa'i dkri tshul la bsams nas tshogs pa shin tu mang ba la de ltar byed pa ni gang dang yang
mi mthun nam snyam lags zhes gsungs so/ /gong du tshangs pa'i rigs sngags kyi 'phros don bshad pa de la mkhan chen bzang bkras pas snyan brgyud 'khrul sel las lan gang yang
ma gsungs par btang snyoms su 'jog par mdzad cing / sgyi chu ba buddha shrI'i yang lan nor bu'i phreng bar de la snyan brgyud zab mo'i don go bar mi 'gyur bas mgo sgre'i
lan 'di brjod par bya ste/ khyed kyis gzhung khrid rgyas pa lan gnyis slob ma la 'chad pa'i tshe/ gnyis pa de skal ldan cig car ba'i lam mam skal dman rim 'jug pa'i lam
gang yin/ dang po ltar na dbang dang rim gnyis yan lag dang bcas pa'i bar du snang gsum gyis dkri dgos pa ma yin

te/ dang po nyid nas dbang dang rim gnyis 'brel pa can du byas chog pa rgyud sde'i dgongs pa yin pa'i phyir/ ci gsung / gnyis pa ltar na skal ldan cig car ba dbang dang lam
gyis dkris zin nas slar skal dman rim 'jug pa'i lam gyis bkri ba khyed rang ltar na rung ba ma yin te/ gzhan yang dbang bskur zin pa'i slob ma la snang gsum gyi khrid phog
na rtsa ltung 'byung bar bshad pa de'ang dran par gyis la lan gsungs shig khyed kyi bshad pa ni de 'dra/ lag len ni de 'dra na gzu bor gnas pa'i blos dpyod cig ces gsungs
so/ /yang gong du bkod pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyi brgal lan tshangs pa'i rigs sngags su 'phros don du gsungs pa de dang mtshungs par/ rje btsun
de nyid kyis mdzad pa'i gzhung ji lta ba bzhin du dkri ba'i gzhung shing las 'phros pa'i dri bar don tshan lnga yod pa'i dang po las/ snang gsum sngon du dbang bskur ba/
/nges par dgos zhes khas len pa'i/ /lam 'bras pa la 'di skad 'dri/ /lam de'i go rim rgyud gzhung nas/ /bshad pa'i skal dman rim 'jug dang / /skal bar ldan pa cig car ba'i/
/lam rim gnyis po gang yin dri/ /dang po ltar na khrid tshul de'i/ /sngon 'gro 'khor ba'i nyes dmigs dang / /dal 'byor rnyed dka' byams snying rje/ /byang chub sems bskyed
la sogs pa/ /tshad ldan gong mas bshad kun chad/ /chad pa min na go rim nor/ /nges par 'byung ba'i blo tsam yang / /ma skyes pa de sngags lam du/ /ci dgar 'jug pa rgyud
las bkag /phyi ma ltar na snang

ba gsum/ /nges pa can du ston pa lhag /lhag pa min na rnam gzhag 'chol/ /zhes gsungs te/ de dag gi don yang snang gsum khrid kyi sngon du nges par dbang bskur nas dkri ba'i
khrid 'di skal dman rim 'jug pa ltar dkri ba'i khrid yin nam/ skal ldan zhig cig car ba ltar khrid pa'i khrid gang yin/ dang po ltar na khrid tshul de la sngon 'gro 'khor
ba'i nyes dmigs sogs ston dgos pa rnams chad la/ de dag dbang bskur nas de'i rjes su ston pas chad pa min zer na/ lam rim de la thog mar 'khor ba'i nyes dmigs ston pa sogs
thun mong ba'i lam gyis sbyangs pa rnams bstan nas/ gzod thun mong ma yin pa'i lam dbang bskur ba sogs byed dgos pa la/ khyed dag thog mar dbang nges par dgos par 'dod
pas go rim nor zhing 'khor ba las nges par 'byung ba'i blo tsam yang ma bskyed pa'i gang zag de sngags lam du 'jug pa rgyud las bkag la/ phyi ma ltar na skal ldan cig car
ba la dbang gi rjes su snang gsum gyi khrid nges par byed pa lhag cing / ci ste skal ldan cig car ba la yang thun mong gi lam sngon du 'gro dgos pas lhag pa min zer na/
de dag kyang dbang gi sngon du dgos pa la rjes su byas pas rnam gzhag 'chol bar song zhes par snang ngo / /de'i lan du thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam
rgyal dpal bzang po'i thugs sras byang chub dbang rgyal zhes bya bas lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i skabs kyi dri lan rmongs pa'i mun sel zhes bya ba mdzad pa de nyid las/
rje btsun mthu stobs dbang phyug gis/ /gsung gi rdo rje'i tshig

rkang las/ /byung ba'i nyams su blang tshul ni/ /rje btsun rnams kyis bzhed ji bzhin/ /'jam dbyangs drug pa chos kyi rje'i/ /gsung las byung ba'i lam rim 'di/ /gtso bor skal
bar ldan pa yis/ /nyams su blang ba'i rim pa yin/ /min yang rim gyis dkris nas ni/ /snod rung gyur nas blang bya yin/ /de'i yang thog mar dbang bskur ba/ /yin par ljon
shing dag las ni/ /da ni bla med skal ldan pa/ /cig car 'jug pa'i mngon rtogs brjod/ /smin par byed pa'i dbang zhes pa/ /gsungs shing dag ldan nyid las kyang / /thun mong
gis rgyud sbyangs pa dang / /skal ldan rgyud ma sbyangs kyang ni/ /'jug rung phyi ma'i gnyis pa las/ /zhes gsungs dbang gi chu bo las/ /sngar bstan ma zhugs rab 'bring gsum/
/de'i rab dbang gi snod du gsungs/ /gzhan yang gang zag rab 'bring gsum/ /dkri ba'i gzhung shing nyid du ni/ /dang po gang zag bla ma'i drung / /'ongs pa dbang dang
dam tshig dang / /ldan byas bskyed pa'i rim pa dang / /snying por gces pa byed pa de/ khrid kyis bskyang bar 'dod pa na/ /zhes sogs gsungs na thog mar dbang / /nges par dgos
pa gsungs pa nyid/ /khyed rnams rgyud dus dbang gi sngon/ /nges par snang gsum dgos zhes pa/ /snang gsum sngon du ma song bar/ /dbang bskur mi rung pa yin nam/ /dbang
bskur song nas snang ba gsum/ /mi rung ba ni gang yin brtag /dang po ltar na yan gar du/ /dbang bskur byed pa med 'gyur zhing / /phyi ma ltar na lam 'bras ni/ /gnyis pa
'chad

tshe ji ltar byed/ /khyad par du yang rgyud gsum gyis/ /dkri ba'i skabs su rgyu chos can/ /'khor ba'i gnas lugs bsgom zhes pa/ /ma dag snang ba'i skabs bzhin du/ /slar yang
bsgom par gsungs pa dang / /shin tu rgyas bshad skabs su yang / /snang ba gsum gyi don dran par/ /legs par gsungs na ji ltar rgol/ /gzhan yang snang ba gsum gyi sngon/ /bsag
sbyong rnam gnyis bya dgos te/ /khrid kyi sngon 'gro yin phyir ro/ /dgos na dbang bskur ma thob pa'i/ /bla ma skabs 'di'i tshogs zhing du/ /mi rung gal te rung na ni/
/bla ma sangs rgyas nyid yin zhes/ /bya ba dbang bskur thob nas yin/ /zhes gsungs pa yang drang don 'gyur/ /rdo rje sems dpa'i sgom bzlas kyang / /dbang ma thob par mi
rung na/ /sgrib pa sbyong bsag gang du 'gyur/ /gal te dbang rjes byed ce na/ /de gnyis sngon 'gro min pa 'am/ /snang ba gsum po khrid min te/ /sngon 'gro sngon du mi dgos
phyir/ /gal te snang gsum khrid min na/ /khrid tshul nyer brgyad nyer dgu zhes/ /dkar chag tu gsungs ji ltar bgrang / /mdor na snang ba gsum gyi sngon/ /sngon 'gro bcu gnyis
'gro dgos par/ /gang zag dbang po rab 'bring gsum/ /bkri ba'i gzhung shing nyid du ni/ /mi mthun sgrib sbyong yig brgya dang / /mthun pa'i tshogs bsags maNDal dang /
/'khor ba'i nyes dmigs bsgom pa gsum/ /zhes dang / thun thams cad kyi mgor/ /dgos pa rnam pa bcu gnyis te/ /gnad dbab gsum dang sngon 'gro gsum/ /zhes dang khrid kyi dkar
chag tu/ /thams cad sngon

'gro chos bcu gnyis/ /de dag rnams la thun gsum ste/ /gsol ba gdab dang bsag sbyong la/ /thun gcig sbyang ba gsum po la/ /thun gcig khrid kyi sngon 'gro 'o/ /gnad dbab gsum
dang sgom pa gsum/ /thun gcig thun gyi sngon 'gro 'o/ /zhes pa gsungs na mi 'dod ci/ /de ltar tshogs bsgom rin po che'i/ /dngos slob nyan gnyags gnyis kyis kyang / /gzhung
shing dang po'i khrid yig tu/ /gsal ba nyid du gsungs pa dang / /chos rje bla ma dam pa yi/ /khrid yig sbas don gsal ba ru/ /sngon 'gro de dag 'gro dgos par/ /nges pa
nyid du gsungs pa dang / /de nyid tshad mar grub pa yang / /ngor chen rdo rje 'chang chen gyi/ /gsan yig rgya mtsho zhes par ni/ /chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis/ /mdzad
pa'i ngo mtshar snang ba dang / /gzhung bshad man ngag bshad mdzod dang / /khrid yig sbas don gsal ba sogs/ /pod nag ma ru grags pa yang / /legs par thob ces gsungs
phyir ro/ /des na snang ba gsum gyi sngon/ /sngon 'gro de rnams 'gro dgos phyir/ /thog mar dbang bskur byed grub cing / /khyad par snang ba gsum gyi sngon/ /bla ma dam pa'i
zhabs btud de/ /zhes pas rgyu yi dbang bstan par/ /thams cad mkhyen pa chos kyi rjes/ /dbang ma bskur la bla ma med/ /ces pa'i 'brel gyis shes pa'i tshul/ /rgyas bshad
rnam 'grel rnams su yang / /phyi nang gsang ba mthar thug gi /bla ma bzhi yi lus sogs la/ /dbang bzhi bskur nas dbyibs sogs kyi/ /lam bzhi bsgoms pas sku

bzhi ni/ /'grub par gsungs na de yi sngon/ /dbang ma bskur ba de dag gi /bshad pa 'byung ba ji ltar lags/ /rang gi brgyud pa'i bla ma sogs/ /rje btsun dam pa de rnams kyi/
/gsung la tshad mar mi byed par/ /rang bzo'i gya tshom smra ba la/ /yid brtan rung ngam shes ldan dag /gzhan yang khyed rnams la la dag /khrid kyi dkar chag sa paN gyis/
/mdzad pa min te lcang ra ba/ /kun dga' rgyal mtshan byas so zhes/ /mngon sum 'khyog por smra mod kyi/ /des na gsan yig rgya mtsho ru/ /khrid kyi dkar chag sa paN gyis/ /mdzad
pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ /chos rje nyid dang lo phu ba/ /zhes sogs yod na ji skad smra/ /gzhan yang skal ldan cig car la/ /snang gsum nges par mi dgos pa'i/ /shugs
la skal dman rim gyis la/ /nges par dgos pa khas blangs pas/ /rim 'jug lam rim thams cad la/ /snang gsum yod pas khyab lags sam/ /rim gyis 'jug la skyon brjod pa'i/ /rigs
pa rnams kyang ltar snang zhing / /byang chub sems bskyed ma byas par/ /sngags lam 'jug pa med ces pa/ /lam 'bras dus kyi dbang bskur sngon/ /sems bskyed sngags lugs zhes
bya sogs/ /sngar srol med pa'i khyad chos rnams/ /ma byas pa la skyon brjod mod/ /des na sta gon dus su sngon/ /sems bskyed gur nas bshad pa dang / /de yi sngon du sems
bskyed tshul/ /dbang chu'i tshig gis zin gyur na/ /de dag sems bskyed min pa 'am/ /yin kyang de 'dra'i sems bskyed kyis/ /go mi chod par smra na ni/ /yan gar dbang bskur
byed tshe

yang / /sems bskyed khyad chos byed dgos pas/ /rje btsun rnams la rgol ba'i phyir/ /de la bdag gis ci zhig bya/ /zhes gsungs so/ /de dag las/ rje btsun mthu stobs dbang phyug
gis/ /zhes pa nas/ nges par dgos par gsungs pa nyid/ /ces pa'i bar gyis ni gong gi dri ba de'i dngos lan btab pa ste/ de'ang rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi gzhung rdo rje'i
tshig rkang gi brjod don nyams su len tshul 'jam dbyangs drug pa bla ma dam pa'i khrid yig ltar snang gsum gyi sngon du dbang nges par bskur nas bkri ba'i khrid rim 'di
gtso bor skal ldan cig car ba'i lam rim yin cing / skal dman rim 'jug pa yod kyang / /de la'ang snang gsum thog mar dbang bskur dgos par ljon shing dang / dag ldan/ dbang
chu chen mo/ gang zag dbang po rab 'bring gsum du bkri ba'i gzhung shing rnams las bshad ces pa'i don du snang la/ de nas/ khyed rnams rgyu dus dbang gi sngon/ /zhes pa
nas/ dkar chag tu gsungs ji ltar bgrang / /zhes pa'i bar ni ngor lugs la phar 'dri ba ste/ /de'ang rgyu dbang gi sngon du snang gsum nges par dgos zer ba de snang gsum sngon
du ma song bar dbang bskur mi rung ba yin nam/ dbang bskur zin pa la snang gsum ston mi rung ba gang yin/ dang po ltar na dbang logs su byed pa med par 'gyur/ phyi ma
ltar na lam 'bras tshar gnyis 'chad pa'i tshe ji ltar byed/ khyad par rgyud gsum gyis bkri ba'i skabs su/ rgyu chos can 'khor ba'i gnas tshul zhes sogs slar yang ma dag
snang

ba'i skabs bzhin bsgom dgos par gsungs pa sogs dang 'gal zhing / gzhan yang khrid kyi sngon 'gro yin pas bsag sbyong gnyis snang gsum gyi sngon du 'gro dgos/ de byas na dbang
ma thob pa'i bla ma tshogs zhing du mi rung bar chos rje sa paN gyis bshad pa dang 'gal ba dang / rdo rje sems dpa'i bsgom bzlas kyang dbang ma thob na mi rung bas de
byas na sgrib pa sbyong bsag gang du 'gro mi shes/ gal te bsag sbyong gnyis dbang gi rjes su byed zer na/ 'o na de gnyis khrid kyi sngon 'gro min pa'am/ snang gsum khrid
min pa gang rung las ma 'das/ snang gsum khrid min na gsung ngag lam 'bras la khrid tshul nyer brgyad nyer dgu sogs su dkar chag las gsungs pa dang 'gal zhes pa'i don no/
/de nas/ mdor na snang ba gsum gyi sngon/ /zhes pa nas/ legs par thob ces gsungs phyir ro/ /zhes pa'i bar gyis slar yang snang gsum gyi sngon du dbang dgos pa'i shes byed
'don pa ste/ de'ang mdor na snang ba gsum gyi sngon du sngon 'gro bcu gnyis 'gro dgos par rje btsun gyis dbang po rab 'bring gsum gyi bkri ba'i gzhung shing dang / chos
rje sa paN gyis mdzad pa'i khrid yig dkar chag dang / tshogs bsgom rin po che'i dngos slob nyan gnyags gnyis kyi gzhung ji lta ba bzhin bkri ba'i khrid yig dang / chos rje
dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i khrid yig sbas don gsal ba rnams su gsal bar gsungs shing / khrid yig de tshad mar ni gsan yig rgya mtshor bshad/ snang gsum gyi sngon du sngon
'gro de dag byed par 'dod dgos la/ des snang gsum gyi sngon du dbang

bskur byed par yang grub ces pa'o/ /de'i rjes su/ khyad par snang ba gsum gyi sngon/ /zhes pa nas/ yid brtan rung ngam shes ldan dag /ces pa'i bar ni snang ba gsum gyi sngon
du dbang dgos pa'i rgyu mtshan gzhan 'don pa ste/ de'ang rnal 'byor dbang phyug gis lam 'bras rdo rje'i tshig rkang las snang ba gsum dang rgyud gsum sogs kyi thog mar/
bla ma dam pa'i zhabs pad btud de zhes gsungs pa dang / de'i don gzhung bshad rnams su'ang thog mar phyi nang gsang ba mthar thug gi bla ma bzhis dbang bzhi bskur lam bzhi
bsgoms pas sku bzhi 'grub par gsungs pa sogs kyi bshad pa rgyas par mdzad pas kyang snang gsum gyi sngon du dbang dgos pa grub ces pa'i don dang / de nas/ gzhan yang khyed
rnams la la dag /ces pa nas/ snang gsum yod pas khyab lags sam/ /zhes pa'i bar ni ngor lugs la 'gal ba brjod pa ste/ de'ang khyed la la khrid kyi dkar chag 'di sa paN
gyis mdzad pa min/ lcang ra ba kun dga' rgyal mtshan gyis byas zer ba ni gsan yig rgya mtshor/ khrid kyi dkar chag sa paN gyis mdzad pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni zhes sogs
gsungs pa dang 'gal zhing / gzhan yang skal ldan cig car ba la snang gsum nges par mi dgos zhes pa'i shugs la/ rim 'jug pa la de nges par dgos pa khas blangs pas rim 'jug
pa'i lam rim thams cad la snang gsum nges par yod dgos sam zhes pa'i don no/ /de nas/ rim gyis 'jug pa'i skyon brjod pa'i/ /zhes pa nas/ de la bdag gis ci zhig bya/ /zhes
pa'i

bar ni gong du bkod pa'i dri tshig tu/ nges par 'byung ba'i blo tsam yang / /zhes sogs kyis lan 'don pa ste/ /de'ang dbang gi sngon du khyod 'dod pa'i rgyud sde nas bshad pa'i
sems bskyed sngags lugs zer ba de ma byas pa rgyu mtshan du bkod nas kho bo cag la skyon brjod mod/dbang gi sta gon gyi dus su sems bskyed gur nas bshad pa bzhin byas
pa des sems bskyed kyi go mi chod na/ yan gar dbang byed ba'i tshe'ang khyed 'dod pa'i sems bskyed de byed dgos par 'gyur bas de ni rje btsun gong ma rnams la rgol bar song
zhes pa'i don no/ /yang rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyi dri ba gnyis pa ni gong gi dri ba'i gsung de nyid las/ thun mong lam gyi sngon 'gro ru/ /dbang bskur nges par dgos
pa mtshar/ /snang gsum thun mong lam min na/ /sngags lam kho nar 'dod nus sam/ /nus na mdo rgyud thams cad kyi/ /snying po bsdus pa yin no zhes/ /smra ba ne tso'i 'don
pa ste/ /mdo sde'i snying po gang la byed/ /sngags lam yin na smin grol las/ /gzhan med smin byed yin nam ci/ /grol lam yin na lta ba yi/ /rgyas thebs rim gnyis 'khor bcas
las/ /rgyud gzhung kun nas bshad pa med/ /rim gnyis gang du 'du ba smros/ /khrid tshul gnyis ka ma yin pa'i/ /lam 'bras phung po gsum pa zhig /rgyud gzhung dgongs par 'chad
nus sam/ /zhes gsungs/ de'i don yang snang gsum mdo sngags thun mong ba'i lam yin pas de'i sngon 'gro la dbang bskur bas nges par byed pa mtshar che/ ci ste snang gsum
mdo sngags thun mong ba'i lam min zer na/ 'o

na de sngags lam kho na yin na gsung ngag lam 'bras 'di mdo rgyud ma lus pa'i snying po bsdus pa'i nyams len min par 'gyur ba dang / der ma zad rim gnyis yan lag dang bcas
pa las gzhan pa'i bla med kyi sngags lam ma bshad pas snang gsum de nyid gang du 'du ba yin/ des na skal ldan cig car ba dang rim 'jug pa gnyis kyi lam gyi bkri tshul gang
yang ma yin pa'i lam 'bras kyi khrid tshul phung po gsum pa zhig 'dod nus sam zhes 'dri ba yin la/ de'i lan du chos rje byang chub dbang rgyal gyis mgo mtshungs dang /
rnal ma'i lan gnyis su mdzad nas dang po la/ de la snang ba gsum po ni/ /thun mong lam yin shes byed med/ /yod na sngags lam yin nam ci/ /sngags lam yin na smin grol las/
/gzhan med smin byed yin nam ci/ /zhes sogs skyon brjod thams cad kyang / /rang la log pa ma yin nam/ /de ltar min na snang ba gsum/ /mdo lam kho nar 'dod nus sam/ /nus
na mdo rgyud thams cad kyi/ /snying po bsdus pa yin no zhes/ /smra na ne tso'i 'don pa ste/ /sngags kyi snying po gang la byed/ /gzhan yang lam 'bras lam rim 'di/ /sngags
lam yin phyir smin grol las/ /gzhan med smin byed yin nam ci/ /grol lam yin na lta ba yi/ /rgyas thebs rim gnyis 'khor bcas las/ /rgyud gzhung kun las bshad pa med/ /rim
gnyis gang du 'du ba smros/ /rdzogs rim yin na thabs rgyud kyi/ /bum dbang lam de gang du 'gyur/ /srin bu'i kha chus srin 'bu bzhin/ /rang gi tshig gis rang nyid ni/

/bcings par gyur pas mi ngal lam/ /phyi nas bag yod bsten par rigs/ /zhes gsungs/ gnyis pa rnal ma'i lan la/ gnyis pa nges pa'i lan du ni/ /snang gsum thun mong lam yin pa/
/nyes dmigs byams dang snying rje sogs/ /theg pa gzhan la'ang yod bsam mod/ /de lta yin na lta khrid kyang / /thun mong 'gyur te de bas kyang / /thun mong 'gyur te de bas
na/ /dbang bskur dang ni sngon 'gro yang / /phyis nas byed pa cis mi rigs/ /'di ni thun mong ma yin te/ /sgom pa gsum gyis zin pa'i phyir/ /khyad par lam 'bras khrid yin
na/ /thun mong ma yin khrid du nges/ /lam 'bras min na tshig rkang du/ /lam 'bras 'dri zhes dam bcas nas/ /lam 'bras min pa bris gyur na/ /rnal 'byor dbang phyug 'khrul
lags sam/ /mdor na dbang bskur ma byas par/ snang ba gsum gyis bkri ba'i tshe/ /nyams kyi snang ba'i rten la ni/ /khyad chos gsum gyi rgyud dag la/ /thos bsam dbang gis
rgyud dag par/ /dgos par gsungs na mi 'dod cing / /thun mong min pa'i nyams snang ni/ /rim gnyis bsgoms pa las byung ba'i/ /nyams snang 'char tshul rnams gsungs na/ /gsang
sgrog 'gyur ba ma yin nam/ /thun mong yin na nyams bco lnga/ /sogs dang dag pa'i snang ba yi/ /bde bar gshegs tshul la sogs pa/ /mdo sde'i gsungs rab gang na bshad/ /khyad
par gzhung bzhin bkri bar ni/ /snang ba gsum gyis bkri gsungs nas/ /de rjes kho nar rgyud gsum gyis/ /dkri bar gsungs na bar skabs der/ /rgyu dbang bskur ba su yi

lugs/ /zhes gsungs so/ /de ltar gnyis kyi nang nas mgo sgre'i lan ni rtogs par sla la/ rnal ma'i lan de dag gi don mdor bsdu na snang gsum lam 'bras kyi khrid yin pas thun
mong ma yin pa'i khrid yin cing / snang ba gsum gyi nyams snang gi rnal 'byor pa la thos bsam dang bslab pas rgyud sbyangs pa dbang gis rgyud dag pa sogs dgos par bshad la/
nyams bco lnga po rnams kyang thun mong ma yin pa'i nyams yin pas dbang ma bskur bar de dag bstan na/ gsang sgrog 'byung / ci ste nyams bco lnga po thun mong ba'i lam
yin na mdo sde'i gzhung gang nas bshad/ khyad par rje btsun gyis gzhung ji lta ba bzhin bkri ba'i khrid yig tu/ thog mar snang ba gsum gyis bkri/ de'i rjes kho na la rgyud
gsum gyis bkri bar gsungs na/ de gnyis kyi bar der rgyu dbang byed pa de su'i lugs yin ces pa'i don no/ /yang rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyi dri ba gsum pa ni/ snang gsum
lam gyi bzhi bca' ba/ /rang rkang tshul du 'chad pa yi/ /khyad par gang yin gsal por smros/ /gzhi bca' zhes pa'i nges tshig ci/ /zhes pa yin la/ de'i lan la byang chub dbang
rgyal gyis/ zer mod gzhi bca' rang rkang gnyis/ /go rims ji bzhin bkri ba dang / /rkang 'don tshul du bkri ba yi/ /so so'i skabs su shes bya zhing / /gzhi yis nges tshig
yod pa yi/ /lam ngos min par khas len na/ /rgyud gsum bkri ba'i skabs su gzhi/ /dam tshig la gnas zhes gsungs pas/ /dam tshig nyi shu lam min par/ /khas len dgos pa
ma yin

nam/ /des na smra ba nyung na mdzes/ /zhes gsungs so/ /yang rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyi dri ba bzhi pa ni/ gzhan yang grwa ston zhus lan nas/ /'byung ba'i lam rim lam 'bras
dang / /rgyud gsum dang ni mdo rgyud spyi'i/ /lam rim gsum po gang du 'tshal/ /dang po ltar na snang gsum gyi/ /sngon du dbang bskur bshad 'dug gam/ /gnyis pa ltar na tshul
de dang / /'gal ba'i lam 'bras rgyud gsum nas/ /bshad pa min par khas long zhig /phyi ma ltar na lam 'bras dang / /mi mthun lam de mdo rgyud kyi/ /dgongs par grub phyir
lam 'bras kyi/ /go rim de 'dra gang nas byon/ /mdo rgyud kun dang mi mthun pa'i/ /lam de gong ma'i dgongs pa zhes/ /smra ba de dag gad mo'i gnas/ /zhes pa'i lan du dri
lan de nyid las/ thog mar dbang po rab 'bring gsum gyis bkri ba'i khrid rim rtsod gzhir bzung nas/ sngar gyi dri ba'i tshig de ji lta ba bzhin bkod de/ zhes pa bzlog na
ji skad smra/ /zhes mgo sgre ba mdzad cing / de'i rjes su/ gzhan yang rgyu dus dbang gi sngon/ /snang gsum dgos pa'i skyabs gnas su/ /grwa ston zhu lan 'tshol mod kyi/ /de
ni spyir du mdo sngags kyi/ /lam gyi 'gro tshul bsdus pa tsam/ /bstan pa yin gyi khyad par du/ /gzhung bzhin bkri ba'i khrid kyi rim/ /nges par bstan pa ma yin la/ /yin
na snang gsum rgyud gsum gyi/ /go rim tshang bar ston dgos las/ /thun mong ma yin nyams snang dang / /dag pa'i snang ba'i ming tsam yang / /bstan pa med phyir snang gsum
gyi/ /snang ba phyed gnyis las med pa'i/ /snang

gsum bshad pa ngo mtshar zhing / /de rjes phar phyin gzhung lugs kyi/ /snying po don gyi man ngag ni/ /'di dag yin zhes ngos bzung na/ /thun mong yin pa gang gis bstan/ /des
na khyed rnams bzhes pa yis/ /khrid rim nges par zhus lan dang / /mthun par 'dod na de nyid las/ /dben par bsam gtan bsgom pa la/ /byis dang 'grogs na mi thob pas/ /skye
bo dag la skyo bsgom ste/ /'di yi dben thob log 'tsho ni/ /spong zhes gsungs na deng sang dus/ /lam 'bras khrom bshad mdzad pa ci/ /khyad par gsung ngag rin po che'i/ /med
mi rung ba'i khyad chos rnams/ /chab gcig bsdus pa glegs bam zhes/ /rje btsun chen pos dkar chag tu/ /grangs nges mdzad pa'i gzhung bor nas/ /phyis su la la'i ngor mdzad
pa'i/ /gdams yig tsam zhig gtsor byed pa/ /'di la dgos pa ci zhig yod/ /ces gsungs so/ /yang rje btsun dkon mchog lhun grub kyi dri ba lnga pa ni/ mdor na grwa ston zhus
lan dang / /mthun pa'i nyams len khungs ma zhig /gangs can 'di na yod dam med/ /yod na de yi mtshan gzhi dri/ /med na tshul de bshad pa la/ /dgos pa ci zhig yod dam dri/
/zhes pa'i dris lan du/ mdo rgyud bstan bcos la sogs nas/ /bshad pa'i lam rim thams cad dang / /mthun pa'i nyams len yod dgos shing / /med na bshad pa don med kyi/ /dam
bca' ha cang ma thal lam/ /des na gzhung shing bzhi po las/ /khrid tshul nyer brgyad nyer dgu zhes/ /gsungs pa de dag rnams dang ni/ /mthun pa'i

nyams len khungs ma zhig /gangs can 'di na yod dam med/ /yod na de yi mtshan gzhi dri/ /med na tshul de bshad pa la/ /dgos pa ci zhig yod dam ci/ /zhes pa brjod na lan ci zhig
/lung rigs gtan tshigs dang bral ba'i/ /gzhan la bab col smra ba 'di/ /skyes bu rdza yi khur thogs nas/ /rdo ba'i g.yul ngor 'jug pa 'dra/ /de dag rang dga'i dri lan
du/ /mdor bsdus tsam zhig brjod pa yin/ /zhes gsungs so/ /yang ngor lugs kyi bzhed pa'i snying po rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyi gsung ngag 'chad thabs kyi man ngag gsang ba
sgo 'byed las 'phros pa'i dris lan zab don snying po las/ /de ltar bshad ma thag pa'i khrid tshul de rnams kyi go rim gyi nges pa de ltar 'byung ba'ang rje btsun gong ma
nyid kyi bzhed pa yin te/ rje sa chen gyi dbang bzhi ngo sprod las/ mtshan nyid ldan pa'i bla ma la/ /snod dang ldan pa'i slob ma yis/ /dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob nas ni/
/rgyu dus lta bas rab brgyan pa'i/ /bum dbang bskyed rim thog mar bsgom/ /zhes dang / de'i rang 'grel las/ thog mar bla ma zhig la dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa gal che/
dbang de'ang brda tsam byin rlabs tsam ma yin par/ grub pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i bka' ma chad pa/ lhad ma zhugs pa zhig la dkyil 'khor chen por dbang bskur ba thob dgos/
de nas thog mar lta ba bsgoms la/ de'i ye shes cung zad skyes pa na zhes sogs dbang rjes de ma thag par lta ba 'khor 'das dbyer med ston par gsungs pa dang / a seng ma
las/ snang ba gsum gyis lam gyi gzhi bcas la/ /

nyams len ma lus rgyud gsum dag gis shes/ /zhes gsungs la/ de dang mthun par rje btsun gyis gzhung ji lta ba bzhin bkri ba'i khrid yig jo lcags kyi don du mdzad pa las/ snang
ba gsum gyis bkri ba'i skabs bstan zin to/ /de'i rjes kho na la rgyud gsum gyis bkri bar bya ste/ de la gsum/ rgyu chos can 'khor ba'i gnas tshul/ lam ji ltar bsgom pa'i
tshul/ 'bras bu sangs rgyas kyi sa'o/ /dang po 'dir mi 'chad de ma dag pa'i snang ba'i skabs su bstan zin to/ /lam la gsum ste gzhi dam tshig la gnas par bya ba dang /
gang zag bkri ba'i tshul gang yin pa dang / nges shes bskyed la ting nge 'dzin ngo shes par bya ba'i lam gyi sa mtshams bzhag pa'o/ /dang po ni lam thams cad kyi rtsa ba
yin cing / gang zag 'bring gi lam gyi gtso bo yin pas dam tshig nyi shu bskyang bar bya ste/ dbang dang dam tshig la gnas pa ni lam thams cad kyi gzhi yin no zhes snang
ba gsum gyis dkris zin nas dbang dang dam tshig ston par gsungs pa dang / rje sa paN gyis brda don gsal ba las/ dbang thob zin pa'i gang zag la dang po nyid nas lta ba ston
par gsungs pas zhes gsungs pa ltar yin la/ de dag la rang gi go tshod kyis rnam dbye cung zad re phye na/ rje btsun thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis gsung
ngag 'chad pa'i tshe snang gsum sngon du nges par dbang bskur ba byas nas khrid ston pa 'di skal ldan cig car ba dang / skal dman rim 'jug pa gang gis lam gyi bkri tshul
yin zhes dri ba mdzad pa la/ sgyi chu ba buddha shrIs de

gnyis gang yin gyi gsal kha ma phye bar lam 'bras tshar gnyis 'chad pa'i tshe gnyis pa de rtsod gzhir bzung nas mgo mtshungs kyi lan mdzad pas ni rdzong pa rang da lta phyag
len mdzad pa'i lam 'bras kyi khrid tshul 'di skal ldan cig car ba dang / skal dman rim 'jug pa'i lam gnyis kyi bkri tshul gang yang min gsungs pa 'dra ba zhig 'dug pa de
ltar bzhed na/ rtsa ba'i rgyud brtag pa gnyis pa las/ skal dman sems can 'dul dka' ba/ /gang gis 'dul bar 'gyur ba lags/ /zhes pa'i lan du/ dang por gso sbyong sbyin par
bya/ /zhes pa nas/ de rjes kyai rdo rje bstan/ zhes pa'i bar gsungs pa 'dis skal dman rim 'jug pa'i lam rim dang / de'i shugs la/ skal ldan sems can 'dul sla ba/ /gang
gis 'dul bar 'gyur ba lags/ /zhes pa'i zhu ba dang / de'i lan du/ dang por kyai rdo rje bstan/ /zhes pa don gyis thob par bshad pa des skal ldan cig car ba'i lam rim bstan
pa de mi 'thad par 'gyur zhing / de ltar bdag med mas gdul bya la skal dman rim 'jug pa dang skal ldan cig car ba gnyis su phye nas de gnyis 'dul thabs zhus pa dang / bcom
ldan 'das kyis de gnyis 'dul tshul gsungs pa'ang 'brel med du bzhed dgos par 'gyur ro/ de bzhin du chos rje byang chub dbang rgyal gyis kyang mgo mtshungs kyi lan mang
du mdzad mod/ spyir mgo mtshungs kyi lan gtan nas mi rung ba ma yin kyang / mgo mtshungs mi mtshungs brtags nas bya dgos te/ ma brtags par gya tshom du bkod na mgo sgre
mi nus pa mang du 'byung bas so/ /de'ang

mkhas pa'i dbang po dkon mchog lhun grub kyis/ snang gsum thun mong lam min na/ /sngags lam kho nar 'dod nus sam/ /nus na mdo rgyud thams cad kyi/ /snying po bsdus pa yin no
zhes/ /smra ba ne tso'i 'don pa ste/ /mdo sde'i snying po gang la byed/ /ces gsungs pa la/ chos kyi rje byang chub dbang rgyal gyis/ /de la snang ba gsum po ni/ /thun mong
lam yin shes byed med/ /yod na sngags lam yin nam ci/ /sngags lam yin na smin grol las/ /gzhan med smin byed yin nam ci/ /zhes sogs skyon brjod thams cad kyang / /rang
la log pa ma yin nam/ /de ltar min na snang ba gsum/ /mdo lam kho nar 'dod nus sam/ /nus na mdo rgyud thams cad kyi/ /snying po bsdus pa yin no zhes/ /smra ba ne tso'i
'don pa ste/ /sngags kyi snying po gang la byed/ /ces gsungs pa 'di'i mgo mtshungs dang po de ngo thog tsam la cung zad 'grigs pa ltar snang yang / mgo mtshungs phyi ma de
la rnam dpyad cher ma byung ste/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyi gsung de'i don ni snang gsum thun mong ma yin pa'i lam yin na/ gsung ngag lam 'bras 'di mdo rgyud thams cad
kyi snying po bsdus pa'i lam du mi 'gyur te/ snang gsum ni sngags lam du bsdus/ de las gzhan pa'i gsung ngag lam 'bras kyi nang na mdo sde'i snying por grub pa'i lam med
pas gang la ngos 'dzin zhes pa'i don yin la/ de la rje byang chub dbang rgyal gyis mgo mtshungs brjod pa'i don ni snang gsum mdo lam kho nar 'dod nus sam/ nus na lam 'bras
la mdo rgyud

kyi snying po bsdus pa'i lam rim zhes brjod pa mi rigs te/ snang gsum ni mdo lam yin/ sngags kyi snying po gang la ngos 'dzin zhes par song bas/ de la ni ngor lugs pa dag gis
lam 'bras la mdo rgyud gnyis ka'i lam tshang bar bshad pa'i sngags lam ni rgyud dbang bskur nas rgyud gsum gyi sgo nas bkri ba'i lam rim 'di yin zhes pa'i lan don mthun
du thebs pa'i phyir ro/ /de dag ni dgag sgrub kyi tshe brjod tshul gyi cha la rnam dbye cung zad phye ba yin gyi/ don gyi snying po ni gsung ngag 'chad pa'i tshe snang
gsum gyi sngon du dbang bskur ba 'di gtso bor rdzong lugs kyi phyag len la snang zhing / de lung rigs kyis sgrub pa'ang mdzad do/ /ngor lugs la gsung ngag 'chad pa'i tshe
thog mar snang ba gsum gyi khrid bstan/ de nas rgyu dbang bskur/ de nas sngags lam gyis bkri ba 'di gtso bor phyag len la mdzad cing / de'ang khrid yig jo lcags ma dang
grwa ston zhus lan gyi dgongs pa dang mthun par sgrub pa mdzad pa yin no/ /de la snang gsum gyi sngon du dbang bskur ba 'di gtan nas mi rung ba ma yin te/ skal ldan cig car
ba'i rigs can 'ga' zhig la thun mong ba'i lam gyi sbyangs ba sngon du ma song yang dang po nyid nas dbang bskur bas chog pa ni/ skal dman sems can 'dul dka' ba/ /zhes
sogs kyi shugs bstan gyi zhus lan dang / gdol pa smyig mkhan la sogs pa/ /gsod don don du sems pa po/ /de rnams kye rdo rje shes na/ /'grub 'gyur 'di la the tshom med/ /zhes
gsungs pa sogs la brten nas rje btsun gong ma dag gis gsal bar bshad pas

grub cing / de lta bu la gsung ngag 'chad pa'i tshe snang ba gsum gyi khrid nges par bstan mi dgos kyang / de bstan pas gzhung ji lta bzhin bkri ba'i khrid kyi kha tshang pa'i
dgos pa yod cing / gang zag des thun mong gi lam byams pa dang snying rje sogs bsgom pa la phan yon ma gtogs nyes pa 'byung ba'ang ma yin la/ dper na rgyu dbang thob
pa'i gang zag gis/ dbu ma'i lta khrid dang / zhi byed/ gcod khrid/ blo sbyong gi khrid la sogs pa nyan bsgom gnyis ka rung ba bzhin no/ des na gang zag de lta bu ma yin yang
rgyud sbyangs ba sngon du song ba'i gdul bya 'ga' zhig la snang gsum gyi sngon du dbang byas pas nyes pa med cing / dbang gi rjes su snang gsum bstan na mi legs pa'ang
ma yin par bshad do/ /yang snang gsum gyi sngon du dbang nges par dgos pa'ang ma yin te/ skal dman rim 'jug pa'i lam rim ltar na dang por 'khor ba'i nyes dmigs/ las rgyu
'bras/ 'chi ba mi rtag pa/ byams snying rje/ byang chub kyi sems sogs thun mong ba'i lam rnams kyis blo rim gyis sbyangs nas/ gzod sngags la mos shing sngags kyi snod rung
du gyur pa na dbang bskur zhing khrid ston pa ni mdo rgyud kyi lam spyi dang mi 'gal zhing gsung ngag rdo rje'i tshig rkang gi bzhugs tshul dang babs 'grigs pa dang /
der ma zad rje btsun rin po che'i grwa ston zhus lan 'di mdo rgyud spyi'i lam rim ston byed dang / gsung ngag gzhung ji lta ba bzhin gyi khrid rim dang mthun pa'i lam rim
ston byed gang yin la ngor rdzong gnyis mi mthun yang / de

gnyis gang yin la khyad par med de/ ji skad bshad pa'i khrid rim de zhus lan gsal ba der bshad pa'i lam gyi go rim dang mthun pas rje btsun gyi dgongs par snang bas so/ /de
ltar yang zhus lan de nyid las/ pha rol phyin pa'i lam gyi rim pa bshad zin pa'i 'og tu/ de tsam gyis kyang blo gros ma khengs pa'i/ /blo can sbyangs pa zab mo dag la mos/
/rdo rje 'chang dbang myur du sgrub 'dod pa/ /de la rdo rje theg pa sbyin par bya/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de ltar lugs gnyis po de'i dgongs pa len lugs 'di lta bu zhig
shes na ngor rdzong gnyis po ha cang mi mthun pa rgyab 'gal du song 'dug snyam pa'i blos dus 'da' mi dgos par 'gal med kyi gnad zab mo rtogs par 'gyur ro/ /rgyu mtshan
des na rdzong lugs kyi mi shes pa dag gis ngor pa'i lugs 'di rje btsun gong ma'i gsung dang mi mthun no zhes skur ba 'debs pa dang / ngor lugs kyi mi mkhas pa dag gis kyang
rje btsun gong ma'i bzhed pa ngor pa'i 'di kho na yin gyi rdzong pa'i lugs de sa lugs dang gtan nas mi mthun no zhes zer ba dag yod kyang / de dag ni chos spong ba'i
las su 'gro bas blo gros dang ldan pa dag gis bya ba ma yin te/ lugs de gnyis kar 'thad ldan yin par shes ldan gzu bor gnas pa'i mkhas pa dag gis mgrin gcig tu gsungs pas
so/ /de ltar yang mkhas pa'i dbang po dkon mchog lhun grub kyi gsung ngag bshad thabs kyi man ngag gsang ba sgo 'byed las 'phros pa'i dri lan zab don snying po las/ rje
btsun rdo rje 'chang chen po'i drung gi gsang ba sgo 'byed du nyams myong ma skyes

pa skyed par byed pa khrid kyi rnal 'byor la bzhi'i/ dang po gzhung ji lta ba bzhin du bkri ba'i gzhung shing la/ gzhung ji lta ba bzhin du bkri ba dngos dang / de'i gnad bsdus
nas nyams su len pa'i gdam ngag gnyis kyi/ dang po gzhi dam tshig la gnas par bya ba la gnyis/ dam tshig ma thob pa thob par byed pa dbang bskur ba dang / thob pa mi
nyams par byed pa'i phyir dam tshig gi tshogs bstan pa'o/ /dang po ni dbang chu chen mo la sogs pa gsum dang / yab yum gyi bskyed rim rgyas bsdus rnams la brten nas yab
yum gyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba rnam par dag pa blang ba'o/ /gnyis pa la gsum gyi/ dang po bsrung ba'i dam tshig ni rtsa ltung 'khrul spong dang / gnyis
pa bza' ba'i dam tshig ni bdud rtsi ril bu sgrub pa'i man ngag dang tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i cho ga rnams bshad cing nyan pa dang / gsum pa bsten pa'i dam tshig ni/ lam
rim pa gnyis tshul bzhin du nyams su len pa ste zhes sogs dang / gnyis pa gnad bsdus te nyams su len tshul ni/ lam 'bras khrid kyi snying po ni/ /zhes sogs kyi don/ rje btsun
dam pa 'di'i dgongs pas gzhung ji lta ba bzhin bkri ba'i khrid la lugs gnyis kyi dang po 'chad pa de'i tshe thog mar dbang bskur/ de rjes dam tshig gi chos skor dang
bskyed rim yan lag dang bcas pa/ tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i cho ga rnams 'chad par gsungs pa dang / gnyis pa ni lam rim pa gnyis tshul bzhin du nyams su len pa ste zhes gsungs
pas/ khrid kyi dmigs pa rnams phyogs mthun du

gsungs pa la/ gzhung ji lta ba bzhin du bkri ba dngos su mdzad pa'i lugs gcig dang / thog mar snang ba gsum gyi khrid mdzad/ de nas dbang bskur te lta ba 'khor 'das dbyer med
sogs nas rim par gsungs pa la/ de'i gnad bsdus te nyams su len pa'i gdams ngag ces tha snyad mdzad nas/ 'og ma 'di rje btsun dam pa de nyid kyis rtsal du ston nas gnang
ba 'dra bsam pa/ bdag lta bu dad pa la nor du byed pa'i lugs gnyis ka la dad pa mi 'dor bdag gi blo la shar ba de'i tshe/ rje sa paN gyi khrid yig dkar chag kyang dngos
bstan dang sbyar nas mdzad do zhes brjod na/ rjes btsun dam pa de'i dgongs par e 'gyur/ bkri tshul phyi ma'i shlau ka gcig po'i snying po dang / gnyis las gsum byung dang
/ kun dang / bla ma'i drin ces pa'i gsung gi nus pa gong gi gnyis po la ngos e 'dzin/ mdor na shlau ka gcig po'i 'bru gnon gsal ba gcig mkhyen zhes pa ni dri ba'o zhes
dang / lan la gzhung shing dngos las brtsams pa'i dri lan dang / gnad bsdus te nyams su blang tshul las brtsams pa'i dri lan gnyis su mdzad nas/ dang po la rjes btsun dam
pa 'di'i bzhed pas gzhung ji ltar ba bzhin du bkri ba'i gzhung shing las/ gzhung shing dngos dang / de'i gnad bsdus nas nyams su len tshul gnyis su mdzad pa de'i ngos 'dzin
thog ma nyid nas rgyu dus kyi dbang bskur te dam tshig la sogs pa bstan nas/ phyis snang ba gsum la sogs pa'i khrid kyi rim pa thams cad phyogs mthun du ston pa'i lugs
gcig dang / thog mar snang ba gsum gyi khrid

bstan/ de nas dbang bskur/ de nas lta ba sogs kyi khrid ston pa'i lugs gcig ste gnyis su mdzad nas/ phyi ma rtsal du ston pa ni gtan ma yin te/ bshad tshul gong 'og gnyis po
de la de tsam gyis khyad par 'byed pa'i dmigs bsal dang don thob ci yang mi snang ba dang / spyir snang ba gsum gyi sngon du dbang bskur ba mdzad pa'i phyag len de gdul
bya'i gang zag la ltos nas byar rung ba'i skabs du ma yod kyang / de tsam gyis snang ba gsum gyi sngon du dbang bskur nges par byed dgos pa bsgrub par mi nus shing / nus
kyang 'chad tshul de rdo rje theg pa'i rgyud gzhung nas bshad pa'i skal ldan cig car ba dang / skal dman rim 'jug pa'i lam gnyis po gang yin brtags na phyogs gnyis po gang
du'ang khas len nus pa dka' bar snang zhing / gzhung ji lta ba bzhin du bkri ba'i gzhung shing gi babs dang / phyag len gyi rim pa de gnyis 'grigs pa'ang shin tu dka'
bas gzhung ji lta bzhin du bkri ba'i gzhung shing dngos la go rim nges pa can de lta bu zhig nges par dgos par mi bzhed par mchis lags/ de lta na gsang ba sgo 'byed las/
dang po nyid nas dam tshig ma thob pa thob par byed pa mngon par dbang bskur ba bshad pa ma yin nam zhe na yin mod/ des de ltar bstan pa mtha' gcig tu nges pa ma yin te/
dam tshig ma thob pa thob par byed pa la dbang gi mngon par rtogs pa brgyad dang ldan pa'i sgo nas rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du smin byed kyi dbang bskur ba tshul bzhin
du bsgrub dgos pa yin la/ dbang bskur zhu ba po'i slob ma de la'ang

rigs legs par brtags te skal ldan cig car ba'i rigs can yin na thun mong ba'i lam gyis bkri ba la ma ltos par dang po nyid nas dbang bskur te lta ba la sogs pa bstan pas chog
pa yin yang / skabs 'dir gang zag skal dman rim 'jug pa bkri tshul gyi rnam gzhag gtso che bas/ de'i lugs la dbang gi sngon du thun mong ba'i lam gyis nges par bkri dgos
par dbang gi chu bo chen mo bklags pa tsam gyis kyang go bar nus pas/ snang ba gsum gyi khrid kyang gzhan don du slob ma rjes su bzung ba'i sa khongs su bsdus nas dbang
gi sngon 'gror bzhed pa yin gyi/ smin grol gnyis kyis phye ba'i phyi ma'i khongs su 'dren par mi mdzad par mchis lags/ gal te de ltar mi bzhed par dngos bstan sgra ji bzhin
pa de las gzhan ci yang bshad du med na snang ba gsum gyi khrid gang du ston gyi gsal kha ci yang med pas gsang ba sgo 'byed khas len pa dag gi lugs la snang ba gsum
gyi khrid gtan nas ston mi dgos par thal ba'i skyon du 'gyur ba ma lags sam zhes pa dang / gzhan yang snang ba gsum gyi khrid thog mar bstan nas/ de nas dbang dang dam tshig
sogs ston par gsungs pa'i khrid rim de gong ma'i gsung mang po zhig gis sgrub par mdzad rjes su/ rje btsun gong ma'i phyag len ma 'chugs pa rnams la bkri tshul de 'dra
ba zhig yod par snang yang / bar skabs su gdul bya la ltos nas dbang bskur dang po nas thob zin pa la khrid dmigs rnams phyi nas ston pa'i phyag len sgo yang phyogs nas
ston pa du ma zhig byung bar snang zhing / 'chad tshul de la snang ba gsum

gyi khrid ma bstan yang rung mod/ 'on kyang nges 'byung gi bsam pa bskul ba sogs dgos byed khyad par can du ma gzigs nas snang ba gsum yang khrid kyi kha tshang ba'i phyir
ston par mdzad pa yin gyi/ gzhung gi babs la go rim de 'dra zhig nges par dgos par bzhed pa ma yin pa 'dra lags zhes sogs dang / mdor na gzhung shing gi babs la dang por
snang ba gsum bstan nas dbang bskur te grol byed kyi lam rnams rim gyis ston pa dang / gdul bya la ltos nas ci rigs par ston du rung ba'i khyad par so sor shes na log rtog
kho nas dus 'da' mi dgos shing / thub pa'i bstan pa gces par 'dzin pa'i gang zag dam pa rnams la ngan smras 'ba' zhig byed pa'i sdig pa'i khur chen pos mi non par mchis
lags zhes gsungs shing / bdag gi bla ma mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos kyi grags pa'i gsung las/ snang gsum khrid kyi skyabs 'gro'i dmigs pa'i skabs/ /bla
ma bla ma'i rnam pa'am gang du bsgom/ /'ga' zhig rdo rje 'chang du bsgom zhes pa/ /phar phyin lam gyi snying por 'di 'thad dam/ /zhes pa'i dri ba mdzad nas/ de ltar 'dri
dgos pa'i rgyu mtshan du/ rdzong phyogs pa dag snang gsum khrid kyi skyabs 'gro la bla ma rdo rje 'chang du bsgom pa chos rje bla ma dam pa'i khrid yig sbas don gsal bar
de bzhin bshad pa la brten pa yin la/ de'i rgyu mtshan yang sngon la dbang bskur nas de'i rjes su snang gsum gyi khrid ston pas na skyabs 'gro'i skabs su bla ma rdo rje
'chang kye rdor du bsgom pa gzhir bzhag la/ de nyid

phyag len ma dag pa'ang ma yin te/ rje btsun gong ma'i skabs nas rgyud sbyangs ba sngon du song ba'i slob ma rnams la thog mar dbang bskur nas/ de nas snang gsum sogs khrid
kyi rim pa ston pa'ang mang du byung / yang rgyud sbyangs pa sngon du ma song ba 'ga' zhig gam sbyangs ba sngon du song ma song thun mong du tshogs pa rnams la thog mar
snang ba gsum gyi khrid rim phar phyin rang rkang la sbyar nas rgyud sbyangs te de tsam gyis chog par bzung nas sngags la mi mos pa dag la dbang mi bskur/ sngags la mos shing
rdo rje 'chang gi go 'phang myur du 'dod pa dag la dbang bskur te sngags lam gyi khrid sogs rgyas par 'chad pa da lta'i bar du ngor pa dag gi phyag len la yod cing /
grwa ston zhus lan du gsal bar 'byung ba de yin/ de ltar snga mo nas srol gnyis byung ba de mi sems par phyogs 'dzin gyi sgo nas chos spong gi las bsog pa 'ga' zhig chos
rje bla ma slob brgyud dang bcas pa la skur 'debs byed pa dang / ngor pa nang tshogs kyi lugs srol tha dad pa na yang paN chen kong ston gyis mdzad pa'i khrid yig na snang
gsum gyi skabs su bla ma rdo rje 'chang du bsgom par bshad pa dang / khyad par bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po brgyud 'dzin dang bcas pa snang
gsum khrid kyi skabs 'dir bla ma brgyud pa dang bcas pa rdo rje 'chang du bsgoms nas skyabs su 'gro bar mdzad pa la/ phyis kyi rang phyogs pa phal cher de ni mi 'thad
de/ snang gsum khrid 'di phar phyin lam gyi skabs yin zhing / pha rol tu phyin pa la bla ma rdo rje 'chang du bsgom pa med pa'i phyir/ des na

'di ni mi 'thad pa chen po yin no zhes ma brtags par cho nge chen po 'debs pa mang po 'dug pa'i rgyu mtshan gyis bris pa yin zhes pa dang / de'i 'og tsam du khyad par rnal
'byor dbang phyug birWa pa'i gsung ngag lam 'bras kyi lam gyi rim pa 'di skal dman rim gyis pa'i lam gyi bkri tshul kho nar 'dod pa'ang sngon gyi dam pa gong ma rnams la
skur 'debs su 'gro zhing / rang phyogs 'ga' zhig la sdang shugs kyi dmod par song bas 'di 'dra'i rigs gsung rab kyi gnad go ba rnams dang / de ma go'ang las 'bras la 'dzem
bag byed pa rnams kyis mi gsung ba zhu/ chos kyi spyan ldan ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub kyis/ snang gsum sngon du dbang skur ba/ /nges par dgos zhes zer ba yi/ /lam
'bras pa la 'di skad dri/ /zhes gsungs pa'i tshig gi nus pa myang shes na snang gsum gyi sngon du nges par dbang bskur ba dgos zer ba la dgag pa mdzad pa yin gyi/ spyi babs
sngon la dbang bskur nas lam 'bras kyi sngon 'gro dngos gzhi'i khrid bstan pa la dgag pa mdzad rgyu ma yin/ ngor pa rang gi lam 'bras kyi khrid 'chad tshul gyi dgongs
pa 'di grwa ston zhus lan las ji skad gsungs pa dang mthun pa yin zhing / deng sang gi gdul bya dag la bkri tshul gyi rim pa 'di legs shing skabs su babs pa yin/ de skad
du'ang ngor chen nyid kyi gsung sngar drangs pa'i 'phro las/ mdor na grwa ston zhus lan dang / /mthun pa'i nyams len khungs ma zhig /gangs can 'di na yod dam med/ /yod na
de yi mtshan gzhi 'dri/ /zhes gsungs pas kyang ngor

pa rang gi phyag len snang gsum khrid kyi rjes dbang bskur te/ de nas sngags lam gyi khrid ston par mdzad pa 'di grwa ston zhus lan gyi lung gis sgrub par mdzad pas/ deng sang
rdzong phyogs pa dag gis phyag len gyi rim pa 'di 'gog rgyu ga la yin/ des na rdzong phyogs pa'i rigs can kha cig gis rang gi phyag len tsam mthong ba'i rgyu mtshan gyis
snang gsum sngon du dbang bskur nges par byed zer ba de 'dra'ang grwa ston zhus lan dang dngos su 'gal bas sgro 'dogs kyi mthar lhung / ngor phyogs kyi ma go ba 'ga'
zhig gis kyang snang gsum sngon du dbang bskur ba gtan nas mi 'thad zer ba'ang gzhan la skur 'debs kyi mthar lhung zhing / jo lcags ma las rnal 'byor pa la/ ting nge 'dzin
la/ zhes sogs kyi rnal 'byor pa de la thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa gnyis su gsungs 'dug pa la ji ltar 'chad/ so so nas mi shes pa dag gis rang nyid gang la zhen pa'i
phyogs bzung nas gsung rab rang bzor bkral ba 'di nyes pa che bas phyogs 'dzin a 'thas kyi las bsog pa mi rigs so zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /gsum pa sta gon la 'brel ba
yod med kyi rnam gzhag ni/ mus srad pa chen po rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis/ sta gon 'brel ba med pa dang / /zhes pa'i rgyas bshad du/ slob ma smin byed rdul tshon gyi dkyil
'khor gcig tu thog ma'i dbang bskur tshar gcig po de rigs mod/ de'i rjes su dkyil 'khor gcig po de nyid kyi steng nas nyin re bzhin sta gon snga ma'i dngos gzhi re dang
/ dngos gzhi rting ma'i sta gon re spel nas zhu mkhan ma rdzogs kyi bar du byed

do/ /'di shin tu mi rigs pa'i rgyu mtshan smin byed rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor gcig tu dbang bskur gcig las lhag pa yang bskur du mi rung ste/ dkyil 'khor de la sta gon gcig
las med pa'i phyir zhes sa skya pa'i srol 'dzin gzhan thams cad 'chad la/ khyed kyi de ni bu ston gyi slob brgyud dag gi lugs yin gyis sa skya pa'i lugs min/ des na de
lta bu la gong ma'i lung yod na ston cig gal te sta gon gsum po de sngar byas pas chog ce na/ 'o na sgrub mchod sogs kyang sngar byas pa de nyid gnas pas nyi ma gzhan la
byed ci dgos zhes dang / gzhan yang rtsod pa dang rtsod lan 'ga' re bkod nas/ ngor lugs pas/ rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor gcig tu smin byed lan mang du byed pa 'di la ched
du rgol bar mdzad do/ /paN chen rin po che dang tshangs pa'i rigs sngags su gong du bkod pa de'i steng du gal te sta gon snga ma rnams bskyar nas byed ce na/ dkyil 'khor
bsgrubs zin nas de'i lha sta gon ji ltar byed ces dang / gzhan yang 'brel med kyi rtsod lan kha cig bkod nas/ de'i shugs la sgrub mchod rting ma rnams kyi tshe lha sta gon
byed thub pa zhig yod na/ sta gon 'brel pa med pa dang / /zhes pa'i rgol ba de bzlog thub par khas len no zhes pa rgol ba'i gsung du bkod nas so so'i lan re'ang mdzad mod/
mus srad pa chen po'i chu rgyun bzhi pa'i dpe phal cher las kho bos bkod pa de las phyi ma de dag dngos shugs gang la'ang mi snang ngo / /de dag la lan 'debs paN chen
rin po che'i rnam thar sgo brgyad par shin tu rgyas pa zhig 'byung

ba'i rkang grangs rags pa tsam brjod na/ dngos bstan rtsod phreng so so'i lan dang / zhe 'dod dgongs pa'i lan dpyis phyin pa dang gnyis su mdzad nas/ dang po la'ang rtsa ba'i
gtan tshigs ma nges pa dang / de sgrub byed kyi rigs pa mtha' ma chod pa gnyis su mdzad nas/ dang po la 'o na smin byed kyi dkyil 'khor gcig la lha sta gon gcig las med
cing / gcig po de slob ma gral gong ma de'i sta gon dang 'brel la/ gral 'og ma rnams kyis sta gon la 'brel yul gyi lha sta gon med pas na dkyil 'khor gcig tu slob ma gcig
las lhag pa la smin byed mi rung bar 'gyur la/ gal te lha sta gon gcig pu de slob ma gral 'og ma rnams kyi sta gon dang yang 'brel zer na/ dbang tshar rting ma rnams kyi
slob ma sta gon yang lha sta gon gcig pu de dang 'brel bar mtshungs pas sta gon gcig pu ji srid gnas kyi bar du dkyil 'khor yongs rdzogs gnas/ de gnas pa de srid du slob
ma sta gon gyi snod du rung ba stong tsam byung yang smin du rung ngo / yang khyed kyi zhe 'dod dbang tshar rting ma rnams la slob ma sta gon gzhi ma grub zer bar song
ba/ de ni legs par grub pas na rtsa ba'i gtan tshigs de la 'gal ma nges ma grub pa'i skyon gsum kar tshang bas ltar snang yin par gsungs/ gnyis pa sgrub byed kyi rigs pa
mtha' ma chod pa la rtsa ba'i gtan tshigs de'i rtags chos kyi 'brel pa ni lha sta gon gcig las med na slob ma sta gon yang gcig las mi rung zhes pa dang / lha sta gon gcig
las med pas gcig pu de slob ma sta gon dang po la 'brel nas rdzogs pas na/ tshar rting ma rnams

la lha sta gon dang 'brel ba med ces pa dang / lha sta gon zhig bskyar nas byed na slob ma sta gon 'brel pa srid kyang de med ces pa dang / snga ma gnas pas bskyar mi dgos
na ha cang thal ches pa rnams su song bas/ dang po la 'o na slob ma nyer lnga po re re la sta gon re re te nyer lnga yod pas lha sta gon yang nyer lnga yod dgos par 'gyur/
de mi dgos na 'brel zla dang 'brel yul grangs mnyam dgos pa dang 'gal lo/ /sta gon snga ma gnas pa de la rting ma bskyar dgos sam mi dgos/ dgos na slob ma sta gon rting
ma de lha sta gon rting ma dang 'brel bas sta gon 'brel pa yod par 'gyur/ bskyar mi dgos na sgrub mchod phyi ma rnams kyang bskyar mi dgos par 'gyur te snga ma gnas pa'i
phyir ro/ /des na dngos lan ni/ dbang tshar rting ma rnams byed pa'i tshe lha sta gon gnas pas bskyar mi dgos shing / dgos kyang skyor thabs med pa ma yin te/ sgrub mchod
dang po'i dus su sta gon gyi lha nam mkhar bteg pa de ji srid kyi bar nam mkhar bzhag nas skabs su babs pa re re'i tshe mar me gcig las gnyis mched kyi tshul du dkyil 'khor
la bcug chog pa'i phyir/ gzhan du na rang bzhin gyi gnas nas 'dir spyan drangs pa'i tshe gnas de na lha med par 'gyur ro gsungs/ gnyis pa zhe 'dod dgongs pa'i lan dpyis
phyin pa la rgol ba po'i bsam pa blangs nas nyes pa de rang la med cing gzhan la yod pa dang / rgol ba po nyes pa dang bcas par bstan pa dag tu mdzad nas/ dang po la/
rgol ba po ltar na slob ma rjes 'dzin nyer lnga la byas pa de dag

gi don du bzhengs pa'i dkyil 'khor de dang / dbang tshar rting ma bskur rgyu'i slob ma rnams la 'brel pa med pas dbang rting ma mi rung zer rgyur snang ba/ snang gsum gyi khrid
zin pa'i slob ma mang po la grangs nges med par rjes bzung byed pa grub cing / ma byas na nyes pa chen po yod pas de ltar rjes bzung byas pa de dang / de dag gi don
du bzhengs pa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor shin tu 'brel/ sta gon bzhi po'ang go rim ji lta ba bzhin du 'brel bas/ rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor gcig pu de slob ma ji tsam pa
thams cad smin byed kyi dkyil 'khor du rung ba yin no zhes pa dang / rgol ba po nyes pa can du bstan pa la khas blangs 'gal ba dang / nyes pa chen po gzhan gyis gnod pa
gnyis su mdzad nas/ dang po la dbang tshar dang po byas zin pa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor la sta gon bskyar ma dang / sgrub mchod bskyar na sta gon 'brel ba yod par 'dod
pa dang / dbang tshar rting ma mi rung bar khas len pa 'gal bar gsungs/ nyes pa chen po gzhan gyis gnod pa la rdul tshon la dbang tshar gcig las mi rung na ras bris la'ang
mi rung bar 'gyur/ ras bris smin byed ma yin pa la de ltar rung ba dang / gzhan du spyan 'dren du btub pas de gnyis mi mtshungs she na/ rdul tshon la'ang smin byed ma
yin pa la de ltar rung zhing / de ring gi rdul tshon mi dmigs par byas rjes sang gi rdul tshon la de ltar rung bar 'gyur ro/ mdor na rdul tshon dang ras bris gang yin kyang
rung / slob ma smin byed du rung mi rung ni slob ma dang dkyil 'khor de la 'brel pa yod med la thug de'ang dbang

gi mngon par rtogs pa mtha' dag tshang ma tshang la thug de tshang ba'ang rang don du bzhengs pa'i dkyil 'khor de la dgos pa'i yo byad rnams slob dpon la sbyar ba nas bzung
mngon par rtogs pa bshad tshod rnams tshang na ras bris kyang smin byed du 'gro ba ni dbang chu'i dgongs pa dang / de ma tshang na rdul tshon yang smin byed du mi 'gro ba
ni chos rje pa'i dgongs pa'o/ /nges pa'i don du blos bslangs dang tshon rtsi las grub pa sogs ni dmigs pa'i rkyen tsam yin gyi/ smin byed kyi dkyil 'khor dngos ni ye shes
las grub pa nyid gtso bo yin no zhes sogs gsungs so/ /yang tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i rdo rje 'khrul 'khor gyi zegs ma las/ smra ba gsum pa nub dang po las lha/ bum
pa sta gon byas pa'i nub de kho na la slob ma sta gon byed kyi/ nub phyi ma phan chod kyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor dang 'brel bar slob ma sta gon bya mi rung ste/ de'i
dus kyi slob ma sta gon dang sta gon snga ma gsum la 'brel pa med pa'i phyir zer ro zhes khas blangs bkod nas/ lan dngos la de ltar na nub phyi ma rnams la sgrub mchod
kyang mi rung bar 'gyur te/ de dus kyi dngos gzhi'i sgrub mchod la sta gon snga ma gsum dgos pa gang zhig de med par ma zad de dang 'brel pa tsam yang med pa'i phyir/ gzhan
yang dkyil 'khor gcig tu dbang lan gcig las bskur du mi rung na ras bris la'ang mtshungs shing / rje btsun chen po'i gzhan phan bdud rtsir nub drug gi bar du rdul tshon
gyi dkyil 'khor du sbrel nas dbang bskur ba bshad pa sogs gnod byed mtha' yas so/ /des na rdul

tshon gyi dkyil 'khor gcig tu dbang lan mang du bskur ba sa skya pa'i lugs min/ bu ston pa'i slob brgyud dag gi lugs yin zer ba rje btsun chen po ngor pa dang bzhed pa gcig
pa 'dug pas sa skya pa'i khyu nas 'bud kyang bu ston pa'i slob brgyud du 'ong don med pas thugs dran bsten pa zhu zhes nyams ldan dang bcas gsungs so/ yang mkhas pa'i dbang
po dkon mchog lhun grub kyis tshangs pa'i rig sngags su mgo mtshungs dang / rnal ma'i lan gnyis su mdzad nas/ dang po la/ 'o na smin byed kyi dbang tshar re la gzhi bsnyen
dang sa chog sogs zhal dang 'dra ba'i cho ga'i gzhi chen po mtha' dag tshar re bya dgos par 'gyur te/ smin byed re la sta gon re byed dgos pa gang zhig brgyad po de
smin byed la dgos pa'i cho ga yin par mtshungs pa'i phyir/ mi mtshungs te bsnyen pa kha gso tsam dang / dkyil 'khor gyi khang pa rnying par sa chog ma byas kyang rung bar
bshad pas so snyam na/ 'o na sngar byas zin pa'i gzhi bsnyen dang / sa chog rnams dang / da lta'i slob ma'i don du bzhengs pa'i dkyil 'khor la 'brel pa de med pas na/ gzhi
bsnyen 'brel pa med pa dang / /sa chog 'brel pa med pa dang / /zhes pa'i nyes pa re'ang 'byung ngo zhes pa dang / gzhan yang rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor gcig tu slob ma
gcig las gzhan la dbang bskur du mi rung bar 'gyur ba'i gnod byed paN chen gyi gsung de dang phal cher mthun pa zhig 'god par mdzad nas/ de'i rjes su yang 'brel zla'i don
slob ma la mi byed par cho ga de'i byed las la byed zer na/ 'o na sta gon dang 'jug pa'i tshe las

bum gyi bskyed chog re re dang bum chus gsang ba re re spel nas bya dgos pa dang / rin 'byung cod pan gyi dbang man chad kyi mtha' rten chu dbang re la'ang bum pa las bskyed
chog re bya dgos par 'gyur te/ cho ga tshar re dang de'i byed las re 'brel dgos pa'i phyir/ gal te bum pa sta gon dang chu dbang gi tshe bsgrubs zin pas mi dgos snyam na
de ni sta gon la'ang mtshungs so/ /de la dngos gzhi sgrub mchod kyi mtshungs pa byed pa ni blun po'i rigs pa ste mi mtshungs pa'i rgyu mtshan slob ma dbang bskur dang rang
nyid bdag 'jug len pa gnyis ka la dbang blang ba'i yul tshul bzhin du bsgrub dgos la/ de lta bu'i dkyil 'khor bsgrub pa dang / bdag 'jug len pa dang / slob ma la dbang
bskur ba gsum cho ga rigs mi mthun gzhan gyis bar ma chod par 'brel chags su dgos pas so/ /de sta gon la'ang mtshungs she na/ lha sta gon dang dngos gzhi sgrub mchod gnyis
kyi bar du lha'i rnal 'byor gzhan dang cho ga gzhan mi rung ba khyod khas long zhig ces pa dang / rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor gcig tu sta gon gcig las med pas dbang tshar
gcig las mi rung ba/ gzhan phan bdud rtsi las/ mdor na sta gon nub gcig dngos gzhi nub drug la lhag ma gshegs pas nub bdun du 'gro bas bdun tshigs zhes bya ba yin te
zhes gsungs pa dang 'gal gsungs shing / yang sta gon snga ma rnams bskyar nas byed na dkyil 'khor bsgrubs zin pas sta gon ji ltar byed ces pa'i dkyil 'khor sgrub pa de ci/
dngos gzhi sgrub mchod dam dkyil 'khor

bris pa gang la byed/ dang po ltar na sta gon de la ltos pa'i dkyil 'khor bsgrubs zin pa brgya byin gyis kyang sgrub mi nus/ phyi ma ltar na ras bris kyi phyogs la sta gon
bya mi rung bar 'gyur te/ sta gon de'i sngon du ras bris de bris zin pa'i phyir dang / dkyil 'khor bris zin nas sta gon ji ltar byed ces smras na chos dang mthun pa'i lan
mi 'dug pa'i phyir zhes gsungs/ gnyis pa rnal ma'i lan la rgol ba'i bsam pa blang pa/ rang lugs nyes med du bstan pa/ rgol ba po nyes pa can du bstan pa rnams su mdzad nas/
dang po la khyod ltar na rjes bzung gi skabs kyi slob ma nyer lnga po'i don du bzhengs pa'i dkyil 'khor der nyer lnga las gzhan smin byed mi rung ste/ nyer lnga las gzhan
pa'i slob ma rnams dang dkyil 'khor de la 'brel pa med pa'i phyir dang / dngos gzhi phyi ma rnams la sta gon med pa'i phyir snyam du sems pa'o zhes gsungs/ rang lugs
nyes med du bstan pa la snang gsum gyi khrid zin pa'i slob ma mang po la grangs nges med par rjes bzung bya rung bar grub cing / slob ma de dag gi don du bzhengs pa'i dkyil
'khor dang de rnams shin tu 'brel pa dang / sa lha dang lha sta gon byas pa'i dgos pa ni/ sa phyogs der dkyil 'khor bzhengs su rung ba dang / slob ma'i ched du dkyil
'khor bris te gzhan don bya ba'i gnang ba zhu ba dang / byin gyis brlabs pa'i ched yin la/ de tsam ni sta gon gcig pu des grub/ bum pa dang slob ma sta gon yang ji tsam skabs
su babs pa'i tshe byas pas/ dbang zhu ba ji snyed pa dag la mngon par rtogs pa brgyad car tshang

bas smin byed du mi rung ba'i dogs pa skye don med la/ dkyil 'khor gcig tu smin byed gcig las mi rung bar smra ba'i sa skya pa'i srol 'dzin gzhan su zhig ces dris na ston rgyu
med/ 'ga' zhig yod na'ang de dang khyod gnyis char gang zag gcig la smin byed gcig las med par bshad pa de dkyil 'khor gcig tu smin byed gcig las mi rung bar go 'dug
pas ches blun pa yin no gsungs/ rgol ba po nyes can du bstan pa la/ khyod ltar na sgrub mchod phyi ma rnams la sta gon gyi 'brel ba med pas smin byed ma yin pa'i dbang dang
/ sgrub mchod kyang nyin zhag sbrel nas mi rung bar 'gyur/ de 'dod na gong du drangs pa'i gzhan phan bdud rtsi'i lung dang 'gal lo/ /gzhan yang dkyil 'khor gcig tu dbang
re las mi rung na deng sang gi rdo rje slob dpon dag la gsang ba chos kyi dkyil 'khor gsum po re re las med/ de dag gi tshe gang la dbang gong ma gsum tshar re las bskur
mi rung bar 'gyur la/ der ma zad ras bris kyi steng nas smin byed tshar gcig byas pa'i ras bris de'ang rdul tshon bzhin du chu bor spyan 'dren pa'am rgyas btab ste dben
par 'jog pa sogs bya rigs par 'gyur/ gal te de la sta gon bskyar bas rung snyam na de rdul tshon la ci'i phyir mi mtshungs/ legs par brtags na ras bris dang / sa 'dir dkyil
'khor bri bar bya/ /zhes pa'i sa gnyis la khyod 'dod pa'i 'brel ba de med pas ras bris su sgrub mchod kyang mi rung bar 'dod dgos/ de rung na ni/ dkyil 'khor 'brel ba
med pa dang / /zhes pa'i dogs pa'ang

'jug go /ma yin te dkyil 'khor bri zhes pa ting nge 'dzin gyi dkyil 'khor la'ang rung snyam na/ kho bo cag la rung yang khyed la 'gal te dkyil 'khor bris zin nas sta gon bskyar
thabs med pas so/ /de ltar na'ang rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor gcig tu smin byed tshar mang po rung ba'i gong ma'i gsung bstan dgos zer na/ de mi rung ba'i lung khyed
kyis bstan dgos/ des na 'di rigs dkyil chog dag las dbang tshar re bskur ba'i tshul las mi 'byung bas dngos bstan de las gzhan bya ma shes/ bla ma mkhas pa'i mthong ba brgyud
pa'i phyag len yang med pas byis pa'i blos chu la brgal ma nus pa'i mun sprul la khyad nor du bzung ba yin gsungs so/ /de'i don bsdus don brgyad pa las/ de lta yin na
rje rtse mos/ /mdzad pa'i Dombhi dkyil chog las/ /sgrub mchod nyi ma lngar byas nas/ /sta gon gcig la dngos gzhi gnyis/ /mdzad pa'i dngos gzhi dang po la/ /rab gnas dang
ni gnyis pa la/ /slob ma dbang skur byed do zhes/ /gsal bar gsungs pa ma shes par/ /gong ma'i chos rnams 'gegs par zad/ /rtse mo 'gegs pa'i sa skya pa'i/ /rjes 'brangs
rnying pa gang nas byon/ /rje btsun chen pos dus mtha' ma'i/ /sta gon gcig la dngos gzhi drug /byed par bshad pa'i phyi ma lnga/ 'brel med yin phyir mi rung bar/ /rjes 'brangs
tha shal khyed 'dod dam/ /rje btsun dgag pa'i sa skya pa/ /rnying pa de 'dra gad mo'i gnas/ /dkyil 'khor gcig tu dbang bskur ba/ /gcig las nam yang mi rung na/ /ras
bris bzhengs pa don re chung / /sta gon

bskyar nas rung zhe na/ /dkyil 'khor bsgrubs nas sta gon ni/ /ji ltar byed ces khyed nyid kyis/ /gzhan la smras pa de brjed dam/ /slob dpon lus kyi dkyil 'khor ni/ /gcig las
med phyir lus dkyil du/ /dbang bskur slob dpon tshe gang la/ /gcig las byed du mi rung bar/ /gzhung bshad mkhas rlom khyed 'dod dam/ /de lta na ni lam 'bras kyang / tshar
gcig nyid las mi rung bar/ /thal ba 'di la 'dod lan thob/ /mdor na 'di 'dra'i grub mtha' ni/ /mthong ba brgyud pa'i phyag len gyis/ /brgyan pa'i slob dpon ma bsten par/
/dkyil chog rnams kyi tshig rigs la/ /thug phrad byas pa'i gtam du snang / /zhes kyang gsungs so/ /de ltar rgyas par gsungs pa dag gi lan la mkhan chen bzang bkras pas
snyan brgyud 'khrul sel las/ tshangs pa'i rig sngags las byung ba'i mgo mtshungs kyi rigs pa rnams brjod pa'i rjes su/ 'o na smin byed tshar re la/ /slob ma sta gon tshar
re dang / /'jug cing dbang bskur len pa sogs/ /tshar re dgos na bsnyen sogs brgyad/ /tshar re dgos sogs sgrub byed kun/ /ri bong tshang log cis mi 'gyur/ /sgrub mchod la
sogs bar ma chad/ /dgos na dbang chur sgrub mchod dang / /'jug pa'i bar du sbyin sreg sogs/ /gsungs pa ma mthong de nyid bstan/ /zhes pa dang / yang tshangs pa'i rig sngags
las rnal ma'i lan gsungs tshul bkod pa'i rjes su/ sta gon dang po gnyis po de/ /tshar re byas pa'i dgos pa des/ /dbang bskur phyi ma kun 'grub na/ /bdag

mdun 'jug pa bum sgrub sogs/ /kun kyang tshar res dbang bskur kun/ /'grub par 'gyur te dgos pa mtshungs/ /khyed la'ang slob ma sta gon dang / /dngos gzhi grangs mnyam dgos
pa'i phyir/ /rin 'byung man la bum chog re/ /dgos pa mtshungs shing rdul tshon gyi/ /dkyil 'khor gcig tu gshin po la/ /dbang bzhi nub drug bskur ba'i rjes/ /gshegs gsol dgos
ltar lus dkyil gsum/ /gshegs gsol dgos pa'i rigs pa mtshungs/ /gshegs gsol rdul tshon gzhir bzhag nas/ /drug gam gcig kyang de bzhin yin/ /zhes pa dang / yang tshangs
pa'i rig sngags su ras bris dang rdul tshon du dbang tshar gcig las rung mi rung gi mtshungs pa mdzad pa bkod pa'i rjes su/ ras bris dkyil 'khor gcig nyid du/ /dbang bskur
yang yang rung ba ltar/ /rdul tshon yang yang 'degs 'jog sogs/ /shes na khyod ni rdzu 'phrul che/ /sa 'dir dkyil 'khor sogs kyi don/ /bsgrub bya yin gyis sgrub byed min/
/mdor na brgya phrag brgal ba la/ /dmigs nas sta gon gcig nyid kyis/ /dngos gzhi du ma rung gyur na/ /'o na sta gon gcig nyid kyis/ tshe gang go chod 'gyur ba sogs/ /ha
cang thal phyir log pa yin/ /rdul tshon dkyil 'khor gcig nyid du/ /lus rten gcig la zhag drug bar/ /dbang bskur rung gis zhag bdun nas/ /dkyil 'khor gsar du 'dri dgos na/
/lus rten 'phos pa'i rigs pa yis/ /de 'dra'i dkyil 'khor gcig nyid du/ /dbang tshan tha dad gyur pa la/ /dbang bskur min zhing dkyil 'khor yang / /tha dad

dgos pa smyon med grub/ /'di yis khyed kyi grub mtha' de'i/ /ngan tshang thams cad brtol ba yin/ /zhes gsungs/ yang sgyi chu ba buddha shrI'i yang lan nor bu'i phreng bar tshangs
pa'i rig sngags kyi mgo mtshungs kyi lan rnams la lan 'debs gang yang ma mdzad la/ rnal ma'i lan gyi rang lugs nyes med du bstan pa rnams kyi yang lan du/ 'di ni rgya
bod kyi rdo rje 'dzin pa rnams la med pa'i grub mtha' ste/ khyod kyi dbang bskur phyi ma rnams la bdag bskyed kyang mi dgos par 'gyur te/ bdag bskyed byas pa'i dgos pa
ni bdag nyid lhar bskyed pa yin la/ de tsam gyis skabs don bdag bskyed gcig pu des grub zin par mtshungs pa'i phyir zhes pa dang / de bzhin du mdun bskyed kyi dgos pa dbang
len pa'i dmigs rten dang / mchod pa'i dgos pa bsod nams kyi tshogs gsog pa dang / bdag 'jug gi dgos pa dam tshig nyes pa bsal nas slob ma byin gyis brlabs pa'i phyir
dang / bum pa sta gon gyi dgos pa dbang bskur ba'i phyir rnams yin la/ dgos pa de dag mdun bskyed sogs de dag dang po de rnams kyis grub zin pas/ dbang phyi ma rnams la
mdun bskyed sogs mi dgos par 'gyur ro zhes mtshungs pa brjod nas/ skabs don grub kyang cho ga kha lag tshang ba'i phyir yin zer na sa lha sta gon la'ang ci'i phyir mi mtshungs/
gal te dngos gzhi'i sngon 'gro gtor ma nas mjug gi bya ba'i bar cho ga tshar gcig yin pas mi mtshungs snyam na/ dbang gi chos brgyad po de dag cho ga tshar gcig yin
cing / rjes bzung bsnyen pa sa chog

gsum ni cho ga de'i yan lag yin pas dbang bskur ba man chad du mi dgos la/ lhag ma lnga ni sbyor dngos rjes gsum tshang ba'i cho ga tshar gcig yin pas dus thams cad du mtshungs
so/ /gzhan yang tshe stod la sta gon tshar gcig byas pas khyod rang gi tshe ril po dbang bskur ba'i sta gon gyi go chod par 'gyur te/ khyod rang gi sta gon byas pa'i
skabs don de dag sta gon gcig pu des 'grub pa'i phyir dang / rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor gcig gis slob ma brgya stong grangs med pa smin gyi 'dug pa'i phyir ro/ /yang dkyil
'khor de dang tshogs de dag 'brel ba'i phyir zhes pa'i don ci/ tshogs de dag gi don du bzhengs pas zer na/ rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor des sems can thams cad smin par gyis
shig ces gsungs/ yang tshangs pa'i rigs sngags su ras bris dang rdul tshon gnyis dkyil 'khor gcig tu smin byed tshar mang po rung mi rung gi mtshungs pa brjod nas/ dbang
bskur tshar re la sta gon tshar re dgos pa'i lung bstan dgos zhes sogs kyi lan du/ ras bris dang rdul tshon mtshungs pa ma yin te/ ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor gcig nyid
du sbyor dngos rjes gsum tshang ba'i cho ga re byas nas/ slar yang de bzhin du byas pas dbang tshan mi gcig pa mang du smin pa mngon sum du mthong na/ khyod kyis rdul tshon
gyi dkyil 'khor du ras bris ltar gyis shig kho bos khyod grub pa thob par khas blangs so/ /dbang gi rgya gzhung bod gzhung thams cad dbang tshar re sta gon tshar re dgos
pa'i bshad pa dang lag len kho na yin na sems rnal du phob cig kye rdo rje'i ras bris

dang rdul tshon du dbang bskur ba la sta gon mi dgos zer zhing lag len du byed pa khyod min su yang ma byung ngo / /des na rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor kho na smin byed du 'dod
pa grub pa'i mthar byas pa 'di dang / dad pa'i rjes 'brang gi slob tshogs mang ba 'di dang / rdul tshon yang nas yang du 'dri mi nus pa'i las sla 'di gsum gyis rdo rje
theg pa'i bstan pa rmang nas zhig pa ma mkhyen pa'i rdo rje slob dpon mang du mthong ste dbang lam gyi rtsa ba yin pas skal ldan dag zon gyis shig ces gsungs so/ /yang tshangs
pa'i rigs sngags su dkyil 'khor sgrub pa dang bdag 'jug dang dbang gsum gyi bar du cho ga rigs mi mthun gzhan gyis bar ma chod pa dgos pa dang / sta gon dang dngos
gzhi sgrub mchod la de mi dgos par gsungs pa'i lan du/ de ltar na slob dpon rin po ches dkyil 'khor sgrub cing mchod pa'i cho ga'o/ /rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg byed na bar 'dir
sbyin sreg gi cho ga las 'byung ba ltar sbyin sreg bya'o/ /gal te rab tu gnas pa byed pa yin yang de'i tshe rab gnas kyi sta gon bya'o/ /gal te dkyil 'khor nub gsum pa'i
lugs su byed na yang de'i nub mo rab gnas kyi sta gon byas la phyi nyin/ snga dro rab gnas kyi dngos gzhi dang rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg byas la/ de'i nub mo slob dpon bdag
nyid 'jug cing dbang blang ba dang slob ma gzhug cing dbang bskur ba'i bar du bya'o/ /gal te rab tu gnas pa la sogs pa mi byed de/ dkyil 'khor nub gsum par yang mi byed
na de ltar sgrub cing mchod pa'i rjes la slob dpon bdag nyid 'jug cing dbang bskur

bar bya ste de'i cho ga ni zhes gsungs na/ rab gnas sbyin sreg sogs dang dkyil 'khor nub gsum pa sogs kyi 'jug pa ma shar bar/ rang nyid sgrub mchod bdag 'jug dbang bskur ba
gsum bar ma chad par byas pa blo yul du bzhag nas/ dbang chu chen mo tshar gcig kyang ma bklags par sa skya pa'i bstan 'dzin du khas blangs te 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi
khur 'khur ba ngo mtshar che'o/ /des na rje ngor chen nyid ni las rgyu 'bras la shin tu brtsi bar grags na 'di lta bu'i rtsing chos la grub mthar byas nas bla ma mkhas
pa'i phyag len mthong brgyud du smra zhing yi ge ris su bris pa 'dis rje btsun sa skya pa'i bstan pa 'jig cing dad ldan mang po bslu ba dang ngor pa chen po'i zhabs ri rtse
nas drangs pa kho bos mthong ngo zhes gsungs so/ /de ltar ngor rdzong gnyis kyi bzhed pa mi 'dra ba de dag las rdzong lugs kyi dgongs pa'i snying po slob ma sta gon sta
gon gzhan gsum dang 'brel chags su ma byung na slob ma sta gon gyi cho ga de cho ga rnam dag tu mi 'gyur zhing / slob ma sta gon rnam dag ma byas pa la dngos gzhi bskur
du mi rung la/ rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor gcig tu lha sta gon tshar gcig las med cing / gcig pu de dang tshar rting ma'i slob ma sta gon 'brel chags su ma byung bas dbang
yang tshar gcig las mi rung ba yin zhes pa dang / ngor pa'i bzhed pa ni lha sta gon byas pa'i dgos pa gzhan don byed par gnang ba zhu ba yin pas de nyid ni lha sta gon
gcig pu des grub pas/ lha sta gon gcig pu de dang slob ma sta gon nges par 'brel chags su dgos pa'i tshad ldan gyi lung med

pas rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor gcig tu smin byed kyi dbang mang po mi rung ba'i don med ces par snang zhing phyag len kyang mdzad pa 'di yin la/ rang gi bsam tshod ni slob
ma smin byed la phyag len dog pa dang cho ga rgyas pa'i dbang du byas na dbang re la dbang gi mngon par rtogs pa brgyad car tshang ba re thub na shin tu legs te de dag smin
byed la dgos pa'i cho ga yongs su rdzogs pa gcig yin pas so/ /ci ste dbang re la cho ga brgyad po de yongs rdzogs re byas nas bskur ba dang / sta gon sogs sngon du byas
pa'i de dag gis go chod par byas/ slar dkyil 'khor sgrub pa man chad tsam re byas nas dbang bskur ba gnyis la phan yon gyi khyad par gang yang med na/ deng sang gi rdo
rje slob dpon phrin las shin tu che ba rnams kyis sku tshe'i stod la lha sta gon sogs lan gcig byas te sku tshe hril po'i sta gon go chod par byas nas slar dngos gzhi sgrub
mchod nas bzung ste cho ga dag byas te dbang bskur bya rigs par 'gyur zhes rdzong lugs pa dag gsung ba 'di'ang cung zad 'jug par snang ste phan yon nam dgos nus lhag po
med pa mnyam po la cig shos cho ga zor yang bas so/ /yang phyag len yangs phyogs dang cho ga zor yang pa'i dbang du byas na slob ma mang po la dbang bskur byed pa'i tshe
bsnyen pa kha gso dang rjes bzung sa chog sogs sngon du song pa'am ma song yang rung / nub dang po la bdag bskyed zin nas sa lha sogs sta gon gsum byas/ de nyid dang 'brel
bar slob ma nyer lnga la sta gon byas/ sang nyin rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor bris te sgrub cing

mchod pa byas te sngon du sta gon grub pa rnams la dbang bskur/ gzhan slob ma nyer lnga pa zhig sta gon byed pa sogs slob ma ji tsam yod pa ma rdzogs kyi bar du dngos gzhi
re dang / slob ma sta gon re spel nas byas pas mi rung ba ma yin te/ lha sta gon sogs kyi dgos pa de dag sta gon gcig pu des grub pas gzhan dgos pa lhag po med cing / dbang
re la lha sta gon re nges par dgos pa'i dmigs bsal yang med la/ des na spyir btang smin byed re la cho ga brgyad car tshang ba zhig byung na legs pa yin kyang / dmigs
bsal rjes bzung ma byas pa'i slob ma la slob ma sta gon dang dbang bskur chog pa ni/ slob ma yongs su bzung ba gang / /sta gon gnas tshe med na ni/ /zhes sogs kyis bstan
pa'i de dang 'dra bas so/ /slob ma sta gon la ni mi mtshungs te slob ma sta gon la med pa la dbang gi dngos gzhi mi bya bar dmigs bsal du gsungs pa'i phyir ro/ /ji ltar zhe
na/ sta gon gnas par byas pa la/ /gal te 'ong bar ma gyur na/ /bla ma blo ldan mkhas pa yis/ /der ni slob ma gzhan mi bzung / /zhes pa 'dis so/ /rgyu mtshan des na spyir
gsung rab 'chad pa dang / lag len cho ga'i rnam gzhag sogs la spyir btang re dang / dmigs bsal gyi rnam dbye re mchog tu gces te/ mkhyen rab dbang phyug sa skya paNDi
tas/ spyir btang ba la dmigs kyi bsal/ /bstan bcos kun la mkho ba yin/ /zhes gsungs pas so/ /de ltar gnyis kyi nang nas spyir btang de bya ba'i nus pa yod bzhin du dmigs
bsal de byar mi rung / spyir btang de bya mi nus pa la

dmigs bsal de byas pas phan yon chen po yod na dmigs bsal de nges par bya rigs te/ chos rjes/ dgag bya dang ni dgos pa gnyis/ /gtso bo gang che'i lugs su thongs/ /zhes gsungs
pas so/ des na slob ma brgya stong las brgal ba sogs rab tu mang po dag tshogs pa'i tshe ngor pa'i phyag len 'di ma mdzad par slob ma nyer lnga pa re la cho ga yongs su
rdzogs pa re re smin byed tshar re la sbyar nas byas na lo dang zla ba sogs yun ring po'i bar mi rdzogs shing / de ma rdzogs na slob ma rjes ma rnams la dbang bskur ba'i
sngon la tshe'i bar chad dang / gzhan yang rkyen 'ga' zhig gis phyogs gzhan du 'gro dgos pa sogs dbang thob pa'i gegs su 'gyur ba sogs yod pas na sta gon 'brel pa med pa'i
dgag bya las dgos pa de gtso che bas so snyam la/ gzhan yang ngor rdzong gi mkhas pa de dag gi gsung la rnam dbye phye rgyu 'ga' re snang zhing / khyad par thams cad
mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis bsgrub cing mchod pa dang / bdag nyid 'jug pa dang / slob ma la dbang bskur ba gsum la cho ga rigs mi mthun gzhan gyis bar ma chod pa
dgos gsungs pa la/ sgyi chu ba buddha shrI'i dbang chu chen mo'i lung drangs nas de dang 'gal gsungs kyang / rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg dang rab gnas sogs skabs der byed na kye
rdor la ma brten pa ni mi rung la/ kye rdor la brten pa ni kye rdor gyi dkyil 'khor sgrub mchod kyi cho ga dang rigs mthun yin zhing / khyad par rab gnas bzang po drug
pa ni kye rdor gyi rgyud kyi bshad tshul rang yin par gsungs

pas/ cho ga rigs mi mthun yin pa'i dogs pa tsam yang med pas thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyi gsung de dbang chu chen mo dang 'gal ba'i dogs pa cung zad kyang dgos
pa ma yin no//yang sgyi chu ba buddha shrI'i rdul tshon kho na smin byed du 'dod pa'i grub mtha' 'di dang zhes sogs gsungs kyang / ngor lugs la rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor
kho na smin byed kyi dkyil 'khor du mi bzhed pa'i phyir na skyon de mi 'jug la/ 'on kyang ngor lugs la gtso bor smin byed kyi dkyil 'khor rdul tshon la bzhed par snang
ba ni rje btsun gong ma'i dgongs pa ste/ de la'ang las dang po pa ma smin pa smin par byed pa la rdul tshon nyid legs pas rgyud sde thams cad las 'di nyid gtso bor gsungs
la/ de la dgongs nas bdag nyid chen pos kyang / deng sang gang zag rab 'bring kun/ /rdul tshon gyi ni dkyil 'khor du/ /dbang bskur bya bar gsung mod kyi/ /gzhan gyi smin
byed rgyud las bkag /ces gsungs pa yin no/ /gzhung 'di'i tshig zin tsam la dgongs rtse gtad nas 'brug pa padma dkar pos brtag gnyis 'chad pa rnams la dri ba mdzad pa
de'i lan gong dkar ba mkhyen brtse chos mdzad ces pas mdzad pa de la/ slar 'brug pa sprul sku nyid kyis yang lan zhig mdzad 'dug pa'i nang na/ mngon brjod bla ma'i dgongs
pa dang / grub thob gong ma'i phyag len la'ang yod 'dug pas mtha' gcig tu mi rung ba ma yin no zhes smras pa/ sdom gsum mdzad pas/ deng sang gang zag rab 'bring kun/ /rdul
tshon gyi ni dkyil 'khor du/ /dbang bskur bya bar gsungs mod kyi/ /gzhan gyi

smin byed rgyud las bkag /ces rdul tshon ma gtogs mtha' gcig tu mi rung bar gsungs pa dang 'gal lo zhes dang / smin byed rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du mtha' gcig tu dgos par
gsungs pa dang / de las gzhan rgyud las bkag gsungs pa'i rgyud de sa skya pa thams cad la logs nas ston par rigs so zhes phyogs snga ma'i bzhed pa ma longs pa'i gsung mang
du 'god par mdzad do/ /de la/ deng sang gang zag rab 'bring kun/ /zhes sogs kyis smin byed kyi dbang rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor kho nar bya dgos pa bstan pa min te/ kho
bo cag gi lugs la ras bris su'ang smin byed rung bar bzhed pas so/ /de ltar yang rje btsun rtse mo'i dbang chu chen mo las/ ras bris la brten pa'i lugs 'di ni bde mchog
a bhi dha na la brten/ slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pa dang dga' rab rdo rje la sogs pas gsungs/ deng sang rgya gar na'ang cho ga phal cher 'di la byed la/ bla ma gong ma
rnams kyang skabs su phyag len 'di la mdzad pas lugs 'di ha cang mi legs pa ma yin no zhes gsungs pa yin la/ des na gzhung de'i don ni deng sang so so skye bo'i gang zag
dbang po rab 'bring mtha' ma kun/ so so skye bo'i rdo rje slob dpon gyis smin par byed pa la gtso bor rdul tshon gyi ni dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur bya bar rgyud sde las gsung
mod kyi/ de las gzhan phag mo brda bzhi'i dbang dang / sprul pa'i dkyil 'khor du so skye smin pa rgyud las bkag ste tshul de lta bu rgyud sde las ci yang gsungs pa med
pa'i phyir zhes pa yin la/ gtso bor rdul tshon bya

bar rgyud sde las gsung te/ spyi rgyud las/ rnam dpyad dang po sa gzhi bzung / /zhes dang / brtag gnyis las/ gsar pa legs par bkal ba dang / /shin tu tshad ma mdzes pa yi/
/srad bu shes rab can gyis gdab/ /zhes dang / rdul tshon dam pa'i tshon dang ni/ /zhes sogs so so skye bo'i rdo rje slob dpon gyis slob ma smin par byed pa'i dbang du byas
nas sa brtag bslang sbyang gsum dang / thig gdab tshul sogs dang rin po che lnga'i phye ma la sogs pa rdul tshon gyi dbye ba gsungs pa yin gyis/ sprul pa'i dkyil 'khor
du dbang bskur ba na de dag gis dgos pa med pa'i phyir/ gzhan gyi smin byed ces sogs kyi gzhan gyi smin byed de phag mo brda bzhi sogs la ngos 'dzin pa ni/ chos rje nyid
kyi sdom gsum rang mchan na/ gzhan gyi smin byed rgyud las bkag /ces pa 'di'i mchan bur/ phag mo la sogs pa zhes gsungs yod pas de ltar du 'chad pa yin la/ khyed kyi 'ol
tshod kyis ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor sogs la 'dod pa ni rgyus med kyi rgyus gtam mo/ /der ma zad gzhung nyid kyi 'phros dang yang 'grigs te/ deng sang rdo rje phag mo yis/
byin rlabs dbang bskur yin zhes zer/ zhes phyogs snga bkod nas/ 'di 'dra rgyud sde las ma gsungs/ /bstan bcos rnams las bshad pa med/ /ces sogs lung rigs du ma'i sgo nas
'gog par mdzad pa'i log chos rnams dang / gzhan yang / kha cig gang zag dbang po rab/ /smin byed phag mo'i byin rlabs yin/ /zhes sogs smin byed ma yin pa smin byed du 'dod
pa dang / la la slob dpon gyis sprul

pa'i dkyil 'khor sprul nus shing / slob mas blta nus pa'i tshe dbang bya ba yin gyi/ de las gzhan du deng sang dbang bskur du mi rung zer ba sogs gang du bskur ba'i dkyil 'khor
la 'khrul pa yod pa rnams chabs gcig tu 'gog pa la/ deng sang zhes sogs 'byung bas so/ /des na khyed kyis de las gzhan rgyud las bkag gsungs pa'i rgyud de sa skya pa
thams cad logs nas ston par 'os so gsung ba dang / khyed nyid kyis rjes zhugs sangs rgyas rdo rje bas kyang / gzhan gyi smin byed gang yin dang / /de bkag pa yis lung khungs
dang / /'gegs pa'i rgyu mtshan tshad thub rnams/ /smra mkhas nyin skar bas kyang dkon/ /zhes zer zlos byed mod kyang de ni rang gis ma go bas gzhan gyis kyang go ba
med snyam pa'am/ gzhan dag go ba dag gis bshad kyang rang gi blo la gsal ba de dang ma mthun pas na 'dis kyang ma go 'dug snyam pa sogs log pa'i shes pas yid drangs pa'i
nyes par zad do/ /de lta min na kho bo cag ni/ gzhan gyi smin byed rgyud las bkag /ces 'byung ba'i gzhan gyi smin byed ni sngar bshad pa ltar yin la/ de nyid bkag pa'i lung
khungs ni rgyud sde thams cad yin te/ khyed cag dag 'dod pa'i phag mo brda bzhi'i dbang bya ba de dang / gzhan yang so so skye bo'i rdo rje slob dpon gyis sprul pa'i dkyil
'khor du dbang bskur ba sogs smin byed kyi dbang du rgyud sde gang du'ang bshad pa med pa'i phyir/ 'gegs pa'i rgyu mtshan ni/ rdo rje phag mo'i byin rlabs la/ /sdom
pa gsum ldan byar mi rung / /phyi nang rten 'brel

'grigs mi 'gyur/ /sku bzhi'i sa bon thebs mi nus/ /de phyir 'di ni byin rlabs tsam/ /yin gyis smin par byed pa min/ /zhes gsal bar gsungs pa 'dis phag mo'i byin rlabs smin
byed du 'gegs pa'i rgyu mtshan bstan pa yin la/ so so skye bo'i rdo rje slob dpon gyis so so skye bo'i slob ma sprul pa'i dkyil 'khor du smin par byed pa 'gog pa'i rgyu mtshan
ni de lta bu'i rdo rje slob dpon gyis sprul pa'i dkyil 'khor ston mi nus shing / slob mas blta yang mi nus pas na de 'dra'i rdo rje slob dpon gyis dkyil 'khor de lta
bur de lta bu'i slob ma smin pa mi rung zhes pa yin no/ /de ltar dpyis phyin par 'doms kyang khyed la ni tshad thub tu 'gro ba ches dka' ste gzu bor gnas pa'i thugs dang
mi ldan pas so/ /rgyu mtshan de dag gi phyir na sprul sku mchog padma dkar po rjes 'brangs dang bcas pa'i gsung de dag ni phyogs snga ma longs pa'i sun 'byin te phyogs
snga'i nam ma langs par dgag sgrub kyi nyi ma shar ba zhes pa der snang ngo / /de bas na padma dkar po khyed rang gi brtag gnyis 'chad pa po rnams la dri bar/ mchog dbang
gsum la dkyil 'khor bsgoms pas rung / /bum pa'i dbang la de lta mi rung ba'i/ /rgyud lung ci yod med na smin byed dbang / /rdul tshon nyid du 'gyur zhes smras kyang ci/
/zhes pa dang / gzhan yang rdul tshon rang mtha' cig tu mi dgos zhes thugs snyung snyung mo'i gsung yang yang phebs 'dug pa de'i khongs de na ras bris sogs dang rdul tshon
la smin byed du rung mi rung gi khyad par cung zad tsam yang med snyam pa zhig yod snang ba/ khyad par med na slob

dpon rtse mo'i lugs 'di ha cang mi legs pa ma yin no zhes rdul tshon las ras bris la brten pa 'di cung zad mi legs pa yin par bshad cing / de la khyed rtsi dogs med na'ang
/ slob dpon dza ya se nas/ rdul tshon bri bar ma nus na/ /dkyil 'khor dang mnyam ras la ni/ /nges par bcom ldan he ru ka /phyag rgya'i tshogs dang bcas pa bri/ /zhes pa 'dis
cho ga rgyas par nus na legs pas rdul tshon bya la/ mi nus na ras bris la brten pas kyang rung zhes bstan pa ma yin nam/ de min na 'o na/ rdul tshon bri bar ma nus na/
/zhes pa'i tshig gi nus pa ji ltar 'chad/ de gnyis la khyad par yod na kho bo cag gi lugs la'ang rgyud sde rnams las rdul tshon gtso bor gsungs pas thub na rdul tshon ka
legs shing / ras bris su'ang mi rung ba ma yin pas spyir btang dang dmigs bsal du 'chad pa dang mthun par 'byung bas tshul de yang yang smras pa la dgos pa ci yod legs
par soms la smros shig de dag ni cung zad 'phros pa'o/ /bzhi pa slob dpon gyi dbang la grangs nges yod med kyi rnam gzhag la rje mus srad pa chen pos chu rgyun bzhi par/
slob dpon grangs nges med pa dang / zhes pa'i rgyas bshad du/ kha cig rdo rje slob dpon gyis dbang gi skabs su slob ma der 'dug pa thams cad la dus gcig tu slob dpon gyi
