dbang byed pa shin tu mi rigs te/ slob dpon rin po che'i 'grel lugs kyi dbang chu las/ gsol btab kyi rjes su/ de nas slob dpon gyis tshogs pa la dbang bskur bar bya ba yin
te/ slob dpon snying rje chen po

yis/ /slob ma dam pa snying rje can/ /sngags dang rgyud rnams 'dzin pa po/ /gcig ni nan tan bskyed de bzung / /slob ma re re la dbang bzhi cig car ram rim can du bskur bar
bya ba yin pas gzhan bkye la/ ji skad du bshad pa'i dbang stegs kyi steng du slob ma'i gtso bor gyur pa sngar dngos grub kyi rdo rje brtul zhugs kyi skabs su bstan pa'i rdo
rje sems dpa'i phyag rgya chen pos bzhag la dbang bskur bar bya'o zhes dang / khyad par du man ngag lugs kyi dbang chu chen mo las/ slob dpon dbang gi gsol btab kyi rjes
su/ de nas slob ma gcig dbang stegs kyi steng du bzhag la rdo rje 'chang chen po'i rnam par bsam zhes pa dang / su pra tiShThas me tog gtor ba'i rjes su/ de ltar slob
ma re re nas rdzogs pa dang / slob ma rnams la dus gcig tu de kho na nyid bstan par bya ste zhes gsungs pa rnams ma mthong ngam ci/ gang bkag pa de nan gyis sgrub pa la brtson
par byed par zad do zhes gsungs nas/ ngor pa dag nyer lnga po thams cad la rdo rje slob dpon gyis dbang dus gcig tu bskur ba'i phyag len mdzad pa la rgol bar mdzad
do/ /rgol ba'i gsung bkod pa 'di la rnam thar sgo brgyad pa sogs su snying po blangs nas bkod pas gong gi de dang tshig rigs mi mthun pa re 'byung yang / 'dir ni chu rgyun
bzhi pa rang las ji skad 'byung ba bzhin bkod pa yin la/ de ltar mus srad pa chen pos brgal zhing brtags pa de'i lan du/ paN chen rin po che'i rnam thar sgo brgyad par
tshogs pa la rdo rje slob dpon gyis dbang bskur ba nyes can yin na kun gyis sel dgos par bstan pa

dang / dgos pa'i dbang gis de ltar mdzad pas dgag bya mang po khegs par bstan pa dang / slob ma slob dpon gyis skal ba can la phyag len de nges par byed dgos par bshad pa dang
gsum du mdzad nas/ dang po la slob ma smin byed kyi rig pa'i dbang lnga bskur ma thag slob dpon gyis dbang byed pa 'di dbang chu chen mo dang 'gal ba ma yin mod/ khyed
kyis 'gal bar go nas de'i dgongs pa bzhin byed na/ rjes 'dzin gyi tshe lus longs spyod gang yod mi 'bul na rjes 'dzin mi byed/ tshe 'di don du gnyer na slob ma sta gon
mi byed/ sems ma bskyed pa dang ye shes ma phebs pa dkyil 'khor du mi 'jug pa sogs khungs thub kyi bshad tshod thams cad khyed kyis phyag len du khel ba yod dam/ yod na mngon
sum dang 'gal/ med na ma bshad pa thams cad nan gyis byed dam zhes gsungs/ gnyis pa la/ slob dpon gyi dbang bskur tshul 'di cis kyang byed dgos pa grub mtha' la ma byas
pas/ dam bca' med pa la lung 'gal brjod pa mkhas pa'i lugs min/ spyir btang la slob dpon gyi dbang don du mi gnyer ba dag bkye dgos par bshad kyang / nged kyi bla ma'i
dbang gral du de 'dra ma byung / don du gnyer bzhin phud na dgag bya cir 'gyur/ dgos pa ni ma mtha' mtshan brjod kyi lung tsam zhig len pa la'ang slob dpon gyi dbang mi
dgos sam/ slob ma nyer lnga po thams cad dbang de don du gnyer mnyam la 'ga' zhig smad de phud na/ slob mas slob dpon la khong khro sogs kyis dgag bya cir 'gyur/ slob dpon
'phrin las chung ngu dag

gis re re nas dbang stegs la 'god par nus kyang / 'phrin las rlabs po che dag la dgos pa gzhan du ma 'byung ngo gsungs/ gsum pa la/ bod 'dir thun mong gi dbang drug po tsam
thob pa rnams kyis bla med kyi rgyud mtha' dag nyan rung pas/ slob dpon gyi dbang gi snod du'ang rung / 'o na bla med kyi rgyud nyan pa la slob dpon gyi dbang mi dgos sam
zhe na/ bla med rigs drug gi rgyud dngos su nyan pa dang lta ba la lha dang dkyil 'khor sogs kyi de kho na nyid shes dgos/ des na 'phags yul lta bu na rgyud sde bzhi'i
gdul bya so sor nges pa dang / bla med kyi gdul bya la'ang dbang gong ma don du gnyer mi gnyer so sor nges pa yod pas/ de dag la dkyil 'khor la 'jug pa tsam dang / slob ma'i
dbang tsam dang / bum dbang tsam bskur nas 'gyes mi 'gyes kyi dbye ba yod kyi/ rdo rje'i rigs can gcig tu gyur pa la de ltar med do/ /de'i tshe re re nas byas pa'i dgos
pa dbang stegs kyi dkyil 'khor gcig las med pas de'i don dang / de kho na nyid 'chad pa'i tshe dbang stegs la 'jog mi dgos pas thams cad bkug pa yin gyi/ dgos pa gzhan
med la/ 'o na rdo rje theg pa'i snod rung thams cad de'i slob dpon gyi 'os su nges sam zhe na/ slob dpon gyi dbang la dgos pa gnyis te/ bskyed rim gyi dbang du byas pa'i
rgyud mtha' dag la thos bsam sgom gsum byed pa'i don dang / de'i 'og tu chos 'chad pa dang / bgegs gzhom pa dang / dbang gong ma la 'jug pa'i don no/ /dang po de slob dpon
gyi dbang dngos tsam gyis 'grub/ gnyis pa de dag

la chos 'chad pa'i rjes gnang la sogs pa dgos so/ de'i phyir na slob ma dang slob dpon gyi dbang mtshan mo gcig la bskur ba'i phyag len byas pas 'ga' zhig gi bsam pa la slob
gnyer dang bsnyen sgrub byed ma dgos par rdo rje slob dpon du song byung ngo snyam pa'i dwogs pa de'ang khegs so/ /rdzogs rim gyi chos 'chad pa'i slob dpon du 'gro ba la
ni dbang gong ma thob dgos shing / de'ang dbang rnon la dbang bzhi cig car du bskur bas chog kyang / dbang chu las ni rtul 'bring gi dbang du mdzad do zhes gsungs/ yang
tshar chen gyis rdo rje'i 'khrul 'khor gyi zegs ma las/ smra ba bzhi pa slob dpon gyi dbang la grangs nges med pa'i sgrub byed dus gcig la nyer lnga la bskur ba'i phyir
zer bar snang ba/ de ltar na slob dpon gyi dbang la grangs nges yod par thal/ dus gcig la nyer lnga las lhag pa la mi bskur ba'i phyir/ khyab pa tshad grub/ rtags gsal dngos/
'khor gsum/ slob dpon gyi dbang la dbang stegs kyi steng du gcig bsgrengs su bzhag nas bskur dgos snyam na/ ngor pa yang dbang stegs gcig gi steng du slob ma gnyis gsum
la sogs pa dus gcig tu 'jog par mi bzhed cing / dkyus ma la lag len bde ba'i dbang du byas nas so sor ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang stegs bskyed pa la bzhag nas slob dpon
gyi dbang bskur bar mdzad la rgyas par na spyi rgyud las/ bla mas slob ma gcig pu ni/ /dkyil 'khor dag tu dbang bskur bya/ /mkhas pas cig car slob ma gnyis/ /dbang bskur
bar ni yongs mi bya/ /gnyis sam

gsum mam bzhi yang rung / /bla mas dbang bskur bya ba ni/ /yo byad gsar pa gzhan rnams kyi/ /thams cad so so so sor bya/ /zhes dang / dbang bskur don du dkyil 'khor ni/ /bye
ma dkar pos bri bar bya/ /dkyil 'khor dag dang rjes mthun par/ /stegs bu gru bzhi byas nas su/ /de yi dbus su tshon sna lngas/ /padma yongs su rdzogs pa bri/ /zhes sogs
gsungs pa'i don/ rje btsun gong ma'i yi ge las 'byung ba'i phyag len dbang stegs kyi dkyil 'khor mtshan nyid tshang ba'i steng du ji skad bshad pa'i yo byad yongs su rdzogs
pa'i chig bsgrengs su rdo rje slob dpon gyi dbang bskur ba'i phyag len shin tu rgyas pa'ang byed pas/ khyed kyi padma 'dab brgyad kyi ri mo tsam gyi steng du slob dpon
gyi dbang bskur ba la de tsam gyi nga rgyal gyis nyam thag pas ngal ba lhur len par zad do zhes gsungs la/ yang thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis tshangs pa'i
rig sngags su/ rnam dbye spyir bstan pa dang / nges gzung med kyang nyes med du bstan pa/rgol ba po nyid nyes pa chen pos non pa dang don tshan gsum du mdzad nas/ dang
po la tshig rigs cung zad ma gtogs gong du bkod pa'i paN chen gyi lan 'debs don tshan dang po ji lta ba bzhin gsungs la/ gnyis pa la spyir dbang bskur tshul la rim gyis
pa dang cig car ba gnyis las/ snga ma ni gang zag tha ma gtso bor bzung pa dang / lag len spros pa che ba'i skabs yin pas/ de'i tshe dbang stegs dngos su bris nas der slob
ma re re nas bskur ba gtso bor gsungs/ phyi ma la dbang stegs yod med kyi bye brag

gis slob dpon gyi dbang bskur tshul gnyis ka mdzad cing / phyag len de gnyis ka kho bo cag la'ang yod mod/ phyi ma gtso bor mdzad pa ni slob dpon la slob mas khro ba dang /

der ni dngos bstan dbang rim can pa'i dbang du mdzad pa'i phyir ro gsungs/ don tshan gsum pa la rgol ba'i lag len de lung dang mi mthun pa dang / rigs pa dang 'gal tshul
gnyis su mdzad nas/ dang po la/ dbang chu gnyis kyi dngos bstan ltar byed na bka' srol 'di la dbang gong ma gsum yang slob ma re re nas bya dgos te/ slob dpon rin po che'i
'grel pa lugs kyi dkyil chog las/ slob ma re re la dbang bzhi cig car ram rim can du bskur bar bya ba yin pas zhes dang / man ngag lugs kyi dbang chu las/ de la rab mtshan
gcig la dbang bzhi po 'di rdzogs par bskur na dbang gi mtha' rten yang tha dad du byed do/ /de'ang bum dbang gi mtha' rten rjes gnang / gsang dbang gi lung bstan/ shes
rab ye shes kyi dbugs dbyung / dbang bzhi pa'i mtha' rten gzengs bstod do/ /de dag kyang slob ma re re nas rdzogs par bskur ba'i lugs yin no zhes bshad pa'i phyir ro/

mong gi mngon

rtogs mtha' dag nyams su blang rung bar gsungs pas/ lugs 'di la slob dpon gyi dbang ni dbang bzhi char la ngos 'dzin pa yin cing / bde mchog sogs la ni mi mtshungs te/ de dag
las ni yo ga dang sgo bstun nas dam tshig gsum sbyin pa la slob dpon gyi dbang du bshad pas so/ /de la dgongs nas sa chen gyis bde mchog dkyil chog las brtul zhugs kyi

rdzas gnyis ka la dag pa bzhi tshang dgos na rdor sems nyid mi dmigs par byas nas/ slar yang de nyid kyi

bskyed chog rgyas par byed dam/ brtul zhugs kyi tshe sbyang gzhi stong par sbyong ngo zhe na/ de'i sbyang gzhi dang slob ma'i gzhi mthun gang la byed/ khyad par slob dpon gyi
tshe bdag dang dbang rdzas kyi bdag de dbang stegs la 'jog kha de'am zhag zin pa de yin/ de gnyis ji ltar yang thog mar mi dmigs par ma btang ba'i yongs dag bzhi mi srid/
btang na rdor sems med par byed dgos/ byin gyis brlabs tshul rgyu dus dang 'dra na dbang rdzas la dag pa bzhi zin nas slob ma la dbang bskur mi dgos sam/ dbang rdzas
dag pa bzhis sgrub pa'i tshe rdo rje mi dmigs par byas nas lhar bskyed pa zhu ba las rdo rjer gyur pa zhig slob ma la ster mi dgos sam/ yin na rdo rje'i dbang bskur tshul
du song gi slob dpon gyis der ma song / dril bu la'ang de dang 'dra zhing / slob dpon gyi skabs su phyag rgya'ang dbang rdzas kyi gtso bor mi 'dod dam zhes gsungs/ /don
tshan gnyis pa la/ rje btsun gyis gzhan rnams rgyu dus dang 'dra'o zhes pas rgyu lam gnyis ka'i brtul zhugs dang slob dpon gyi dbang la yongs dag bzhi tshang mi dgos par
grub ste/ slob dpon rin po che'i dbang chu gnyis ka las stong pa'i ngang las hU~M las rdo rjer bskyed ces pa yod kyi/ lhar bskyed pa mi snang bas de med par yongs dag bzhi
ji ltar tshang / gal te rdo rje'i de kho na nyid rdzogs par bskyed nas zhes pas dag pa bzhi 'thon snyam na/ yongs dag bzhi la rdo rje'i de kho na nyid du su yang mi bzhed/
nges don gyi rdo rje ni sangs rgyas thams cad tshang ba'i rdo rje sems dpar/ 'di de sangs

rgyas thams cad de/ /zhes sogs kyis ngo sprod la/ /'di ni mdo tsam yin la/ rdor dril gnyis ka'i de nyid gsal po ni slob dpon gyi tshe ston pa de'o/ 'o na bdun ka'i skabs su
dbang rdzas dag pa bzhis byin gyis brlabs par bshad pas/ dbang phyi ma gnyis kyi tshe dbang rdzas kyi dag pa bzhi gang zhe na lam dus su ni rdor dril gnyis po de ltar byin
gyis brlabs ma thag pa de lha'i bdag nyid la so so'i de nyid tshang bar ngo sprad nas byin pa'i mos pa las 'os med/ rgyu dus su mtshan gcig la bdun ka bskur ba'i tshe
gong ma dang 'dra la/ brtul zhugs dang slob dpon gyi bar du lo zlas chod pa'i tshe slob ma dbang stegs la bzhag rjes rig dbang slob dpon dbang gi yan lag tu bskur nas dam
tshig gsum ster dgos pas dbang rdzas la yongs dag bzhi grub la/ rje btsun gyis slob dpon gyi dbang rdzas la dag pa bzhi mi dgos sam snyam pa'i dogs pa dang / de sel byed
gsungs pa'ang de yin la/ brtul zhugs kyi tshe dogs pa dang de sel byed gsungs pa ni/ rdo rje'i dbang ni gong du zin/ 'dir de ster ba ni gzhan zhig go snyam pa de sel byed
du gong gi rdo rje de slob ma'i lag na yod pa slob dpon gyis blangs te byin gyis brlabs nas slob ma'i sems kyi dri ma 'khrud par byed pa'i phyir zhes so/ /khyed kyis ni
rje btsun gyi lam dus kyi yi ge des rtse mo'i dbang chu gnyis bkag ces par song zhes gsungs la/ 'di dag ni paN chen gyis gsung mang po rnams ha cang bsdus pa rang ma yin
par snying po bkod pa yin pas/ rnam thar sgo brgyad pa'i tshig rigs dang ma mthun no snyam pa bya

mi rigs so/ yang tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i rdo rje'i 'khrul 'khor gyi zegs ma las/ 'o na brtul zhugs dang slob dpon gyi dbang rdzas la yan lag bzhi rdzogs kyi bskyed chog
dgos par thal/ rje btsun gyis dgos par gsungs pa'i phyir/ 'dod na mi dgos par thal/ rje btsun gyis mi dgos par gsungs pa'i phyir te/ 'di skabs kyi lam dus kyi dbang dang
rgyu dus kyi dbang lha dam tshig pa bskyed pa'i rgyas bsdus tsam ma gtogs gzhan khyad par med par gsal bar gsungs pa'i phyir dang / rgyud dus kyi dbang la de ltar mi
dgos pa rje btsun rtse mo'i dbang chu dang 'phags pa rin po che'i bdag 'jug gnyis las gsal bar bshad cing / der ma zad gong ma'i yi ge chos rje bla ma/ theg chen chos rje
sogs sus kyang khyed 'dod pa ltar gyi bskyed chog ye ma gsungs so/ /des na rje btsun gyis bdag dang dbang rdzas la yan lag bzhi rdzogs kyi bskyed chog dgos par gsungs pa
gtso che ba la dgongs pa yin gyis re re nas khyab mtha' 'dzin pa ma yin no/ de yin na ming dbang la dbang rdzas nges par dgos pa dang / deng sang lag len la rdo rje dril
bu spyi bor bzung nas ming dbang bskur dus kyang dbang rdzas de la bskyed chog sus kyang mi byed pa sogs la thugs gzhib mdzad pa zhu zhes gsungs la/ mkhas pa'i dbang po
dkon mchog lhun grub kyis tshangs pa'i rig sngags su dngos bstan gyi rgol tshul ma shes pas rje btsun la skur pa btab par bstan pa dang / zhe 'dod kyi lan btab ste rgol ba
po nyes pa can du bstan pa dang gnyis

su mdzad nas gsungs pa'i don gyi snying po ci longs bgyis nas bkod na/ de'ang don tshan dang po la dbang bdun char gyi dbang rdzas la yongs dag bzhi nges par dgos par rje btsun
bzhed na/ mi bskyod pa la yongs dag mdzad nas/ rin 'byung cod pan man chad la mi bskyod pa'i nga rgyal gyis dbang bskur chog pa/ gur gyi/ rdo rje sems dpas dbang bskur
bya/ /zhes pa'i don du/ rje btsun nyid kyis bshad pa dang nang 'gal zhing / rtse mo'i dbang chu gnyis char las/ rig pa'i dbang 'di rnams la slob dpon bdag nyid mi bskyod
pa'i rnal 'byor kho nas kyang rung ngo zhes pa 'di rje btsun gyi gsung des bkag par khas len dgos pas/ rje btsun nyid nang 'gal gsung ba dang / rtse mo 'gegs pa por sgrub
pas rje btsun la skur ba btab par song gsungs la/ don tshan gnyis pa la'ang yongs dag bzhi ngos bzung ste rang lugs nyes med du bsgrub pa dang / rgol ba'i rdor dril gyi
de nyid nor bar bstan pa gnyis su mdzad nas/ dang po la/ spyir 'khor gsum yongs dag bzhis byin gyis brlabs zhes gsungs pa'i 'khor gsum ni slob dpon slob ma dbang rdzas
gsum yin la/ yongs dag bzhi ni bsnyen pa/ nyer sgrub/ sgrub pa/ sgrub chen dang bzhi yin cing / de la rgyas bsdus bzhi las/ rgyas pa dkyil 'khor yongs rdzogs kho na la sbyor
bar gsungs pa dang / 'bring po ni ji skad bshad pa bzhin yin la/ bsdus pa'i dang po ni/ skye mched byin gyis mi rlobs par sku gsung thugs byin gyis brlabs pa dang /
dbang mi bskur bar dbu rgyan rang chas can du sgrub pa'i

yan lag bzhi dang / bsdus pa phyi ma ni dam tshig sems dpa' dbu rgyan rang chas can du skad cig las bskyed pa rnams yin par ljon shing las bshad do/ /de ltar na 'grel pa lugs
kyi brtul zhugs dang slob dpon gyi dbang rdzas la drangs ma thag pa'i bskyed chog 'bring po de sbyar ba yin zhing / man ngag lugs kyi de gnyis la bsdus pa phyi ma de sbyar
ba yin te/ dang po la rdor dril gyi lha thams cad la yan lag bzhi rdzogs dngos su mdzad pa'i phyir dang / phyi ma la rdo rje la lha nyi shu rtsa brgyad dang / dril bu
lha nyi shu rtsa gsum skad cig gis bskyed pa'i phyag len de gnyis so sor mdzad pa'i phyir ro/ 'o na bskyed chog phyi ma de la yan lag bar pa gnyis dngos su med pas bzhi
rdzogs su mi rung ngam snyam na/ de ni rje btsun sku mched la klan kar 'gyur la/ des na rje btsun gyi gsung de dang kho bo cag gi phyag len la mi mthun pa cung zad kyang
med cing / man ngag lugs la bskyed tshul de tsam gyis chog pa ni/ dbang chu las brtul zhugs kyi tshe rdo rje mi dmigs te stong pa'i ngang las hU~M yongs su gyur pa las rdo
rjer bskyed la/ de la de bzhin gshegs pa lnga dang / yum lnga dang / sems dpa' brgyad dang / lha mo la sogs pa rdo rje'i de kho na ltar yongs su rdzogs par mos pa bskyed
la zhes dang / de la dam tshig gsum byin pa ni rdo rje lag tu blangs la/ hU~M las rdor dril gnyis de kho na nyid rdzogs par dran pas lha'i rnal 'byor mos pa bskyed la
zhes dang / dril bu blangs la a'i yi ge las dril bu'i de kho na nyid rdzogs par dran pas dril bur bskyed la zhes

'byung gi bzhi rdzogs dngos su bya dgos pa ma gsungs pas bstan pa yin la/ de kho na nyid rdzogs par dran pas zhes pa des bzhi rdzogs dngos su bya dgos par bstan snyam na/ rdor
dril gyi yongs dag bzhi rdor dril gyi de kho na nyid la 'chad pa'i dpyod ldan su zhig 'byung legs par soms shig gsungs par mdzad la/ gnyis pa la khyed kyis brtul zhugs
dang slob dpon gyi dbang rdzas la yongs dag bzhi byed pa de khyed rang gi bla ma kun rgyal ba'i kye rdor dkyil chog ltar byed na dkyil chog der ni rdor dril gnyis rdor
sems yab yum du bskyed nas/ de zhu ba las rdo rje de ster bar bshad la/ de ni dbang chu las rdo rje la rigs lnga sogs bskyed par bshad pa dang 'gal bas bka' srol gnyis po
gang la'ang mi rung / gal te 'grel lugs kyi dbang chu las sa chog la kha 'phangs pa bzhin no snyam na/ slob dpon rin po che'i 'grel lugs kyi dbang chu las rdor dril la lha
rigs lnga sogs bskyed pa'i sa chog la kha 'phangs mdzad/ khyod kyis sa chog gi skabs su kha 'phangs kyi lha de rnams ma bskyed par rdo rje 'od dpag med dang / dril bu
don yod grub par bskyed pas nor ba yin la/ yang rje btsun gyis mdzad pa'i de kho na nyid kyi yi ge de la khungs su 'dod na/ de ni rtse mo'i sambu Ta'i TIka chen dang mi mthun
pas rngog lugs pa zhig gi byas kyi/ rje btsun gyis mdzad pa ma yin la/ ji ltar mi mthun snyam na/ yi ge der rtse dgu pa ni dam tshig rdo rje/ rtsa lnga pa ye shes kyi
rdo rje zhes 'byung ba dang / TIka chen las rdo rje mkha' 'gror rtse dgu pa ye shes kyi rdo rje rtse lnga pa dam tshig gi rdo rje zhes

'byung bas zhes sogs gsungs pas dngos su 'gal zhing / rtse dgu pa'i lha 'god tshul yang mi mthun te/ yi ge der steng gi rwa dgu'i phyogs kyi bzhi rigs bzhi/ mtshams kyi bzhi
yum bzhi/ dbus nam mkha' kun bzang / 'og gi dgu ye shes lnga/ tshad med bzhi zhes 'byung / TIka chen las/ steng gi rwa brgyad byang chub sems dpa' brgyad de padma'i phyag
dang / byams pa dang zhes sogs dang / 'og gi rwa brgyad ni lha mo brgyad de rdo rje lcags kyu zhags pa ma zhes sogs dang / dbus kyi rwa ni rdo rje rnam par snang mdzad
do zhes bshad pas so/ /de bzhin du mi nyag pradznyA dzA la'i sampu Ta'i rnam bshad du yang TIka chen dang mthun pa kho na 'byung gi yi ge de dang mthun pa mi 'byung la/
bla ma 'ga' zhig rje btsun gyis mdzad nges pa'i yi ge zhig kyang yod nges pas btsal dgos gsungs kyang / bla ma spyil sgom gyi lam 'bras kyi yig cha las/ rje pa'i zhal nas
rdo rje dang / dril bu dang / phreng ba'i de nyid gcig byed par bsam pa la ma grub ces 'byung bas brtsal yang ngal ba tsam du zad do zhes gsungs so/ /de'i don bsdus don
brgyad pa las kyang / brtul zhugs slob dpon dbang bskur gyi/ /dbang rdzas yongs dag bsdus pa yi/ /nam yang bskyed du mi rung ba'i/ /gong ma'i lung khungs ci zhig yod/ /khyed
dag yongs dag ci ltar byed/ /rje btsun gong mas ma bshad kyang / /cho ga gsum bskyed sogs sbyor na/ /mngon byang lnga las bskyed rung zhes/ /bshad na khyed cag ci zhig
smra/ /khyed kyi tshad mar khas blangs pa'i/ /rdo rje dril

bu'i de nyid las/ /bshad pa'i lha yi bskyed tshul dang / /dbang chu nas bshad lha de dag /shar nub ri bzhin ring du gyur/ /de gnyis 'gal spong ji ltar byed/ /khyed kyi bla
mas mdzad pa yi/ /dkyil chog dpag bsam ljon shing las/ /bshad pa'i rdor dril bskyed chog dang / /rje btsun rtse mo'i dbang chu gnyis/ /snang mun bzhin du 'gal bar gyur/ /bka'
srol gnyis la de mi rung / /gal te de ltar bya rung bar/ /bshad pa'i gong ma'i lung yod na/ kho bo khyed kyi rjes su 'brangs/ /de phyir ston pa'i dus la babs/ /zhes
gsungs so/ /de rnams kyi yang lan du mkhan chen bzang bkras pa'i snyan brgyud 'khrul sel las/ slob dpon slob ma dbang rdzas gsum/ /rigs lngar bskyed pa 'dra ba'i mu/ /mi
bskyod me tog phog pa'i lha/ /rigs lngar bskyed pa mi 'dra'i mu/ /slob ma de bzhin dang mtha' gnyis/ /rigs lnga so sor bskyed pa dang / /dang po mi bskyod phyi ma gnyis/
/rigs lngar bskyed pa gnyis min mur/ /mkhas pas bshad ltar thun mong dang / /lam dus bskyed chog thun mong min/ /yang na rgyu lam khyad par yin/ /de 'dra 'gal 'dod blo gros
rtsing / /de phyir lam dus khyab mtha' 'dzin/ /zhes pa dang / rnam snang dbang rdzas med pa dang / /phyi ma gnyis la'ang gzhi med pas/ /mi 'gal brdzun zog ma yin nam/
/rang nyes slob dpon ma bkod cig /rdor dril bskyed chog de 'dra ba/ /man ngag med pa'i 'ol tshod tsam/ /lam dus dbang gi yig chung dang / /khyed kyi lam dus mi 'gal na/ /dngos
bstan min par yongs su grags/

/shugs bstan sgrub byed smra na yang / /rang bzo min pa khyed la med/ /dpyad na 'khrul par shes bzhin du/ /da dung phal cher re dogs byed/ /ces gsungs la/ yang sgyi chu ba
buddha shrI'i nor bu'i phreng bar/ lam dus dbang gi yi ge de/ /dgos med gcig la gsungs bar thal/ /bum pa'i dbang bskur bdun pa la/ /'khor gsum yongs dag med pa'i phyir/ /rje
btsun nang 'gal gsungs pa dang / /sku mched gnyis kyang 'gal bar thal/ /rdo rje gur gyi gzhung don des/ /'khor gsum yongs dag bkag pa'i phyir/ /'khor gsum yongs dag ces
bya ba/ /chu dbang kho na yin par thal/ /dbang bskur phyi ma gsum po la/ /'khor gsum yongs dag med pa'i phyir/ /rdo rje gur gyi gzhung don dang / /slob dpon rtse mo'i
dbang chu de/ /khyed kyi dgag bya yin par thal/ /dbang bskur bdun gyi slob dpon de/ /rigs bdun so sor 'pho ba'i phyir/ /dbang bskur bdun la khyed nyid kyang / /'khor gsum
yongs dag med par thal/ /lam dus dbang gi yi ge dang / /khyed kyi phyag len mthun pa'i phyir/ /lam dus dbang gi ye ge dang / /khyed kyi phyag len 'gal bar thal/ /dbang bskur
phyi ma gsum pa la/ /dbang rdzas yongs dag med pa'i phyir/ /man ngag lugs kyi brtul zhugs dang / /slob dpon gnyis kyi dbang rdzas la/ /bsdus pa phyi ma sbyar zhes pa/
/gyi na tsam gyi tshig tu thal/ /de la dbang rdzas med pa'i phyir/ /zhes gsungs la/ de ltar ngor rdzong gnyis rdo rje brtul zhugs kyi dbang dang / slob dpon gyi dbang

gnyis kyi dbang rdzas rdo rje dang dril bu gnyis la yongs dag bzhi'i bskyed chog dgos mi dgos kyi bshad tshul dang phyag len cung zad ma mthun par snang yang / don gyi snying
po lugs gnyis ka rje btsun gong ma'i dgongs pa dang 'gal med yin par sems te/ rje btsun gong ma'i yongs dag bzhi la rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum don gyis bshad pa'i 'bring
po'i phyogs de gtso bor rdzong lugs pa dag gis lam dus kyi dbang gi tshe'ang chu dbang sogs bdun char la sbyar nas phyag len du mdzad de/ /tshul de ni gong ma'i lung de dag
gis grub la/ ngor lugs pa rnams kyis bskyed chog rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum gyi 'bring po de 'grel pa lugs kyi brtul zhugs dang slob dpon gyi dbang rdzas la sbyar/ bsdus
pa la gnyis su phye nas phyi ma man ngag lugs kyi dbang de gnyis kyi dbang rdzas la sbyar ba yin zhing / man ngag lugs la bskyed chog de tsam gyis chog pa yang dbang chu'i
lung / brtul zhugs kyi tshe rdo rje mi dmigs te stong pa'i ngang las hU~M yongs su gyur pa las rdo rjer bskyed la zhes sogs kyis bstan par ngor lugs pa dag 'chad cing don
la'ang gnas pas so//des na phyag len rgyas bsdus tsam ma gtogs don gyi gnad la 'khrul pa'i cha lugs gnyis char du med par sems so// //drug pa lus dkyil gyi tshe 'byung
khungs kyi tshig yod med kyi rnam gzhag la/ mus srad pa chen po'i chu rgyun bzhi par tshig rigs rgyas pa tsam zhig 'byung yang / snying po blangs nas bkod pa paN chen gyi
rnam thar sgo brgyad par 'byung ba ltar bshad na/ lus dkyil 'byung khungs med pa

dang / /zhes pa'i rgyas bshad dam 'grel pa'i tshul du/ kha cig lus dkyil gyi pho brang lnga'i aM la sogs pa'i yi ge rnams lha rin 'byung la sogs pa'i sa bon du bzhag nas skyed
par byed pa mi 'thad de/ de ltar na bcos ma'i dkyil 'khor du thal ba'i phyir dang / haM dang hU~M lta bu sa bon mgo thur bstan du mi rung ba'i phyir zhes bkag nas/ ngag
'don gyi tshe aM rin chen 'byung ldan zhes sogs sbyar nas 'byung khungs kyi tshig mtha' dag med par byed do/ /'di ni mi 'thad de/ rje btsun rtse mo'i lus dkyil lung dang
sbyar bar le'u gnyis pa'i skabs su/ bhrUM la sogs pa ni pho brang lnga'i lha rnams kyi sa bon te zhes gsal bar gsungs pa dang / gzhung bshad mtha' dag gi grangs bgrangs
nas/ de thams cad las aM las dang / ha~M las zhes sogs 'byung khungs kyi tshig bshad pa dang / khyad par dpe mdzod ma dang / sga theng ma gnyis su rtsa nang gi khams las
yab dang / phyi shun gyi rtsa las yum bskyed par bshad pa dang / gnyags ma'i gsal byed lus dkyil gyi ye ger yang / /de las lte bar aM las bcom ldan 'das yon tan rnam par
dag pa rin chen 'byung ldan zhes lan cig ma yin pa yang yang gsungs pa la de ltar du smras nus pa ya mtshan no zhes rgol bar mdzad do/ /de'i lan du paN chen rin po ches
rnam thar sgo brgyad par nges don gyi go ba ma chags na phyogs gnyis ka nges med du bstan/ nges don gyi go ba zur tsam bstan pa dang don tshan gnyis su mdzad nas/ dang po
la/ las nyon gyi rnam smin du gyur pa'i rtsa khams nyid sangs

rgyas yab yum du 'chad pa'am/ rtsa khams nyid lha zhal phyag gi rnam pa can rdzas gzhan mang po bsgrub pa'i gzhir 'dod kyang rung ste/ phyogs gnyis ka'i ngos ma zin pa'i phyir
'dam kha med do/ /ji ltar zhe na las nyon gyi rnam par smin pa ni rang bzhin gyi sangs rgyas dang / glo bur rnam dag gi sangs rgyas gnyis su sus kyang sgrub mi nus pa
dang / bskyed rdzogs kyi lha gang yin kyang bsgrub gzhi zhig las bsgrub dgos na de'i mthar thug gi rtsa ba gzhi dus kyi ye shes nyid la thug dgos pa'i phyir zhes gsungs/
don tshan gnyis pa la gzhir gnas kyi dkyil 'khor bzhi la sku bzhi rang bzhin lhun grub dang / yon tan gnas 'gyur du 'byung ba gnyis gnyis su dbye ba ni/ rang bzhin rgyu
la bsam na lhun grub ste/ /mtha' yas yon tan tshogs rnams gnas 'gyur yin/ /zhes bstan pas na lus dbyibs kyi rang bzhin dang / de'i chos nyid sprul sku rang bzhin lhun grub
dang / de bzhin du gzhan gsum la'ang sbyar bas chos can dkyil 'khor bzhi po grub tsam nas de'i chos nyid sku bzhi po ngo bo dbyer med yin te/ bum pa rdzas tha dad par snang
ba bzhin dang / de'i go sa na yod pa'i nam mkha' dbyer med pa bzhin dang / ji srid bum pa lta bu'i sgrib thogs ma bsal ba de srid du/ de'i nam mkha' gzugs can gzhan
gyi go skabs mi 'byed pa de bzhin du/ ji srid shes rab kyi dbang po'i rnam smin gyi lus rtsa dang / de'i chos nyid sprul sku rang bzhin lhun grub go sa tha mi dad du gnas
pa la/ de ltar du bla mas brda sprad nas shes pa'i tshe lus dkyil ngo 'phrod pa zhes bya la/ de'i 'og tu shes rab

kyi dbang pos rnam smin gyi lus la sogs pa'i sgrib thogs bsal nas sprul sku rang bzhin lhun grub nyi ma lta bur yon tan gyi tshogs mngon du gyur pa la gnas gyur pa zhes bya'o/
de'i phyir rang bzhin rnam dag la bsams na 'byung khungs kyi tshig mi dgos la/ glo bur rnam dag la bsams na 'byung khungs kyi tshig yod par byed do/ de'ang ngag tu brjod
na rang bzhin rnam dag gi rin 'byung zhal phyag gi rnam pa can ma yin pa ni rtsa yig aM gi rnam par gnas so/ /rin 'byung zhal phyag gi rnam pa can ni aM yig las byung
ngo zhes khas len par bya zhing / /de bzhin du nga rgyal dang tshor ba'i phung po rnam par dag ces pa de la'ang rang bzhin rnam dag dang glo bur rnam dag gnyis las/ las
dang po pa'i lus dkyil gsal 'debs ba'i tshe ni snga ma dbang btsan la/ dbang gi rtogs pa brjod pa'i tshe ni phyi ma dbang btsan no gsungs so/ /yang tshar chen gyi rdo rje'i
'khrul 'khor gyi zegs ma las/ de ltar na lus dkyil gyi lha rnams sa bon las bskyed par thal/ sras don ma sogs las bskyed par gsungs pa'i phyir/ 'dod na mi bskyed par thal/
sga theng ma dang dpe mdzod ma gnyis las mi bskyed par bshad pa'i phyir/ ma grub na der thal/ lte ba'i rtsa aM yig gi rnam pa can dang / de'i nang gi khams gnyis bskyed
rim gyi skabs kyi lha'i bskyed chog gi sa bon yin pa rgya bod su'ang mi 'thad pa'i phyir/ des na slob dpon rin po che'i lung sbyor du gsungs pa'ang pho brang lnga'i gtso
bo'i sa bon tsam bstan pa yin gyi/ khyed 'dod pa ltar yin na de dag brtag gnyis nas

bshad pa'i yig 'bru lnga po de las bskyed dgos pa la/ de 'dra sus kyang ma bshad pa'i phyir ro/ /des na gnas de dag gi rtsa yig hU~M la sogs pa'i rnam par gnas pa rnams de
dang der bskyed pa las de bskyed ces brjod pa la dgongs nas aM las/ hU~M las sogs gsungs/ ngo bo rtsa yi ge'i rnam par gnas pa de nyid ka lhar bskyed rgyu yin pas/ las dang
po pa rnams go bde ba dang / blun po rnams la 'di lta bu'i log rtog skye ba dgag pa'i phyir aM rin chen 'byung ldan sogs gsal bar gsungs/ don la khyad par med pa ni gnad
kyi bshad pa yin no zhes gsungs la/ yang thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyi tshangs pa'i rigs sngags su 'byung khungs kyi don cung zad bshad pa/ skabs don gyi
rtsod lan phye ste btab pa dang don tshan gnyis su mdzad nas/ dang po la/ khyed kyi 'byung khungs kyi tshig ces pa de sangs rgyas las chos 'byung / nyi ma las 'od zer 'byung
/ sprin las char 'byung zhes pa lta bu la 'byung khungs kyi tshig ces bshad pas/ de 'dir yang sbyar na aM las rin chen 'byung ldan 'byung zhes pa lta bur 'gyur bas/
de'i tshe aM las byung ba'i rin 'byung aM nyid las logs pa zhig 'dod dgos pa snga ma de rnams kyi rigs pas shes shing de ni skabs 'dir mi rung ste/ aM las logs su gyur pa'i
rin 'byung zhig sprul 'khor gyi dbus su bsgom pa tshad ldan sus kyang ma bshad pa'i phyir zhes sogs gsungs/ don tshan gnyis pa la'ang yin lugs kyi go ba chags pa la phyogs
gnyis mi 'gal ba dang / dang po'i las can la ngag 'don cig shos

'khrul gzhi chung ba gnyis su mdzad nas/ dang po la/ spyir rnal 'byor pa'i rten dkyil 'khor bzhi grub tsam nas sku bzhi rang bzhin lhun gyis grub pa yin pas gcig la mtshon
na sprul 'khor gyi dbus kyi aM rtsar grub tsam nas sprul sku rang bzhin lhun grub/ yi ge'i gzugs su grub tsam na longs sku/ de'i bdud rtsi grub tsam na chos sku/ thams cad
la khyab pa'i rlung grub tsam na ngo bo nyid kyi sku grub pa yin no/ /de lta bu'i lus kyi aM yig de zhal phyag gi rnam par grub pa ni rin 'byung yin la/ rin 'byung de rtsa
yi ge'i rnam par gnas pa ni sprul 'khor gyi dbus kyi aM yig go /de ltar kha sbyor dang / bde mchog rtsa rgyud las bshad la/ de bzhin du 'khor lo gzhan rnams la'ang shes
par byas la 'bras bu la zhen cing lam la zhugs pas lus kyi rtsa yig la sogs pa lhar mthong ba sogs kyi gsal snang khyad par can skyes pa'i tshe lus dkyil mthong ba zhes
bya/ mthar dkyil 'khor bzhi po de las logs su sku bzhi btsal mi dgos par yon tan gyi tshogs yar ldan du gyur pa de nyid la 'bras bu mthar thug ces bya'o/ /de lta bu'i go
ba rags pa tsam yod pa'i gang zag la aM yig las logs pa'i rin 'byung zhig bskyed chog gi sgo nas gsar du bskyed dgos pa'i dogs pa mi 'byung bas ngag 'don gang byas kyang
don la 'gal ba med gsungs/ don tshan gnyis pa la/ dang po'i las can 'ga' zhig la aM las rin 'byung zhes sogs byas na phyi dkyil ltar aM yongs su gyur pa las byung ba'i
rin 'byung zhig cho gas bskyed dgos pa'i dogs pa skye srid pas

'khrul gzhi de mi 'byung ba dang / yi ge de ltar go ba'i phyir ngag 'dod ltar mdzad pa yin gyi/ las zhes pa'i tshig de nor zhes pa'i don min pas de tsam la dgag sgrub byed
pa blo gros chung ba yin/ bshad mdzod ma dang / sga theng ma las bshad pa de kho bo cag kyang 'dod la/ de dag tu bskyed pa dang rang bzhin gyis grub pa gnyis 'gal lo snyam
na/ de ni chos lugs 'di las phyi rol du gyur pa yid srubs kyi gsang tshig snying la zhugs pa'i bshes gnyen gzhan lus la lha bskyed pa dang lus dkyil gyi khyad par ma phyed
ces sun 'byin 'phangs mkhan dag gi rjes su khyed kyang zhugs pa'o/ /'o na slob dpon rin po ches bhUM la sogs pa pho brang lnga'i sa bon du bshad pas phyi dkyil ltar lha
rnams sa bon las bskyed pa las 'os med do snyam na/ dogs pa de 'ga' zhig la skye srid pa la dgongs nas ngag 'don de ltar mdzad pa yin la/ slob dpon rin po che'i gsung
gis ni bhrUM la sogs pa pho brang lnga'i gtso bo rnams kyi sa bon du bstan gyi/ lus dkyil gyi tshe sa bon de rnams las bskyed dgos pa ma bstan no/ /'o na ci snyam na lam
dus kyi rig pa'i dbang lnga'i rigs lnga pho brang lnga'i gtso bor gnas gyur pa lta bu'i tshe rgyu dbang dang mthun par rdo rje'i cho ga las bskyed pa'am sa bon las bskyed
na bhrUM la sogs pa las bskyed ces pa yin gyi/ lus dkyil gyi tshe sa bon bhrUM sogs las bskyed pa'i don ma yin te/ de yin par khungs thub kyi gzhung bshad dag las ma bshad
pas/ sa chen gyi gsung dang 'gal ba zhig slob dpon rin po che'i dgongs par bsgrubs na slob dpon rin po che la skur

'debs su 'gro/ des na bhrUM sogs rigs lnga'i sa bon du bshad pas lus dkyil gyi lha sa bon las bskyed dgos na/ rnam bshad nyi 'od las bhrUM sogs rigs lnga'i bdag nyid du bshad
pas de dag de rnams kyi ngo bo'am bdag nyid du 'gyur la/ de ni khyed la 'gal te pho brang lnga'i dbus kyi yig 'bru rnams rigs lnga'i ngo bo las gzhan pa'i sa bon du khyod
kyis khas blangs pa'i phyir ro/ /des na slob dpon rin po che'i gsung gi don pho brang lnga'i gtso bo rnams sa bon las bskyed pa'i tshe bhrUM sogs las bskyed/ lus dkyil
gyi tshe tsaNDa lI dang mthun pa'i yi ge rnams lus dkyil gyi lhar bsgom zhes pa'i don gnyis ka tshig nyung ngus bstan pa yin pas rang gis mthong ba de kho na yin gyi/ gzhan
ni gti mug go snyam pa'i phyogs re ba'i blo de dor na legs par mngon no zhes gsungs shing / don bsdus don brgyad pa las kyang / lus dkyil lha rnams bskyed pa'i gzhi/
/aM las zhes sogs 'byung khungs kyi/ /tshig tu 'dod na gzhan dag las/ /sangs rgyas las chos chos las ni/ /'phags pa'i tshogs zhes gang gsungs pa/ /'di 'dra'i rigs la 'byung
khungs kyi/ /tshig ces mkhas pa rnams la grags/ /khyed kyang de ltar 'dod na ni/ /aM las byung zhing aM yig las/ /logs su gyur pa'i rin 'byung zhig /sprul 'khor dbus
su 'dod dgos par/ /snga ma de yi rigs pas grub/ /de 'dra khyed cag bzhed lags sam/ /zhes dang / rje btsun rtse mo'i lung sbyor gyi/ /tshig des lus dkyil sa bon las/ /bskyed
par grub na bhrUMaM

sogs/ /rtsa rgyud nas bshad yig lnga las/ /lus dkyil lha rnams bskyed par rigs/ /lus dkyil sa bon bhrUM aM sogs/ /yin zhes bsgrubs nas lha bskyed tshe/ /de dag min pa'i ha~M
sogs las/ /bskyed pa 'gal ba ltag sprod yin/ /gal te bhrUM aM la sogs pa'i/ /sa bon nyid las bskyed do zhes/ /'dod na gzhung bshad thams cad las/ /tsaNDa lI dang mthun
pa yi/ /yig 'bru rnams las bskyed pa'i tshul/ /gsal bar bshad pa gzhung bshad la/ /mkhas par rlom pa khyed kyis bkag /sa chen 'gegs pa'i sa skya pa'i/ /gzhung bshad mkhas
rlom de re blun/ /gzhan du 'dam kha byung mod kyang / /skabs 'dir lus 'di grub zin shig /lhar bsgoms pa las 'dam kha med/ /yang na 'gal la ma 'khrul pa'i/ /tshad ma khas
len byed dam ci/ /kho bo cag ni lung de'i don/ /rig pa'i dbang lnga'i rigs lnga po/ /pho brang gtso bor gnas gyur tshe/ /bhrUM aM sogs las bskyed pa dang / /lus dkyil bsgom
tshe ha~M sogs las/ /bskyed pa gnyis ka tshig nyung ngus/ /bstan par 'dod kyi cig shos min/ /dang po'i las can gang zag gis/ /lus dkyil lha rnams sa bon las/ /gsar du
bskyed pa ma yin par/ gdod nas grub par go ba'i phyir/ /ngag 'don tshe na de mdzad kyi/ /las zhes bya ba'i tshig de dag /nor pa yin par su zhig smra/ /de phyir skabs don
ma longs par/ /tshig tsam rtsod pa'i ngal ba de/ /byis pa rnams kyi khyad nor yin/ /zhes gsungs so/ de dag gi yang lan du mkhan chen bzang bkras pas snyan brgyud 'khrul
sel

las/ sa bon phyir na aM yig las/ /logs su rin 'byung bsgom pa'i phyir/ /'byung khungs ji skad bshad bzhin 'dod/ /phyogs snga ma longs rang 'dod bris/ /gzhan du lung rigs gnod
pa yod/ /sras don ma las rtsa med na/ /sprul sku 'byung ba'i rgyu med cing / /lam gyis gnas 'gyur sprul skur 'char/ /de bas rang bzhin lhun grub dang / /'gyur rung gnyis
dgongs rgyu ni rtsa/ /sprul sku rang bzhin lhun grub bzhag /de ltar yang yang rgyu zhes gsungs/ /rig pa aM gi yi ge de/ /rin 'byung yin na ser sna yi/ /dri bral mnyam
nyid ye shes 'gyur/ /des na hU~M sogs bzhi po yang / /ye shes bzhi ru cis mi 'gyur/ /sems can dri bral ye shes lnga/ /ldan phyir ha cang thal bar 'gyur/ /rang lus rgyal ba'i
dkyil 'khor zhes/ /grags kyang gnad 'di shes pa dkon/ /'on te rang bzhin rnam dag la/ /bsams na zhal phyag rnam pa 'gal/ /bsgom pa'i blo ngo yin na ni/ /grub tshig smos
pa 'gal ba yin/ /bsgrub gzhi rang bzhin lhun grub phyir/ /phyi dkyil dang ni mi 'dra zhes/ /mkhas mang mthun pa kho bos mthong / /khyed kyi go lugs 'di ltar na/ /lus dkyil
rtsod pa'ang spang bar dka'/ /zhes dang / sa bon dang ni bskyed pa la/ /skyog bshad 'khrul pa'i rjes gnon yin/ /bhrUM sogs lus dkyil bskyed pa yi/ /sa bon 'di lngas
bya ba 'am/ /tsaNDa lI dang rjes mthun par/ /gang rung bya zhes 'dam khar gsungs/ /gzhung bshad rnams su phyi ma bris/ /de ltar ma mthong tshod rgyag mang / /sgra grub

tshul la'ang dpyad gzhi yod/ /yi ger skyon snyam re zhig bzhag /ngor pa chen po'i bir srung du/ /rang nyid birWar bsgom pa la/ /pho brang lha lnga'i sa bon bsam/ /zhes 'di'ang
skyog bshad ma byed cig /ces gsungs shing / sgyi chu ba buddha shrI'i nor bu'i phreng bar tshangs pa'i rig sngags kyi bzhed pa rags rim bkod pa'i rjes su/ aM las logs
su gyur pa'i rin 'byung sprul 'khor gyi dbus su sgom dgos par 'gyur te aM las byung ba'i rin 'byung aM nyid las logs su gyur pa zhig 'dod dgos pa'i phyir/ 'khor gsum/ aM
las logs su gyur pa'i rin 'byung khas blangs dgos par 'gyur te sangs rgyas las logs su gyur pa'i chos khas blangs pa'i phyir te/ sangs rgyas las byung ba'i chos sangs rgyas
nyid las logs su khas blangs pa'i phyir/ bhrUM la sogs pa pho brang lnga'i sa bon yin par bstan na/ sa bon las mi bskyed pa ci/ sa bon gyi don gang / rig pa'i dbang lnga'i
tshe'ang sa bon las bskyed pa'i don min zhes pa blo gros kyi 'char sgo ya mtshan che/ dang po'i las can la cig shos 'khrul gzhi chung zhes pa/ rje btsun gong ma rnams
kyis brtan pa thob pa'i gang zag 'ba' zhig gi ngag 'don du gsungs pa lags sam/ ma mkhyen pa gang lags/ las zhes pa'i 'byung tshig smos pas ngan par 'gyur du dogs na/ gtum
mo'i aM las me 'byung ba dang / spyi bo'i haM las byang sems 'bab pa rnams la ji ltar chos lags/ bsam mno thong la smros shig ces gsungs la/ mkhas pa gong ma'i gsungs
de dag las/ paN chen rin po ches rten dkyil 'khor

bzhi grub pa na sku bzhi rang bzhin lhun grub tu 'byung ba'i rang bzhin lhun grub kyi sku bzhi po de rten lus kyi dkyil 'khor bzhi'i chos nyid la bshad pa 'di ji ltar yin dpyad
par bya zhing / ngor rdzong gnyis po lus dkyil gyi tshe ngag 'don la aM las zhes pa dang / aM rin chen 'byung ldan zhes pa tsam gyi khyad par ma gtogs sgom don la khyad
par ma byung bas rnam dbye ha cang 'gal ba bya rgyu mi snang la/ 'on kyang aM las logs su gyur pa'i rin 'byung yod med kyi rnam gzhag la/ bdag nyid chen po sa paN gyis/
thub pas 'jig rten mthun 'jug la/ /dgongs nas phyi rol don du gsungs/ /tha snyad dpyod pa'i rigs pa la/ /dgongs nas chos rnams sems su gsungs/ /dam pa'i don la dgongs
nas ni/ /chos kun spros pa bral zhes gsungs/ /zhes pa dang / de'i don kun mkhyen chen pos bdud rtsi spel bar/ 'on kyang 'di la sa paN gyis gsung rab 'chad pa la 'jug tshul
la/ tha snyad khas ni ma blangs par/ /nged cag 'chad par mi byed do/ /zhes par ltar tha snyad khas blangs pa 'jig rten mthun 'jug gi skabs dang / tha snyad dpyod pa'i rigs
pa'i skabs dang / don dam dpyod pa'i rigs pa'i skabs gsum gsungs pa bla med 'chad tshul la sbyar na/ skabs dang po'i tshe snang ba lha yin par khas mi blangs te 'di ni
sems can yin/ 'di ni sangs rgyas yin/ 'di ni bum pa yin/ 'di ni snam bu yin zhes sogs rnam gzhag so sor phye ba'i skabs yin pa'i phyir ro/ /gnyis pa'i tshe phung po lnga
sangs rgyas lnga yin pa sogs snang ba thams

cad lhar khas len dgos te bskyed rim gyi sbyang gzhi sbyong byed sbyar ba'i rigs pas dpyad pa'i tshe lha ma yin pa'i snang ba gang yang med pa'i phyir ro/ /gsum pa'i tshe lha
yin pa dang ma yin pa sogs mtha' gang yang khas mi len te/ spros pa thams cad dang bral ba'i phyir ro zhes gnas skabs gsum du phye nas gsungs pa ltar 'dir yang 'chad dgos
shing / de ltar bshad pa de'i tshe gnas skabs dang po'i tshe sangs rgyas dang sems can sogs 'di dang 'di'o zhes so sor 'byed pa 'jig rten mthun 'jug ltar khas len dgos
shing / de bzhin du aM dang rin 'byung yang so so ba yin pas aM las logs su gyur pa'i rin 'byung 'dod dgos shing / gnas skabs gnyis pa'i tshe snang ba thams cad sems su
khas len pas na sems las logs su gyur pa'i phyi rol gyi don med ces 'chad pa dang tshul mtshungs par lus dkyil sgom pa'i tshe'ang aM de nyid ka rin 'byung du sgom pa yin
zhing / de ltar bsgom pa'i rnal 'byor pa de'i blo ngo na rang gi sprul 'khor gyi dbus su aM las logs su gyur pa'i rin 'byung med de/ de'i aM de nyid ka rin 'byung du bsgom
pa yin gyis de las logs su gyur pa'i rin 'byung bsgom rgyu ma yin pas so/ /gnas skabs gsum pa'i tshe spros pa thams cad dang bral bas na aM las logs su gyur pa'i rin 'byung
yod med kyi spros pa'ang bkag ste brjod pa dang sgom pa sogs thams cad khas len dang bral ba zhig tu 'chad dgos pa 'dra snyam te dpyad par bya'o/ /des na sgyi chu ba
buddha shrI'i aM las logs su gyur pa'i rin 'byung 'dod dgos te/ aM las

byung ba'i rin 'byung aM nyid las logs su gyur pa'i phyir zhes pa lta bu gnas skabs dang po la dgongs par song bas dpyad pa de lus dkyil gyi skabs 'dir 'jug pa dka'o/ /des
na phyogs gnyis kyi gsung de dag gi go don la legs par brtags na ngag 'don ma mthun pa tsam ma gtogs/ don gyi cha la mi mthun pa cher med pa 'dra snyam pa rang nyid kyi blo
la shar ba tsam ste/ da dung blo gros dang ldan pa dag gis legs par dpyad dgos so// //bdun pa lus dkyil gyi lha la rgyas btab rigs mtshon yod med kyi rnam gzhag la/ mus
srad pa chen po'i rgyas btab rigs mtshon med pa dang zhes pa'i rgyas bshad du/ yang kha cig rgyas btab kyi skabs su sambu Ta las/ rdo rje sems dpa' zhes byar bshad/ /bde
ba dam pa ru ni brjod/ /ces pa 'khor lo drug tu 'dod pa rnams kyi lugs la spyi gtsug gi 'khor lo rdo rje sems dpa' bsgom pa la 'bru mnan pas chog mod/ man ngag 'di pa'i
lugs la rgyas 'debs kyi lha bstan pa yin cing / de dang mthun par slob dpon dgra las rnam rgyal gyi phyag rgya bzhi'i rgyas 'debs las/ kun gyi dbang bskur gnas su ni/ rdo
rje sems dpa' zla ba'i mdog /ces bshad pas lus dkyil gyi lha la rdo rje sems dpas rgyas 'debs rgyud dang rgya gar ba'i dgongs pa yin par gsal lo zhes zer zhing / ngag 'don
gyi skabs su lus dkyil gyi lha thams cad la rdo rje sems dpas dbu brgyan zer ro/ /de las sambu Ta'i lung de'i rigs bdag gi rgyas btab ston pa gang las bshad/ gnad kyi
gsal byed las

ni/ gsang ba las ni sa'i khams/ /zhes pa nas brtsam te/ chos kyi skur ni rab tu grags/ /zhes pa'i bar gyis rang byung gi ye shes kyi mtshan nyid ston pa las/ de la rgyas par
bstan pa dang / bsdus te bstan pa dang / shin tu bsdus te bstan pa'o/ /dang po la gsum/ rten zhu ba 'byung ba lngar bstan pa/ brten pa bde ba ye shes lngar bstan pa/ de
nyid rigs lngar bstan pa zhes gsungs pa'i rigs lngar bstan pa'i skabs su/ shin tu rnam dag ye shes che/ /rdo rje sems dpa' zhes byar bshad/ /ces pa'i tshig rkang gnyis bsdebs
te mi bskyod pa dang rdo rje sems dpa' gnyis ka phyogs gcig tu thams cad bdag nyid kyi ston pa'i gzhung yin pas/ de ni rgyas par ston pa'i skabs yin la/ bde ba dam
pa ru ni brjod/ /ces pa ni/ bsdus te bstan pa la rten thig le bsdus te bstan pa dang / brten pa bde stong bsdus te bstan pa gnyis kyi/ brten pa bde stong bsdus te bstan pa
yin par gsungs pas/ gzhung mtshams kyang tha dad cing rigs bdag gi rgyas gdab ston par dogs pa'i gnas tsam yang med la/ rang blos sbyar bas rje btsun gong ma'i lugs su
'gyur ram/ slob dpon dgra las rnam par rgyal ba'i gzhung yang pho brang drug pa ston pa'i gzhung yin/ rigs bdag gi rgyas gdab ston pa'i gzhung ma yin te gzhung gi skabs la
dpyad pas shes pa yin no/ /de ltar na sgrub byed rnam par dag pa med bzhin du/ rje btsun gyi gsung rnams dor nas gzhan du smra ba 'di la dgos pa ci zhig yod/ 'o na rje
btsun gong ma'i gsung las ji ltar bshad ce na/ sras

don ma las dbang rtags ni lha thams cad la blangs na gtso bo lnga la sku rdo rje rnam snang la sogs pa'i rigs lnga/ 'khor rnams la rang gi gtso bo'am/ yang na thams cad kyi
dbu la gnas lngar rdo rje rtsa lnga pa re re bsam mo zhes dang / 'phags pa rin po ches gtso bo lnga la rdo rje sems dpa'/ pho brang gi 'khor rnams la rang rang gi gtso bo/
skye mched kyi lha rnams la rang rang gi kha dog dang mthun pa'i rigs bdag khro bo bcu la srung 'khor gyi skabs nas 'byung ba bzhin rigs kyi bdag pos dbu brgyan par bsam
mo zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /'o na bshad pa gnyis po ma mthun pas 'phags pas gsungs pa de mi 'thad do zhe na/ mi mthun par snang ba ni brgyud pa'i man ngag med par yi ge
la thug 'phrad du byas pa'i smra ba de 'dir rdo rje sems dpa' ni rigs lnga po rang rang gi rgyu rdo rje 'dzin pa yin pas rang rigs kyi rgyas gdab pa yang yin la/ rdo rje
sems dpas rgyas gdab pa'ang yin pas don gcig yin no zhes 'byung ngo / de'i lan du paN chen rin po che'i rnam thar sgo brgyad par/ 'di'i lan ni don tshan bdun gyi sgo nas
mgo smos pa tsam gyis go bar bya ste/ 'di ltar kha sbyor rtsa 'grel du rgyas gdab kyi dngos bstan med kyang / man ngag lugs la rgyas gdab tu sbyor dgos pa/ de'i rgyab brten
du man ngag snye ma dang / phyag rgya bzhi pa'i lung sbyar ba/ rgol bas phyag rgya bzhi pa'i khungs ma mthong bzhin du pho brang drug gi khungs su bshad pas pho tshod
kyi rang bzor bstan pa/ lha thams cad la rdo rje sems dpas dbu brgyan pa dang / sras don ma las

bshad pa'i khyad par dbu rgyan rang chas can dang / dbang dngos su blangs pa'i khyad par du bstan pa/ rgol bas 'phags pa'i lung phyogs snga la gnod byed du drangs pa na sras
don ma'i rang lugs bkag par bstan pa/ de dang de mi 'gal ba'i skyon spang byas pa na phyogs snga ma gnod byed du 'phangs pa thams cad rgol ba rang la log pas lung rigs
kyi go ba ma chags par bstan pa/ grub mtha'i gting ma tshugs par lung 'dren mang pas gong ma lnga 'gal ba can du khas len dgos pa rnams byung ba yin no zhes gsungs la/ tshar
chen chos kyi rgyal po'i rdo rje'i 'khrul 'khor gyi zegs mar smra ba bdun pa lus dkyil gyi lha la rgyas gdab rigs mtshon med pa'i sgrub byed du rdo rje sems dpas rgyas
gdab ces zer ba dang / pho brang lnga'i gtso bo lnga la sras don mar rnam snang la sogs pa rigs lnga so sos rgyas gdab pa dang / 'phags pa rin po ches gtso bo lnga la rdo
rje sems dpas rgyas 'debs par gsungs pa la/ de gnyis dgongs pa gcig pa'i sgrub byed du/ de'i skabs kyi rigs lnga dang rdo rje sems dpa' khyad par med par byas nas/ rgyas
'debs de rang rigs kyi rgyas gdab kyang yin la/ rdo rje sems dpa'i rgyas gdab kyang yin par 'dod do/ /de ltar na lus dkyil gyi lha rnams la rdo rje sems dpas rgyas btab
pa rigs mtshon med pa ma yin par thal/ rigs mtshon yod pa'i phyir/ der thal/ rang rigs kyi rgyas gdab yod pa'i phyir/ der thal/ rdo rje sems dpa'i rgyas gdab yin pa'i phyir/
'khor gsum/ sambu Ta'i lung gis bstan pa'i sgrub byed gnad kyi

gsal byed las ma bshad do zhes pa'ang mi 'thad de/ der rgyud 'chad pa'i dbang du byas pa'i bshad pa yin la/ 'dir man ngag lugs kyi lung sbyor du 'dren pa la de ji lta ba dgos
pa'i nges pa med pa'i phyir dang / phyag rgya bzhi pa'i lung gis pho brang drug pa kho na ston rgyu yin na/ bstan bcos der pho brang lnga'i lha brgya lnga bcu rtsa bdun
bstan pa'i rjes su/ kun gyi dbang bskur gnas su ni/ /rdo rje sems dpa' zla ba'i mdog /ces gsungs pas lha de thams cad kyi dbang bskur ba'i gnas spyi bor rdo rje sems dpa'
re re 'god par bshad la/ de ltar min na kun gyi zhes pa'i mang tshig gi 'bru ji ltar gnon soms shig des na sras don mar lha thams cad la rdo rje rtse lnga pas rgyas 'debs
par gsungs pa'ang 'di dang shin tu gnad mthun pa yin no zhes gsungs la/ mkhas pa'i dbang po dkon mchog lhun grub kyi tshangs pa'i rigs sngags su dngos bstan rtsod phreng
so so'i lan dang / zhe 'dod kyi dngos lan ma 'khrul ba gnyis su mdzad nas/ dang po la rgol bas kha sbyor gyi lung don phyogs gcig tu zhen pas blo gros chung ba/ phyag
rgya bzhi pa'i lung ma mthong ba'i 'ol tshod byas pa/ 'gal spong ma shes pas phyogs snga'i 'dod pa bsgrub pa ste don tshan gsum du mdzad nas/ dang po la kha sbyor gyi rgyud
'chad pa'i tshe rdzogs rim gyi ye shes ston byed du 'chad kyang / man ngag gi tshe lus dkyil ston pa mi 'gal ste/ rtsa rgyud kyi/ e yi rnam pa lha mo spyan/ /zhes sogs
dang / kha sbyor las/ e ne sa ru shes par bya/ /zhes sogs rgyud 'chad pa'i tshe

rdzogs rim ston byed du 'chad kyang / man ngag gi tshe lus dkyil gyi khungs su grub pa dang / rgyud kyi tshig re re la'ang spyi sbas mthar thug gi bshad pa du ma bya rgyu yod
cing bya bar yang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i bka' ni rgya mtsho bzhin/ /zhes sogs kyis bstan no/ TIka chen gyi dngos bstan ni rgyud 'chad pa'i tshe lus dkyil ston byed du
skabs su ma babs pas ma bshad pa yin gyi/ don dang ma 'brel ba ma yin te/ lus dkyil 'di dag rdzogs rim gyi ye shes 'dren pa'i thabs su gsungs la/ TIka chen der gzhung de
rdzogs rim gyi ye shes ston byed du gsungs pa'i phyir/ de ltar na lung de'i don man snyer/ 'khor lo lnga'i dbus su lha mo lnga bskyed pa'i lus dkyil du dngos su bshad la/
de'i tshe tshig rkang phyi ma gnyis 'khor lo drug pa rnams kyi de'i khungs dang / lnga pa'i tshe rigs bdag ston par phyag rgya bzhi pa'i lung gis grub bo zhes pa'i don
yin pas/ zin so 'di bzhin yod phyin rang blos sbyar bar sems pa ni phyogs 'dzin yin no/ gal te lung des lus dkyil ye ma bstan na/ gzhan 'khor lo drug pa dngos bstan gyi kye
rdor rgyud gsum gyi lung khungs bstan dgos/ des na chos rjes/ 'di mtha' 'di tsam kho nar gnas so zhes/ /zhes sogs gsungs pa ltar phyogs gcig la ma zhen pa dgos so zhes
gsungs/ gnyis pa la/ khyod kyis phyag rgya bzhi pa ma mthong bzhin du de'i don 'khor lo drug par 'chad pa 'ol tshod de/ phyag rgya bzhi pa las/ rnal 'byor chos mchog rang
gi lus/ /grub pa'i dkyil 'khor skad cig lta/ /lte ba drug cu rtsa bzhi'i

rtsa/ /sa yi rang bzhin spyan ma ser/ /las kyi phyag rgya'o/ /snying khar brgyad kyi rtsa rnams la/ /rdo rje btsun mo mA ma ki /mdog sngon gri gug thod pa 'dzin/ /gar gyis
legs rol chu yi khams/ /chos kyi phyag rgya'o/ /mgrin par 'khor lo longs spyod che/ /bcu drug rtsa las gos dkar mo/ /me khams rnam dag kha dog dmar/ /zhal gcig phyag gnyis
mdzes pa ma/ /phyag rgya chen po'o/ /gsang bar padma sum cu gnyis/ /sgrol ma ljang sngo rlung gi khams/ /steng gi bde chen 'khor lo la/ /rdo rje dbyings kyi dbang byung
ma/ /sum cu gnyis ldan kha dog dkar/ /bde chen nam mkha' nyid du brjod/ /dam tshig gi phyag rgya'o/ /rnam snang la sogs sangs rgyas rnams/ /'khor lo'i dbus su rol zhing
gnas/ /zhal mdog mtshan ma la sogs pa/ /ji skad rgyud las gsungs bzhin sgom/ /bsam gtan mi nus rnal 'byor gang / /rgyal chen 'khor los sgyur ba drug /bde ba dam pa'i yul
dang bcas/ /g.yas brkyang pa yi rol pa'i sku/ /'khor lo'i mdog mtshungs zhal gcig pa/ /'khor lo padma rdo rje dang / /rin chen padma rdo rje dang / /rin chen ral gri g.yas
na ste/ /g.yas min par ni dril bu 'o/ /kun gyi dbang bskur gnas su ni/ /rdo rje sems dpa' zla ba'i mdog /shes rab ma dang mnyam sbyor ba/ /rdo rje dril bu 'dzin pa bsgom/
/zhes pa 'di'i dngos bstan pho brang drug pa yin na/ pho brang dang po lnga la rtsa 'dab kyi grangs dang / lha mo dang / phyag rgya bzhi'i bsdu tshul rnams bshad nas drug
pa la de

dag ma byung ba dang / 'khor lo drug phyogs gcig tu bshad na/ rnam snang la sogs sangs rgyas rnams/ /'khor lo'i dbus su rol zhing gnas/ /zhes spyi sdom phyogs cig tu byas nas/
rgyal chen 'khor los sgyur ba drug /ces bshad chog pa las de mi 'byung bar 'khor los sgyur ba lnga phyogs gcig tu bshad zin nas/ kun gyi dbang bskur gnas su ni/ /zhes
'byung ba ji ltar yin rnam dpyod kyi blo gros yod na da chod cig ces gsungs/ gsum pa la rdo rje sems dpas rgyas btab dang / rang rigs kyi gtso bo rigs lnga gang rung gi
rgyas gdab gnyis mi 'gal bas/ khyod kyi rdo rje sems dpa' ni rigs lnga po rang rang gi rgyu rdo rje 'dzin pa yin pas rang rigs kyi rgyas gdab kyang yin/ rdo rje sems dpa'i
rgyas gdab kyang yin pas don cig ces pa des kho bo cag gi 'dod pa bsgrub pa yin gsungs/ don tshan dang po'i gnyis pa la/ sras don ma'i rgyas gdab dang po dang / 'phags
pa'i dgongs pa mi 'gal bar 'chad pa gnyis char mthun la/ sras don ma'i phyi ma kha cig dbu rgyan rang chas su bsgom pa la 'dod kyang / de ni dmigs pa bsgom sla ba'i phyir
yin cing / gzhan lha thams cad la rang rigs kyi rigs lnga gang rung gi rgyas 'debs rung ba phyag rgya bzhi pa las 'byung ba dang / gong ma'i bshad pa kho bo cag gi ngag
'don rnams gnad gcig pas rgyun gyi nyams len la spros pa'i bye brag gis ci rigs rung ngo / /des na rdor sems rigs thams cad kyi bdag po dang / rigs lnga char gyi rgyu rdor
'dzin yin pas nges gsal med pa rnams la des rgyas 'debs

rung ba yin la/ 'on kyang rgyu rdor 'dzin rigs drug par bshad pas rgyu rdor 'dzin yin na rigs lnga po gang rung yin mi dgos pas rang rigs zhes bya'o zhes gsungs so/ de bzhin
du don bsdus don brgyad pa las/ lus dkyil lha la rdor sems kyi/ /rigs bdag bshad pa de nor na/ /'phags pas lus dkyil gtso bo la/ /rdor sems rigs bdag bshad pa de/ /rnam
pa kun du 'dor dgos so/ /gal te 'phags pas bshad pa de/ /rdor sems rigs bdag rigs lnga yi/ /rgyu yi rdor 'dzin yin pa'i phyir/ /de la 'gal ba med ces smra/ /de lta na ni
lha kun gyis/ /rigs bdag rigs lnga'i rgyu rdor 'dzin/ /rdo rje sems dpa' yin pas na/ /gtso bo kun la rdor sems kyis/ /rgyas 'debs byed pa grub pa'i phyir/ /skabs kyi rtsod
pa sprin bzhin dengs/ /zhes dang / phyag rgya bzhi pa'i dngos bstan de/ /pho brang drug par khyed 'dod na/ /pho brang lnga la rtsa 'dab dang / 'khor sogs bshad nas drug
pa la/ /de dag mi 'byung ba de ci/ /spyi gtsug 'khor lo zhes pa de/ /phyag rgya bzhi po gang du 'dus/ /phyag rgya bzhi ru ma 'dus pa'i/ /phyag rgya bzhi pa gad mo'i gnas/
/'khor los sgyur ba drug yod na/ /rgyal chen 'khor los sgyur ba lnga/ /zhes pa'i gzhung de nor ram ci/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de rnams kyi yang lan du mkhan chen bzang
bkras pas snyan brgyud 'khrul sel las/ thog mar mus srad pa chen po'i bzhed pa bkod/ de la tshangs pa'i rigs sngags su skyon brjod mdzad tshul bshad pa'i rjes su/ a

seng ma las rdo rje yi/ /theg pa dgongs pa du ma bzhes/ /gsungs pa de nyid mthong na yang / /mkha' 'gros byin rlabs birWa sogs/ /grub thob rnams la brten dgos zhes/ /'di 'dra
ma mthong rgyud don rnams/ /rang dgar rtog ge'i rigs pas 'chad/ /birWa'i snyan brgyud zab mo rnams/ /rgyud dang rgya gzhung 'gal lo zhes/ /'brel med tshig 'di gzhan lugs
bzhin/ /snyan brgyud yi ge med pa'i rtags/ /de yi zin so mkhas pas khrel/ /'khor lo drug pa'ang lnga po bzhin/ /don gyis bstan zhing ma bstan na/ /khyed kyi rgyud don
ji ltar 'chad/ /khyad par rgyas btab zur du gsungs/ /'gal yang snyan brgyud ga la gnod/ /'khor lo drug pa man ngag lugs/ /gdan sogs yi ger shin tu gsal/ /dbu rgyan rang chas
zer ba de/ /snyan brgyud med pa'i bab col yin/ /gsung ngag ma rdzogs rang rigs sogs/ /rgyas gdab dgos pa snying po de/ /zhib tu gsang gtam mi sgrog go /zhes gsungs la/
sgyi chu ba buddha shrI'i nor bu'i phreng bar phyogs snga ma'i rjes su zlos pa shes pa'ang ngo mtshar che mod/ des kyang da dung skabs don 'grub pa ma yin te/ sras don
ma'i rgyas gdab ni rgyas gdab rdzogs pa'i skabs la dgongs pas 'phags pa'i lugs ltar byed dgos te/ snyan brgyud kyi skabs tha dad pa yin pa'i phyir/ man ngag dang ldan pa'i
bshes gnyen la gtugs shig ces pa tsam las yang lan rgyas pa ma mdzad la/ de ltar mkhas pa so so'i bshad tshul de dag las/ paN chen gyis lha thams cad la rdo rje sems dpas
dbu brgyan pa dang / sras don ma

las bshad pa'i khyad par dbu rgyan rang chas can dang / dbang dngos su blangs pa'i khyad par du bstan pa zhes gsungs pa 'di dang / tshangs pa'i rig sngags las sras don ma'i
phyogs phyi ma ni dbu rgyan rang chas can du bsgom pa'i don yin zhes 'ga' zhig smra yang / de'i don dmigs pa bsgom sla ba'i phyir yin zhes gsungs pa gnyis cung zad ma mthun
zhing / tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i gsungs dang tshangs pa'i rig sngags kyi de dag dgongs pa mthun par snang la/ mkhan chen bzang bkras pas tshangs pa'i rigs sngags
kyi bzhed pa bkod pa'i skabs su/ sras don ma yi phyi ma ni/ /dbu rgyan rang chas don yin zer/ /zhes pa dang / de ltar 'gog pa na/ dbu rgyan rang chas zer ba de/ /snyan
brgyud med pa'i bab col yin/ /zhes gsungs kyang / tshangs pa'i rig sngags na sras don ma'i bshad tshul phyi ma dbu rgyan rang chas can du 'ga' zhig 'dod kyang zhes gsungs
nas de mi bzhed pas phyogs snga ma longs pa'i sun 'byin du song 'dug go /phyag rgya bzhi pa'i dngos bstan la ni pho brang lnga pa ma gtogs drug pa gsal ba rang ma byung
la/ mkhan chen bzang bkras pa'i gsungs las/ 'khor lo drug pa'ang lnga po bzhin/ /don gyis bstan zhing ma bstan na/ /khyed kyis rgyud don ji ltar 'chad/ /ces gsungs pas rdzong
lugs la pho brang dang po lnga gsal bar bstan pa'i shugs la/ drug pa ni/ kun gyi dbang bskur zhes sogs kyi tshigs bcad gcig gis pho brang dang / de'i gtso bo dngos su
bstan pa'i shugs la rtsa 'dab kyi grangs

dang / 'khor gyi lha mo sogs bstan gsung rgyur snang ngo / /de ltar phyogs gnyis po bshad tshul cung zad mi 'dra ba'ang legs par brtags na/ mus srad pa chen pos sras don ma
dang / 'phags pa'i gsung la 'gal spong mdzad pa de ni ngor lugs la'ang bzhed par snang bas/ gong ma'i dgongs don la gnyis ka zhugs sam snyam ste dpyad par bya'o// //brgyad
pa bza' ba'i dam tshig yod med kyi rnam gzhag la/ mus srad pa chen po'i rnam bshad chu rgyun bzhi par/ bza' ba'i dam tshig med pa rnams/ /zhes pa'i rgyas bshad du mang
du gsungs pa'i snying po blangs nas bkod na/ yang kha cig dbang bskur rab gnas kyi dus su sdom brtson rab byung rnams kyis tshogs 'khor mi byed de/ sa skya paNTi tas bkag
pa'i phyir ro zhes pa phyogs sngar bkod nas sun 'byin pa na/ chos rje rang gi lugs dang / rje btsun gyi lung dang 'gal tshul brjod pa'i tshe/ chos rjes rab byung la dpa'
bo'i ston mo dgos par gsungs shing / dpa' bo'i ston mo tshogs 'khor gyi dbye bar mngon rtogs ljon shing las gsungs shing / chos rje rang gis kyang gsungs/ phyogs snga ma
ni dus khyad par can gyi tshe dpa' bo'i ston mo'ang mi byed pas bza' ba'i dam tshig las nyams shing / chos rjes bshad pa 'di klu sgrub nas/ jo bo rje dang kha che paN chen
sogs kyi lugs yin par bshad pas/ sa skya pa'i rang lugs ma yin gsungs/ dus khyad par can gyi tshe rab byung gis tshogs 'khor ma byas na rtsa ltung bcu gsum par 'gro ba
de 'khrul spong gi dgongs pa yin zhes pa dang / dus khyad

par can gyi bza' ba'i dam tshig dang / dus rgyun du bsten pa'i dam tshig gi khyad par ma phyed ces sogs kyis rgol ba mdzad do/ /de dag kyang ngor lugs kyi bshad tshul gang
la ched du rgol ba yin snyam na/ rje rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po'i tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i cho ga kun bzang rnam rol las/ gnyis pa gang zag mchod pa'i yo byad la/ rnal
'byor pa nus ldan dang / rab tu byung bas mchod pa'i rdzas gnyis kyi/ dang po ni/ Dombhi he ru kas/ de la sha dang chang dag dang / /zhes sogs dang / snying po rgyan du/
chang ni dpa' bos ma spyad par/ /zhes sogs drangs pa dang / gnyis pa ni bu ram dang / bu ram gyi lbu ba dang / zhun mar la sogs pa so sor thar par/ phyi dror gnang ba'i
rdzas rnams sha lnga bdud rtsi lngar byin gyis brlabs nas longs spyod kyi/ thabs shes kyi rdzas la longs spyod pa ma yin no/ /'o na tshogs 'khor gyi gzhung rnams las thabs
shes kyi rdzas gnyis la longs spyod par bshad pa dang 'gal lo zhe na/ de ni rnal 'byor pa chang 'o mar bsgyur nus pa la sogs pa nus pa dang ldan pa'i dbang du byas pa ste/
dri med 'od las/ gang dag gis sngags kyi stobs kyis sam zhes sogs 'dren par mdzad nas/ dge slong dang dge tshul chang 'o mar bsgyur ba'i nus pa dang mi ldan pa la ni
rdzas de dag lce la reg pa tsam ma gtogs longs mi spyod par/ 'phags pa klu sgrub yab sras dang / thogs med sku mched/ kha che paN chen sogs kyang bzhed par chos kyi rje sa
skya paNDi ta'i tshogs 'khor du bshad la/ dus

'khor dang sdom 'byung gi lung 'dren byas pa'i rjes su/ thar pa don du gnyer ba'i sgrub pa po rnams kyis phyi rol pa'i mchod sbyin dang mtshungs pa'i sha chang kho na la longs
spyod pa'i 'jig rten pa'i dga' ston la tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i ming gdags par mi bya'o zhes gsungs pa dang / gsang ba kun rgyan las 'di rab tu byung ba sdom brtson rnams
kyis tshogs 'khor byed na gong 'og gi cho ga rnams 'dra ba las/ dam tshig blangs te lce la reg pa tsam bya/ bu ram dang sbrang rtsi dang zhun mar rnams sha lnga bdud rtsi
lngar byin gyis brlabs la nang gi sbyin sreg gi tshul gyis bza'o/ /rnal 'byor pa rnams kyis kyang dam tshig gi rdzas la ran par longs spyod kyi/ chang myos kyi bar du
'thung ba dang / kha zas ha cang brgyags par longs spyod pa ni tshogs 'khor gyi skabs kyi dgag bya yin la/ khyad par bsad sha la longs spyod pa ni theg pa chen po'i mdo rgyud
mtha' dag las bkag pas/ dgra nag dang / a ra lli'i rgyud las bshad pa ltar ba glang sogs rang shi ba'i sha kho na dam rdzas su bzung ngo / de ltar mchod pa dang longs
spyod la tshim par longs spyad/ zas la dpyas mi gdags par mang du bza'/ skom ji snyed pa btung zhes sogs gsungs pa rnams la rgol ba yin no/ de ltar kun bzang rnam rol dang
/ gsang ba kun rgyan las bshad tshul la/ mus srad pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis lung rigs kyi dpyad pa mdzad pa de'i lan du/ paN chen rin po che'i rnam thar sgo brgyad
par/ rgol ba'i tshig gi dngos bstan la nang 'gal mang bas yid brtan mi rung bar bstan pa dang / dgos pa khyad par

can dang tshogs kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i nus pa yod med kyi sgo nas dngos lan gdab pa gnyis su mdzad nas/ dang po la 'dir rgol ba'i tshig la chos rjes gsungs pa'i dpa' bo'i
ston mo de tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid par rje btsun chen pos bzhed mi bzhed gnyis cig car du smras byung / sa paN gyi bzhed pas 'khrul spong bkag pa'am/ yang na 'khrul spong
gi rtsa ltung bcu gsum pa'i ngo bo nyid rnam par gzhag pa des chos rje'i dpa' bo'i ston mo bkag zer ba gnyis cig car du smras byung / phyogs snga ma dpa' bo'i ston mo la
tshad mar byed na rje btsun dang 'gal zer ba dang / rje btsun yang dpa' bo'i ston mo tshogs 'khor du bzhed zer ba gnyis ka byung / rje btsun dpa' bo'i ston mo tshogs 'khor
du mi bzhed na de bza' ba'i dam tshig ma yin par thal/ dus khyad par can gyi dang rgyun du ba gang yang ma yin pa'i phyir zhes brjod pa mtha' dag khyed rang la 'khor
byung zhes gsungs shing / gnyis pa la phyogs snga mas dbang rab gnas sbyin sreg gi tshe dpa' bo'i ston mo mi byed pa'i rgyus yod nas sus khyed la bshad/ phyogs snga ma kha
zas kyi rnal 'byor dang bdud rtsi myang ba 'od dpag med kyi yan lag sogs mi bzhed pa ci/ rgyun gyi bza' ba'i dam tshig gis dus khyad par can gyi de med pa'i dgag bya mi
khegs na dus khyad par can de dus rgyun du ba'i cha shas su mi gtogs pa yin nam/ spyir sdom brtson rdo rje 'dzin pa sa ma thob pa sogs lta zhog sbyangs rtogs sbar gsum mi
nus na khyim pa'i rdo rje 'dzin pas kyang tshogs 'khor rdzogs pa la longs spyod pa na zag med

kyi dga' bdes lus sems tshim par byas pa yin nam/ zag bcas kyi des de ltar byas pa yin brtags na rnam rtog dang bcas pa'i dga' bde ni tha mal gyi lam mo/ /de dang bral ba'i
dga' bde ni rdo rje 'dzin pa'i lam mo/ /de la sbyangs pa zhes bya ba ni tha mal gyi sha chang sogs lta ci/ rang nyid lhar gsal ba'i ye shes kyi ngo na tha mal gyi snang
ba tsam yang med pa'o/ /de ltar na'ang sangs rgyas ma thob kyi bar du rnal 'byor pa rang gi rnam shes la'ang tha mal pa dang mthun par snang ba ni zlog mi nus pas na gzhi
mi spong ba zhes dang / sgyu ma lta bur snang ba zhes pa de yin no/ /rtogs pa ni tshogs rdzas lta zhog bdag dang snang ba thams cad chos dbyings bde chen du ro gcig pa'o/
/de'i rgyu mtshan gyis de dus kyi rnam rol thams cad chos dbyings dang mnyam par spro nus pa ni sbar ba zhes pa yin no/ /'dir sdom brtson rdo rje 'dzin pa bsnyen pa rdzogs
pa bstan pa'i bdag por gyur pa ni sa la gnas kyang shin tu spros med kyi spyod pa spyad pa nyid kyis/ tshogs 'khor sogs spros bcas kyi spyod pa ma mdzad pa'i nyes pas
cung zad kyang ma gos par mchog gi dngos grub thogs med du 'grub pa yin te/ 'phags mchog klu sgrub dang slob dpon chen po zhi ba lha bzhin no zhes gsungs so/ yang tshar
chen rin po ches rdo rje'i 'khrul 'khor gyi zegs mar mus srad pa'i bzhed pa bskyar ba'i rjes su zhes zer ba rnams rim pa bzhin mi 'thad de/ ngor lugs la bza' ba'i dam tshig
yod par thal/ bdud rtsi ril bu bsten pa de bza' ba'i dam tshig yin pa'i phyir te rgyun gyi de yin pa'i phyir/ ri bong rwa

tshogs kyi 'khor lo yin par thal/ khyad par gyi bza' ba'i dam tshig tshogs 'khor yin pa'i phyir/ shes bya rtag par khas blangs na shes bya la rtag pas khyab pa khas len mi
dgos pas dgongs par zhu/ gzhan yang dpa' bo'i ston mo med par thal/ de yin na bza' ba'i dam tshig yin dgos pa las rgyun gyi de ni yin don med/ khyad par gyi de min te tshogs
'khor min pa'i phyir/ der thal/ rje btsun gyis/ tshogs kyi 'khor lo/ dpa' bo'i ston mo/ dpa' mo'i ston mo zhes de gsum mi 'dra ba tha dad du bshad pa'i phyir/ ma yin
te de gsum ming gi rnam grangs so snyam na/ de ltar na dpa' mo'i ston mo'ang dpa' bo'i ston mor 'gyur zhing / dpa' mo'ang dpa' bor 'gyur ba sogs brjod kyis mi lang bas 'di
'dra'i grub mtha' mi 'dzin par gsol ba 'debs so zhes gsungs so/ /yang thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis tshangs pa'i rig sngags su/ rgol ba'i tshig la nang
'gal mang ba/ gong ma'i gsung la dogs pa dpyad pa/ dngos lan gdab pa 'phros dang bcas pa ste gsum du mdzad cing / dang po la'ang rgol bas dngos brtags ma phye bas sa paN
gyi gsung la nang 'gal bsgrub/ spyi gsal 'dres pas rje btsun gyi gsung la nang 'gal bsgrub/ cal col mang bas klu sgrub sogs rtsa ltung can du bsgrub pa dang gsum du gsungs
nas/ dang po la ljon shing las tshogs 'khor gyi dbye bar bshad pa'i tshogs 'khor yin na/ sa skya pa rang lugs kyi de yin dgos par thal/de las bshad pa'i tshogs 'khor yin
na

sa skya pa rang lugs kyi de yin dgos pa'i phyir/ rtags khyab grub mtha' la song / 'dod na/ chos rjes bshad pa'i dpa' bo'i ston mo chos can/ der thal/ de'i phyir/ 'khor gsum
char la lan med do/ /gzhan yang de chos can/ rnal 'byor pas bya ba'i tshogs 'khor yin par thal/ ljon shing las gsungs pa'i tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid pa yin pa'i phyir/ rtags
khas/ 'dod na ma yin par thal/ rab byung gis bya ba'i dpa' bo'i ston mo yin pa'i phyir/ khyab pa ni rnal 'byor pas bya ba'i tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid pa dang / rab byung
gis bya ba'i rjes mthun pa gnyis so sor phye bas grub gsungs/ gnyis pa la/ rje btsun gyis bshad pa'i dpa' bo'i ston mo de tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid pa yin na/ de dpa' bo
dang dpa' mo gnyis ka tshogs pa'i tshogs 'khor yin par 'dod dgos/ gzhan yang phyogs snga ma ni dus khyad par can la dpa' bo'i ston mo tsam yang mi byed ces pa'i yang sgras
gang 'don smra dgos so gsungs la/ gsum pa la dus khyad par can la rab byung gi tshogs 'khor ma byas na rtsa ltung 'byung ba 'khrul spong gi dgongs pa yin na/ klu sgrub
nas chos rje'i bar thams cad kyis dus khyad par can gyi tshe/ tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid pa dang rjes mthun pa gnyis kyi zlas phye ba'i rjes mthun pa kho na mdzad pas na
thams cad rtsa ltung can du 'gyur zhing / gzhan yang khyod kyis kho bo cag dbang bskur sogs kyi tshe dpa' bo'i ston mo tsam yang mi byed pa nges pa can su las thos/ khyed
ltar du mi byed pa dang / tshogs 'khor mi byed par grags pa tsam la ni nges pa med par

gsungs shing / gnyis pa gong ma'i lung la dogs pa dpyad pa la/ ljon shing las dpa' bo'i ston mo tshogs 'khor gyi dbye ba'i ya gyal du bshad kyang / de yin na dbye gzhi de yin
mi dgos te/ bden gnyis kyi dbye gzhi 'jig rten pa'i blo tsam dang shes bya tsam yin kyang / don dam bden pa de gnyis gang yang ma yin pa bzhin no/ /des na tshogs 'khor
gyi ya gyal du bshad pa thams cad tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid par rje btsun bzhed na/ tshogs 'khor la rnal 'byor pho mo 'tshogs dgos par rje btsun nyid kyis bshad pas nang
'gal bar 'gyur zhing / de gnyis ma 'tshogs na tshim pa drug dngos su byar med pas tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid par mi 'gyur la/ mdor na tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid pa dang rjes
mthun pa ni tshim pa drug dngos su byar yod med kyis phye zhing / de'i phyir las rgya la brten nas rdzogs rim gyi ye shes dngos su bskyed de lus sems lhan skyes kyi bde bas
tshim par nus pa'i rnal 'byor pa kho nas tshogs 'khor bya ba dang / de 'dra'i nus pa med na khyim pa rdor 'dzin yin yang chags pa'i rnam rtog dang bcas pa'i phyir tha
mal pa'i 'dzag bde yin gyi/ 'gyur med kyi bde ba ma yin pas tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid pa byar med pa dang / rab byung rdo rje 'dzin pa ni ji tsam bzang yang bstan pa la gces
spras su bya ba'i phyir spros bcas kyi spyod pa dngos su mi mdzad pa yin no/ 'di la dgongs nas mkhyen rab dbang phyug gis rnal 'byor pas bya ba'i tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid
pa dang / rab byung gis bya ba'i tshogs 'khor rjes mthun pa gnyis

su phye nas gsungs pa dang / Dombhi he ru kas kyang dpa' bo dang bral ba'i dpa' mo dang / dpa' mo dang bral ba'i dpa' bo dag gis tshogs kyi 'khor lo bskor bar mi bya'o zhes
gsungs/ 'khrul spong las tshogs kyi gral du thun mong gi rgyu bzhi gang rung sngon du 'gro bas tshogs rdzas stob pa mi gtsang ba'am/ sdom pa 'og ma'i bcas pa dang 'gal du
dogs nas dang du mi len na rtsa ltung du bshad ces sogs gsungs la/ gsum pa dngos lan gdab pa 'phros dang bcas pa la skabs don dngos lan dpyis phyin pa dang / 'khrul med
kyi lung khungs rgyas par bshad pa gnyis su mdzad nas/ dang po la rje thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyis mdzad pa'i bla chen chos rin dpal ba'i dris lan de nyid kyis 'di'i lan
yang thebs pas zhes gsungs nas/ chen po chos rin gyi dri lan rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang pos mdzad pa de 'god par mdzad la/ gnyis pa la tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid pa rnal
'byor pas bya dgos pa'i lung / rab byung gis de bya mi rung ba'i lung / tshogs rdzas kyi sha chang rgyud sde las bshad pa dgos pa'i lung dang gsum du mdzad nas/ dang po
la/ 'o na tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid pa byed pa la nges par rnal 'byor pa nus pa dang ldan pa dgos par gang nas bshad ce na zhes gsungs nas/ dus 'khor 'grel chen gyi lung
rgyas par 'dren par mdzad do//gnyis pa la sbyangs rtogs sbar gsum nus pa'i rab byung gis tshogs 'khor byas pas skyon med do snyam na zhes gsungs nas bde mchog stod 'grel
gyi lung drangs nas/ des na de lta bu'i nus pa dang ldan pa'i rab

byung gis tshogs 'khor byas na rang nyid la nyes pa mi 'byung yang / gzhan ma dad pa sogs kyis bstan pa la gnod pa spang ba'i phyir dngos su mi mdzad pa yin no/ de ltar na
bza' ba'i dam tshig nyams par 'gyur ro snyam na/ dus khyad par can gyi tshe ni/ chos rje sa paN gyis gsungs pa ltar rjes mthun pa byas pas chog rgyun gyi de la ni bdud rtsi
ril bu bsten pas dgag bya de khegs te zhes gsungs nas 'grel chen de'i lung 'dren par mdzad do/ /gsum pa la spyir rdo rje theg pa'i mchod pa dang tshogs rdzas sogs kyi
sha ni kha na ma tho ba med pa zhig dgos gsungs nas bde mchog stod 'grel dang / dus 'khor 'grel chen dang / gsang 'dus 'grel chen sgron gsal rnams kyi lung 'dren par mdzad
nas/ de bzhin du rnal 'byor pas bsten bya'i chang yang sdom 'byung nas 'byung ba ltar dgos kyi/ ci rung gi chang tshogs rdzas su bshad pa med do/ /de ltar bshad pa'i sha
chang dag kyang dpa' bo'i ston mo sogs kyi tshe lha'i rnal 'byor brtan po dang ldan pas cung zad brten pa yin gyi/ ha cang rgyags pa dang ting nge 'dzin brtan po dang mi
ldan pa'i las dang po pas cho ga shes pa'i rgyu mtshan gyis ci dgar 'jug pa dang / 'dzag bde don gnyer gyis phyag rgya bsten pa bkag gsungs nas/ dus 'khor dang / de'i 'grel
pa dang / slob dpon dznyAn kIrti rnams kyis lung 'dren par mdzad nas/ de bas na gnas skabs su bya ba'i khyad par 'di la snyad btags te bag med par spyod pa dag ni lhag
spyod kyi ting nge 'dzin bsgom pa'i rnam par thar pa dang kun du mtshungs

pa'o zhes gsungs shing / de'i don bsdus don brgyad pa las/ mkhyen rab dbang phyug sa paN gyis/ /bshad pa'i rab byung ston mo des/ /khyad par can gyi bza' ba yi/ /dgag bya de
dag khegs nus sam/ /nus na nged cag sdom brtson rnams/ /chos rjes bshad pa de byed na/ /bza' ba'i dam tshig med pa zhes/ /'brel med smyon de su la smra/ /tshul des dgag
bya mi khegs na/ /klu sgrub nas ni chos rje sogs/ /tshad ldan sdom brtson mtha' yas pa/ /rtsa ltung can du khyed sgrub bam/ /mdor na tshogs 'khor ma byas pa/ /rkyang pas
rtsa ltung 'byung ba de/ /gong ma'i gsung rab gang na bzhugs/ /khyed dag tshogs 'khor byed do zhes/ /kun la rlung ltar sgrog byed na/ /rje btsun gong mas tshogs 'khor la/
/dpa' bo dpa' mo gnyis tshogs dang / /tshim pa drug sogs bshad pa yi/ /mtshan nyid tshang bar khyed byed dam/ /tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid ma tshang na/ /btags pa ba las 'da'
ba med/ /de ltar 'dod na khyed nyid kyis/ /tshogs kyi 'khor lo ma byas phyir/ /rtsa ltung can du khas longs shig /de phyir rang la skyon brjod pa/ /nges par smyon pa
nyid du bas/ /gal te de dag kun byed na/ /phyag na rdo rje'i stod 'grel las/ /chos gos 'dzin pa rnams la ni/ /bla mas tshig gis bstan par bya/ /gzhan du bla ma dam tshig
ni/ /nyams par 'gyur zhes gang gsungs pa'i/ /gzhan gyis ma 'khur sdig pa yi/ /khur de khyed cag 'khor ram ci/ /gzhan yang dus 'khor rgyud 'grel sogs/ /tshad ldan rnams las
rab byung gis/ /de ltar byed pa rgyas par

bkag /chos rjes bshad pa'i ston mo de/ /dpa' bo'i ston mor khas blangs shing / /dpa' bo'i ston mo rje btsun gyis/ /tshogs 'khor dbye bar bshad ces pa/ /gnyis ka cig car khas
blangs nas/ /chos rjes bshad de sa skya pa'i/ /rang lugs min zhes smra byed pa/ /'di yang 'gal ba ltag sprod yin/ /khu dbon gnyis ka bzhed pa de/ /sa skya'i chos su mi
rung na/ /sa skya'i chos kyi mtshan gzhi ni/ /kun mkhyen gyis kyang rnyed mi nus/ /sa paN 'gegs pa'i sa skya pa/ /rnying pa de dag ches cher blun/ /de phyir phyi dro'i kha
zas dang / /sha chang ro la rngams pa yi/ /zol gyis tshogs 'khor byed do zhes/ /'jig rten pa rnams rmongs byed pa'i/ /'dod ldan de dag lhag spyod kyi/ /ting 'dzin bsgom
pa ji bzhin no/ /zhes gsungs so/ /de rnams kyi yang lan du mkhan chen bzang bkras pas snyan brgyud 'khrul sel las/ /'dod lan thebs pa'i thal 'gyur la/ /'khor gsum rigs pa
shes pas khrel/ /pho mo tshogs pa rnams gnyis te/ /gang zag phal la grags pa dang / /rdor sems bsgom pa'i ting 'dzin gyi/ /lha dgu la sogs dkyil 'khor dang / /dpa' bo dpa'
mo rnams kyang yod/ /de ltar min na tshogs 'khor gyi/ /tshim pa lnga yang dka' bar gnas/ /rtsa khams dpa' bo dpa' mo ru/ /gdod nas grub par khyod nyid 'dod/ /gzhan yang
tshogs 'khor rtsod spong las/ /phyi nang mkha' 'gro zhes kyang gsungs/ /rtsa ltung 'byung dang mi 'byung ba/ /klu sgrub la sogs sdom las grol/ /de lta min na de bzhin
byung /

/'on kyang lugs gnyis so sor nges/ /bu ram phyi dro 'dod pa dang / /mi 'dod 'gal ba med pa bzhin/ /gcig tu nges na ha cang thal/ /don dam shes byar khas len pa'i/ /dpe de da
dung bsgrub bya yin/ /zhes dang / 'o na sngon gyi lam 'bras pa/ /kye rdor dbang zhus thams cad la/ /lhan cig skyes pa'i ye shes gang / /dngos su skye bar 'dod dam ci/ /lo
rgyus kun las tshogs 'khor bshad/ /khyad par grub chen buddha shrIs/ tshogs 'khor mdzad pa'i rnam thar ltos/ /rab byung tshogs 'khor mi rung na/ /dge slong dpa' bo rdo
rje de/ /tshogs 'khor gshegs pa'ang mi bden nam/ /'di rnams bod rnams byung rgyal smras/ /tshim pa drug pa'i nyams len dang / /mchog dbang gsum po mtshungs pa'i phyir/ /tshogs
'khor bzhin du de la yang / /dngos btags gnyis su 'byed dgos 'gyur/ /tshogs 'khor dbang bskur gnyis ka la/ /dngos btags 'byed na rtog bzo yin/ /zhes pa dang / 'di
dag gnad kyi snying po'i lan/ /rje yi rtsa ltung 'khrul spong las/ /rab byung phyi dro mi za ba'ang / /bcu gsum pa yi ltung bas 'jig /cung zad 'thung zhing kha zas bsten/
/snod min drung du rab byung la/ /de skad smra na rtsa ltung gsungs/ /tshogs 'khor dus su rab byung gis/ /bslab pas bcings nas chang 'thung dang / /phyi dro'i kha zas bsten
pa yis/ /ltung ba byung dogs ma bsten pa/ /rtsa bar gsungs shing nad pa yis/ /reg pa tsam las mi bsten yang / /nyes med ril bu bsten pa ni/ /'di yi skabs ni min zhes
gsungs/ /gal te gong du bshad pa

ltar/ /bcas 'gal dogs pas rtsa ltung ste/ /bcas 'gal med na'ang bstan pa bsams/ /tshogs 'khor med phyir mi 'gal na/ /'o na de 'dra'i dgos med pa'i/ /rab byung tshogs 'khor
rung bar mthun/ /bstan la phan nam min yang rung / /dgos pa gtso bor rje btsun bzhed/ /chang ni 'o mar bsgyur nus pa/ /tshogs 'khor 'chad dus khyed nyid 'dod/ /'o ma'i ltung
ba'i nyes pa gang / /de la ma dad gang la 'ong / /bstan la'ang gnod par ji ltar 'gyur/ /nad la gnod pa'ang dka' pa yin/ /gzhan gyi rab byung tshogs 'khor dus/ /sha chang
bsten zhes snod min bsgrags/ /rang gis tshogs 'khor ma byas pas/ /khyed la ltung ba gnyis su 'gyur/ /tshogs 'khor ma byas rtsa ltung ste/ /ma bsten pa zhes rtsa ba dang
/ /'grel par dam rdzas mi bsten zhes/ /ma mthong phyogs mthong gzhan la smod/ /rang nyid ngo tsha gzhan gyis khrel/ /'khrul spong don yang dang po yi/ /las can rnams kyis
rung ba ste/ /ljon shing nyid las dam tshig dang / /tshogs 'khor gnas dang gang zag gsum/ /chos rjes tshogs 'khor rtsod spong las/ /gnas dang mdun bskyed tshogs 'khor
dus/ /bzod gsol skabs dang rnam pa bzhir/ /las ni dang po zhes bya ba/ /khu dbon gnyis kyis gsungs pa 'di/ /log rtog brag ri 'joms pa'i thog /tshim pa drug la'ang rnam gnyis
te/ /phyag rgya bsten dang ting 'dzin gnyis/ phyi ma Dombhi he ru kas/ /mar dang mar gyi nying khu yis/ /snying ga ru ni byug par bya/ /ji skad gsungs pa de bzhin

gsungs/ /des na zhib tu ma bltas par/ /rbad gcod sngas na rang nyid 'bebs/ /rigs pa tshogs 'khor mchog dbang mtshungs/ /de phyir rgyu lam mtshan nyid pa/ /rab byung nyams len
mi 'dod dam/ /gal te sha chang dngos su yin/ /mchog dbang ting 'dzin dkyil 'khor phyir/ /mtshungs min snyam na dge slong la/ /sa brko me reg la sogs dang / /dbang dus
gzhu sogs 'gog gam ci/ /dgongs pa gtso phyir de mthong tshe/ /nyes med ces ni rje btsun bzhed/ /ces sogs dang / dus 'khor bde mchog gsal lo zhes/ /snyan brgyud 'gog pa'i
zur za yin/ /zhes sogs rgyas par gsungs la/ sgyi chu ba buddha shrI'i nor bu'i phreng bar/ khyed kyi dbang de dbang mtshan nyid pa yin nam rjes mthun pa yin/ dang po ltar
na rab byung gis dbang mtshan nyid pa byar mi rung ste/ dbang mtshan nyid pa dang rje mthun par 'jog pa ni las rgya'am tshim pa drug pa dngos su byar yod med kyis phye ba
yin zhes sogs tshangs pa'i rigs sngags su gsungs pa de dbang la sbyar nas gsungs te da ci gsungs/ /tshim pa drug pa'i thad kyis bshad pa dang / dbang gong ma'i thad kyis
bshad pa rnams ci'i phyir mi mtshungs/ yang na dbang mtshan nyid pa med par khas longs shig dbang la de gnyis kyi tha snyad gong mas ma bshad snyam na/ tshogs 'khor la
de 'dra'i tha snyad gang du bshad smros shig da lta de 'dra'i dbang mdzad pa med kyang ye shes kyi phyag rgya la brten pas go chod do zhe na/ tshogs 'khor la ci phyir mi
mtshungs/ gzhan yang rdzogs rim gyi ye shes dngos su rtogs pa

'phags pa kho na la yod pas/ 'jig rten pa'i lam du dbang dang tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid pa med par khyod khas longs shig yang khyod nyams su len pa'i lam de lam mtshan nyid
pa dang rjes mthun pa gang yin sogs gong ltar sbyar na'ang mtshungs so/ /gal te phyag rgya la brten pa mtshungs na'ang sha chang sogs rab byung gi spang bya yin pas mi rung
snyam na/ 'o na mda' gzhu dang ral gri sogs rab byung gis spang bya yin pas dbang rdzas su mi rung bar rnam pa kun du mtshungs so zhes sogs dang / yang rje rdo rje 'chang
gis chen po chos rin gyi dri lan tshangs pa'i rigs sngags su bkod pa las/ gnyis pa ltar na rang rgyud la ye shes rgyas pa'i thabs su tshogs 'khor lkog tu bya ba dang
/ gdul bya gzhan ma dad pa bzlog pa'i phyir dngos su byed pa gnyis las ma 'das zhes gsungs pa la/ de ni ma brtags pa de/ 'chi ba'i tshe'am mu ge'am zhes sogs ma mthong bar
zad do zhes dang / yang tshangs pa'i rigs sngags su klu sgrub sogs rtsa ltung can du thal ba'i lan du/ 'khrul spong gi ltung ba'i ngo bo nyid rnam par gzhag pa ni zhes
sogs drangs nas/ de ltar gsungs na khyod kyis klu sgrub sogs rtsa ltung can du sgrubs shig yang na lung de chos rje pas ma gzigs pa'am zhal gyis mi bzhes pa'am/ rnal 'byor
dbang phyug gi man ngag min par khas longs shig gsungs/ yang tshangs pa'i rigs sngags su tshogs 'khor rnal 'byor pas bya dgos pa'i lung zhes sogs kyi lan du/ lung khungs
de khyed rang gis drangs pa bzhin bshad na/ lung dang po'i

don 'dir zhes pa rdo rje theg pa'i dkyil 'khor zhes ston/ byis pa rnams kyis zhes pa so skye ste spyir bstan/ 'o na skye bo kun gyis rung ngam snyam na dbang thob cing dam
tshig dang ldan pa'i rnal 'byor pa rnams kyis rung gi de ma yin pa'i tha mal pa rnams kyis ni ma yin no zhes ston gyis/ mdor na dbang thob dam ldan gyi lha'i rnal 'byor la
gnas pa zhig gis ji skad bshad pa'i tshogs rdzas bsten rung bar bstan/ gang dag gi sngags kyi stobs kyis sam brtan pa thob pa'i gang zag gis tshogs 'khor bya tshul dang
/ sbyangs rtogs sbar gsum gyi tshul rnams rgyas par bstan no/ /lung phyi ma'i don ni tshogs 'khor gyi tshul rnams gsang zhing sba ba dang / gsang spyod bag yangs su mi 'gyur
ba'i phyir gang thod du bya ba bkag pa yin te/ dge slong rnams la zhes sogs ni dngos su dgongs la/ de min na dge slong sngags kyi rnal 'byor pa mchog tu gsungs pa sogs
mi 'grig pa du ma yod pa'i phyir/ gzhan du dbang bzhi dang lam bzhi sogs nyams len yin pa dgag byar thal/ gsang ba shes rab dbang bskur ni/ /tshangs par spyod pas blang
mi bya/ /zhes sogs gsungs pa'i phyir zhes dang / de'i rjes su des na bshad par bya ste/ rje btsun chen pos/ de las sangs rgyas thob pa'i rgyu/ /bsod nams ye shes tshogs
yin te/ /zhes sogs dang / gzhan tshogs rdzas ngos 'dzin pa'i lung dang / tshogs 'khor gyi phan yon ston pa'i lung sogs kha yar zhig drangs pa'i mthar zhes rab tu myos pa'i
chang mi btung / chags sdang gi gtam mi bya/ kha drag dang rtsod pa mi byed ces
