gsungs na sbyangs rtogs sbar gsum nus pa'i rnal 'byor pa la bslab bya de 'dra ci dgos te khyad par gyi dam tshig snub par byed pa'i than skad yin no/ gzhan yang lam 'dir zhugs
pa'i rab byung sogs kyis 'di nas bshad pa'i tshogs 'khor bya rung ste/ 'di nas gsungs pa'i rnal 'byor pa yin pa'i phyir zhes sogs rgyas par gsungs pa yin no/ /de ltar
na ngor rdzong gnyis po bza' ba'i dam tshig tshogs 'khor gyi rnam gzhag la brgal lan gyi spros pa so so nas shin tu che yang / don gyi snying po ni rdzong lugs pa dag ljon
shing dang chos rje pa'i tshogs 'khor gyi yi ge gnyis char las tshogs 'khor la dbye sgo mang du gsungs pa rnams tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid pa rang du bzhed cing / de'i rgyu
mtshan gyis tshogs 'khor la tshim pa drug dngos su med kyang / ye shes kyi phyag rgya'am dpa' mo la brten pas chog cing / tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid pa dang rjes su mthun
pa'i tha snyad rje btsun gong mas bshad pa med/ rab byung gis bya ba'i tshogs 'khor dang rnal 'byor pas bya ba'i tshogs 'khor gnyis su gsungs pa'i dang po de gzhan lugs
dang / sa skya pa rang lugs thun mong ma yin pa ni/ chos rje'i bshad tshul phyi ma rnal 'byor pas bya ba'i tshogs 'khor gyi rnam gzhag 'di yin/ des na ngor lugs ni dus
khyad par can la dpa' bo'i ston mo tsam yang mi byed pas khyad par can gyi bza' ba'i dam tshig med par 'gyur ro zhes gsungs par snang ngo / /ngor lugs pa rnams khu dbon gnyis
kyis tshogs 'khor gyi dbye bar bshad pa de dag ming gi rnam grangs tsam

gyis dbye ba yin pas/ dbye ba'i ya gyal de dag gang rung yin na tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid pa yin mi dgos la/ tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid pa yin na dpa' bo dang dpa' mo gnyis ka
'tshogs dgos shing / de'i gnad kyang tshim pa drug dngos su ldan dgos pa yin cing / des na sdom brtson bslab pas bcings pa dang / khyim pa'ang sbyangs rtogs sbar gsum mi
nus pa rnams kyis tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid pa byar mi rung la/ der ma zad sdom brtson ni nus pa de gsum dang ldan pas rang nyid la nyes pas mi gos kyang gzhan ma dad pa
sogs kyi bstan pa la gnod pa'i nyes pa spang ba'i phyir tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid pa de mi mdzad pa yin par chos rjes bshad la/ 'on kyang dus khyad par can gyi bza' ba'i dam
tshig med par mi 'gyur te/ dpa' bo'i ston mo zhes ming du btags pa'i tshogs 'khor rjes mthun pa de byar rung zhing bya bar yang bshad pa yin zhes par snang la/ de lta
na'ang tshim pa drug dgos pa dang / lus sems lhan skyes kyi bde bas tshim pa zhes pa de la las rgya la brten nas dngos su bya ba dang / ye shes kyi phyag rgya la brten nas
bya ba gnyis su yod pa dang / rnal 'byor pa dang rab byung gi tshogs rdzas la khyad par yod pa sogs ni lugs gnyis ka bzhed pa mthun la/ 'on kyang rdzong lugs pa'i mkhas
pa rnams kyis dbang gsum pa ye shes kyi phyag rgya la brten nas bskur ba de dbang mtshan nyid pa yin pa dper mdzad nas tshogs 'khor gyi tshe'ang rab byung sogs kyis las
rgya la dngos su ma brten par dpa' bo'i ston mo byas pa de'ang tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid par

bzhed cing / tshogs rdzas kyi sha chang sogs la'ang dgag pa byas na rtsa ltung bcu gsum pa 'byung bas bkag cha mi mdzad do/ /de la rang gi blo'i shar tshod ltar na lugs gnyis
char gyi bzhed pa mthun par byung ba de dag ni rje btsun chen po'i ljon shing dang / chos rje sa skya paNDi ta'i tshogs 'khor gyi yi ger bshad pa rnams kyi dgongs pa bla
na med par snang la/ dbang gsum pa dang tshogs 'khor gyi tshim pa drug pa'i skabs phyag rgya la brten tsam zhig mtshungs na'ang / dbang gsum pa la tshim pa drug ces pa'i
tha snyad rje btsun gong ma rnams kyis bshad tshul ji ltar yod/ tshogs 'khor la tshim pa drug dngos gzhi rang du bshad pas rdzong lugs pa'i mkhas pa phyi ma rnams kyis
de gnyis kyi mtshungs pa brjod pa 'di cung zad brtag dgos sam snyam zhing / mdor na sdom brtson rnams kyis khyad par gyi bza' ba'i dam tshig nyams su len pa 'di rdzong lugs
pa ltar tshogs 'khor mtshan nyid pa yin pa'am/ ngor lugs pa ltar rjes mthun pa gang ltar yang / de'i tshe sdom brtson rnams kyis las rgya dngos su bsten pa lta zhog tshogs
rdzas la sha chang sogs rab tu byung ba la spyir bkag pa rnams kyang mi bya ba dang / phyi dro'i zas su gnang ba'i bu ram sogs byed pa'am sha byed kyang bsad sha ma
yin pa dang / chang yang lce la reg pa tsam ma gtogs ha cang mang pa mi bsten no zhes spyod pa dog phyogs kyi mtha' bsdams te bag yod du bya ba nyid shin tu legs pa yin
te/ de las gzhan du gsang spyod 'chol par spyad na 'jig rten tha mal pa dang mu

stegs 'ga' zhig gi spyod pa dang mtshungs par 'gyur ba dang / rab byung gi bslab pa dang 'gal ba'i sha chang bag med bsten pa sogs byas na de la brten nas khyim pa rnams ma
dad pa dang / sngags kyi theg pa la bzhugs pa dag la gzhan gyis brnyas par 'gyur zhing / rgyu de la brten nas sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la gnod par 'gyur bas na tshul de
la nan tan du bya rigs so snyam ste/ don 'di la dgongs te mkhyen rab kyi dbang phyug sa skya paNDi tas tshogs 'khor gyi yo byad la/ rab byung sdom brtson gyi lugs dang /
rnal 'byor pa'i lugs gnyis su gsungs pa dang / dang po de 'chad pa na/ gtor ma la sha chang la sogs pa dbul/ sdom brtson rnams kyis lce la bdud rtsi myang ba tsam bya/ gzhan
bu ram shing tog la sogs pa la bsang ba sogs gtor ma byin rlabs ltar bya/ sha lnga bdud rtsi lngar bsgoms te zos pas rtsa ltung bcu gsum pa'i nyes pa mi 'byung / sangs
rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' dang ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro rnams kyis byin gyis rlabs te/ gsang ba 'dus pa las/ sha rnams thams cad med na yang / /thams cad bsam pas rnam
par brtag /rdo rje sbyor bas zos pa yi/ /sangs rgyas thams cad byin gyis brlabs/ /zhes bya ba dang / sambu Ta las kyang / sha gang yang med na rnam par rtog pas sha'i
rang bzhin du byas la 'jig rten pa gang bza' ba de bza' bar bya'o zhes gsungs pa ltar ro zhes dang / tshul de klu sgrub yab sras/ thogs med sku mched/ jo bo rje/ kha che
paN chen sogs bzhed par bshad pa'i rjes su sdom brtson rnams

kyis dbang bskur ba la sogs pa'i dus su 'di ltar byas na legs so zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /yang ngor lugs bzhed pa'i tshogs 'khor gyi rnam gzhag la/ rdo rje gdan pa chen po kun
dga' rnam rgyal dpal bzang po zhes rdzong lugs pa dag gi bstan 'dzin rnams kyi gtsug rgyan lta bur gyur pa de nyid kyis gzhan lugs kyi tshogs 'khor gyi rnam gzhag dgag
pa dang / rang lugs kyi de'i rnam gzhag legs par bshad pa'i bstan bcos grub pa'i dga' ston zhes bya ba mdzad de/ /de nyid las tshogs 'khor bsten dgos pa/ ma bsten pa'i nyes
dmigs/ bsten tshul dngos dang gsum du mdzad nas/ phyi ma'i skabs su de la log rtog dgag pa sogs don tshan gsum du bshad pa'i dang po la mdor bstan rgyas bshad gnyis su
mdzad pa'i dang po la/ deng sang gi dus 'dir rdo rje slob dpon rdzas la brkam pa dang longs spyod la chags pa 'gas zhes pa nas/ phyogs de la rims nad bzhin du 'dzem par
bya'o zhes pa'i bar gsungs nas ngor lugs la thog mar mdor bstan gyi tshul du dgag pa brjod pa mdzad do/ /de la lan 'debs dngos su mdzad pa po gzhan byung ba ni ma mthong
la/ mkhas pa'i dbang po byams pa rab brtan gyi thugs sras rje bsod nams rab brtan zhes bya bas tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i dgag lan log rtog gi brag ri 'joms pa'i rdo rje zhes
bya ba mdzad la/ de nyid las rdo rje gdan pa chen pos dgag pa'i gsung dang mtshungs pa'i lan yang mdor bstan dang rgyas bshad gnyis kyi sgo nas 'don par mdzad do/ /de'ang
dgag pa mdor

bstan gyi lan du/ 'di dag ni phyogs snga'i nam ma langs par dgag pa'i nyi ma shar ba zhes pa'am/ phyogs snga gzhi med la smyon gtam gsungs pa'i ngal ba 'ba' zhig tu zad de/
'di ltar de nyid du tshogs kyi 'khor lo bsten du rung mi rung so thar gyi gdung ba'i ngos nas 'jog pa bzhin no zhes pa 'di'ang smyon gtam du snang ste/ de ltar khas len
pa po med pa'i phyir/ 'on kyang gang zag gi rigs la ltos nas sdom brtson rdo rje 'dzin pa'i lugs/ de las gzhan pa'i rnal 'byor pa'i lugs gnyis su dbye ba/ rje btsun sa paN
gyis bshad pa ltar nged kyi bla ma rnams kyang bzhed/ de tsam gyis tshogs 'khor thams cad so thar gyi ngos nas bzhag par 'gro na khyed rang yang tshogs 'khor so thar gyi
bslab bya dang bstun nas khas len dgos te/ nyid kyi lung der sa paN gyi gsung dang 'gal spong gi skabs su 'dir ni so thar la bstun pa che chung gi sgo nas bzhag ste zhes
bris pa'i phyir/ gzhan yang rdo rje theg pa yin pas nyan thos kyi bslab pa dang bstun mi dgos na khyed thams cad he ru ka'i cha lugs mi bzung bar rab byung gi cha lugs
bzung nas ci byed ces pa dang / yang rdo rje gdan pas snod kyi skyon yon ma brtags par theg pa ches dman pa'i rigs can la dbang bzhi bskur te zab mo'i gnad rnams bstan pa
las zhes pa'i lan du spyir snod brtag dgos kyang / khyed ltar na gangs khrod kyi skye bo thams cad gsang sngags kyi snod du gzigs par sems te/ gsang sngags thun mong ma
yin pa'i phyag rgya dang gar sogs snod min la gsang dgos pa rnams skye bo thams cad 'dus

par mdzad par snang bas so zhes dang / yang de ni 'dod yon lam du byed pa rdo rje theg pa las 'dod yon spong ba lam du byed pa theg pa gzhan khyad par du 'phags pa yang don
gyis 'dod pas zhes pa'i lan du spyir btang tsam la de ltar 'dod mkhan med/ gang zag gi rigs la ltos nas rdo rje theg pa zab pa'i nges pa med de/ /theg dman gyi rigs can
la de'i chos kho na zab par klu sgrub kyis nad dang sman gyi dpe dang bcas te gsungs la/ de min na sangs rgyas kyis rdo rje theg pa kho na ci'i phyir mi gsung zhes pa'i lan
mdzad cing / yang de lta bu rjes 'brang dang bcas pas lta ba tshogs kyi 'khor lo nyid sngags pa ngan 'gror 'jug pa'i sgor bsam pa ni zhes pa'i lan du/ ngor lugs pas sdom
brtson rnams kyis tshogs 'khor gyi tshe sha chang la longs spyod na ltung bas gos nas ngan song du skye bar bzhed pa la de ltar zer na/ 'o na dbang yang ngan song du skye
ba'i rgyur 'gyur te/ de thob pa'i gang zag rtsa ltung gi dbang gis ngan song du skye ba yod pa'i phyir/ des na tshogs 'khor sogs kyi tshe spyod pa zhib mor byed pa rnams
ltung ba can ltung med du rlom zhing / ltung med ltung ba la sbyor ba'i rgyu yin nam/ sngags la khag btags nas spyod pa 'chol por byed pa rnams rtsing spyod la zhib spyod
du rlom zhing / zhib spyod dang du len pa rnams rtsing spyod la sbyor ba'i rgyu yin/ gzur gnas kyis dpyad 'tshal lo zhes bshad do/ yang rdo rje gdan pa chen po'i grub
pa'i dga' ston las rgyas par dgag pa'i tshe/ 'dir gtso bor dgag bya ni ngor pa'i ngan rtog ste/ 'di bkag

pas gzhan khegs par 'gyur ba dang / sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i dri ma'ang 'byang bar 'gyur bas so zhes sogs kyi dgag yul ngos bzung ste/ de la kun bzang rnam rol las 'byung ba
dgag pa dang / gsang ba kun rgyan las 'byung ba dgag pa gnyis su mdzad nas/ dang po la gong du bkod pa'i kun bzang rnam rol las bshad tshul de phyogs sngar bkod nas/ de
skad smra ba po'i don gyi snying po ni spyir 'jig rten pa'i zas la tshogs kyi 'khor lo gdags su mi rung zhing / khyad par sha chang rab tu byung bas tshogs kyi 'khor lo bsten
pa gtan mi rigs zhes par snang ba ches shin tu mi 'thad de zhes sogs mi 'thad pa'i sgrub byed dang bcas dgag pa'i rnam grangs shin tu rgyas par 'byung ba'i lan du/ chos
rje bsod nams rab brtan gyis lan 'debs rigs pa'i rnam grangs mang po dang bcas gsungs kyang / dngos lan snying po blangs te bkod na kun gyis rtogs sla bar 'gyur bas lan
rgyas bshad rnams kyi snying po ni/ dgag pa de dag ni phyogs snga ma longs par mdzad par song ste/ 'jig rten pa'i dga' ston dang kha zas yin na tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i rgyur
mi rung bas khyab pa dang / sha chang rab byung gi tshogs 'khor gyi dus su gtan nas bsten mi rigs par 'dod pa med bzhin du dgag pa mdzad pas so/ /kun bzang rnam rol
las sha chang kho na la longs spyod pa 'jig rten pa'i dga' ston la tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i ming gdags par mi bya'o zhes pa'i don ni/ thar pa don gnyer rnams kyis sha chang
kho na la longs spyod pa 'jig rten pa'i dga' ston dang tshul mtshungs pa'i longs spyod la

tshogs 'khor gyi ming btags nas bag med du longs spyad par mi bya zhes pa'i don yin la/ yang rab byung gis tshogs 'khor gyi tshe sha chang gtan nas bsten mi rung ba'ang gsang
ba kun rgyan gyi dgongs pa ma yin te/ ting nge 'dzin la brtan pa thob pa'i sdom brtson rnams kyis tshogs 'khor gyi tshe sha chang sogs khyim pa rdor 'dzin rnams dang khyad
med du longs spyad kyang dran shes nyams pa sogs kyi nyes par mi 'gyur yang / gzhan ma dad pa sogs kyi rgyur song dogs nas cung zad tsam longs spyod cing / de min pa'i
sdom brtson rnams kyis ni dam rdzas ma bsten pa'i nyes pa spang ba'i phyir sha chang sogs cung zad bsten par gsungs shing / mang du bsten par ma gsungs pa'i phyir/ gal
te 'dul ba dang bstun na cung zad tsam re'ang bsten du mi rung / tshogs 'khor gyi tshe tshim par longs spyod ces gsungs pas de dang 'gal lo snyam na/ lha mchod pa'i bsam
pas cung zad re bsten pas bcas 'gal gyi nyes pa'ang mi 'byung / dam rdzas ma bsten pa'i nyes par yang mi 'gyur bar rje btsun khu dbon gyis/ sdom brtson rnams la cung zad
tsam/ /zhes dang / bag tsam zhes dang / bdud rtsi myang ba tsam zhes dang / rab tu byung ba la tshogs kyi 'khor lo la sogs pa dgos pa rgya chen po mthong ba'i tshe ni phyi
dro'i kha zas kyi nyes pa med la zhes sogs kyi dmigs bsal gsungs pa yin cing / tshim par longs spyod ces pa'ang rang nyid lhar gsal ba lus dkyil gyi lha dang bcas pa thams
cad mnyes shing tshim par bsam pa'i don yin

gyis/ khams kyis 'chun tshad longs spyod pa'i don min la/ des na rje btsun gong ma rnams kyis tshogs 'khor lugs gnyis gsungs pa yang ting nge 'dzin mi brtan pa'i sdom brtson
la sha chang sogs mang po bsten na bcas 'gal gyi nyes pa dang / de brtan pa rnams la gzhan ma dad pa sogs kyi nyes par 'gyur du dogs pa'i rgyu mtshan gyis yin no/ /de'i
rjes su 'brangs nas thar 'dod rnams la blang dor gyi gnas tshul bzhin ston pa'i bshes gnyen la phrag dog sogs kyis skur 'debs mi rigs zhes pa'i lan 'debs mdzad do/ /yang
grub pa'i dga' ston du tshogs 'khor gyi tshe sha chang bkag pa la legs par brtags na rtsa ltung du mi 'gyur ba med do zhes sogs rtsa ltung dang po nas bcu bzhi pa'i bar
thams cad rje ngor chen nyid la byung bar bshad pa'i lan du/ rje bsod nams rab brtan gyis 'di dag ni rang kho na mchog dang / gzhan nyes can du kun gyis mthong na snyam pa'i
rang 'dod khong tshang du snang bas dgag bsgrub kyis ga la lang / 'on kyang de ltar smra ba po rang nyan thos ltar na gzhan la skur 'debs kyi lhag ma dang / rdo rje theg
pa ltar na rtsa ltung bzhi pas gos par song ste/ de bas rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan zhabs yang dag pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen du byed na smra ngan 'di'i
'gro ba ni cir 'gyur/ gzhan du dam tshig las nyams na/ /nyams pa bdud kyis bzung bar 'gyur/ /de bas sdug bsngal myong 'gyur te/ /thur du bltas te dmyal bar 'gro/ /zhes pa'i
don rtogs par bya'o zhes pa nas/ nyes pa 'di rnams byas pa'i rjes la ni dbang yang gzhan

la ma zhus pas khron par ltung ba'i rdo ba bzhin du rig par bya zhing zhes sogs kyi bar bris pa'i sgo nas gzhan ngan song du skyes nas sdug bsngal myong ba la dga' ba bsgom
zhing yid smon btab pas byams pa'i sems spang bar 'gyur ba'i phyir zhes bshad cing / yang grub pa'i dga' ston las dbang gsum pa'i skabs su dge slong rdo rje 'dzin pas chags
pa'i gtam smras pas lhag ma'i ltung bar 'gyur ba dang / dam bzhag sogs kyi skabs su khyod kyi rdo rje 'chang nga yin gyi zhes sogs la 'pham par 'gyur dgos na tshogs 'khor
las 'jigs pa dbang bskur ba yang 'gegs dgos so zhes sogs gsungs pa'i lan du/ rje bsod nams rab brtan gyis/ 'khrig tshig smra ba'i lhag mar 'gyur ba la chags sems kyis
kun nas bslangs pa zhig dgos la/ dbang gsum pa'i skabs su de ltar smra ba ni dbang gi ye shes ngos zin pa'i ched yin pas mi mtshungs so/ gal te tshogs 'khor gyi tshe'ang
sha chang sogs la sred pa'i sgo nas ma yin par lha mchod pa'i bsam pas tshogs rdzogs pa'i ched yin pas mtshungs so zhe na/ tshogs 'khor gyi tshe dge slong rdo rje 'dzin
pas sha chang cung zad bsten pa ni nged kyang 'dod la/ mang du longs spyod na dran pa nyams nas bag med kyi spyod pa dang / gzhan ma dad pa sogs su 'gyur dogs nas mang du
longs spyod pa de bkag pa yin la/ dbang gsum pa'i tshe chags pa'i gtam smra ba tsam gyis dran shes nyams nas bag med kyi spyod pa dang / gzhan ma dad pa sogs su mi 'gyur
ba'i phyir/ dam bzhag gi tshe'ang de

ltar smras pas brdzun smra ba'i pham par mi 'gyur te/ nyan thos kyi lugs la der 'gyur ba la dran shes bzhin gyis zin pa zhig dgos shing / rdo rje theg pa'i skabs su rang nyid
sangs rgyas su bskyed cing sangs rgyas su gsal ba'i sgo nas de ltar smra ba la pham par ga la 'gyur zhes gsungs so/ /yang rdo rje gdan pa chen po'i grub pa'i dga' ston
las gsang ba kun rgyan las 'byung ba 'gog pa'i tshe/ thog mar 'dir rab tu byung ba sdom brtson rnams kyis tshogs 'khor byed na zhes sogs gsang ba kun rgyan las 'byung tshul
gong du bkod pa de rnams phyogs sngar bshad nas/ de dgag pa ni skyes bu gang dag gzhan la zhe sdang bzhin du chang gis myos na smra ba thams cad la go rim med cing rang
gi phyogs blos btang nas ldab ldib tu smra bar byed pa ltar/ khyod kyang bla brang gi chags sdang gis snyigs dus kyi thub pa rdo rje 'chang theg chen chos kyi rgyal po
la zhe sdang bzhin du mi shes pas myos te lung rigs dang bral zhing / rdo rje theg pa'i nyams len thams cad blos btang nas ngan g.yo'i rtsom pa 'ba' zhig byed par zad mod/
rigs pa dang 'gal ba ni ci dge slong rdo rje 'dzin pas sngags kyi nyams len byed pa ni gang 'dul ba dang mi mthun pa de'i tshe sngags gtso che ba zhig gam/ 'dul ba gtso
che ba zhig dang po ltar na tshogs 'khor gyi tshe 'dul ba dang ma mthun ces sun dbyung du ci yod/ phyi ma ltar na dge slong rdor 'dzin gyis 'dod yon bsten byar mi byed
par thal/ theg pa thun mong bas 'dod yon spong ba gang zhig gong ma las 'og ma gtso che ba'i phyir/ phyi ma khas/ 'dod na

dge slong rdo rje 'dzin pa sngags pa ma yin par thal/ 'dod pa'i phyir/ khyab ste/ 'dod yon bsten pa theg pa'i chos nyid kyis thob pa'i sngags pa'i dam tshig yin pa dang / mdo
sngags kyi dbye ba'ang 'dis 'byed par dpal sa skya pa yab sras bzhed pa'i phyir/ de'ang 'dod na/ dge slong rdor 'dzin dge slong rdor 'dzin ma yin par thal/ de sngags pa
ma yin pa'i phyir/ 'dod na dge slong rdor 'dzin dge tshul dge bsnyen gsum gyi rdo rje 'dzin pa go rim bzhin rab 'bring tha gsum ma yin par thal/ dge slong rdor 'dzin med
pa'i phyir/ gzhan yang dge slong rdo rje 'dzin pas gsang sngags mi spyod par thal/ des gsang ste spyod dgos pa med pa'i phyir/ der thal/ 'dul ba ji lta ba bzhin spyod pa'i
phyir/ 'dis mtshon nas rigs pa grangs med pa 'gro ste/ rigs pa shes pa rnams kyis spros te dgag par bya'o zhes gsungs/ de'i lan du rje bsod nams rab brtan gyis dgag lan
las/ 'o na khyed rang dge slong rdo rje 'dzin pas sngags kyi nyams len byed pa na de ltar gang gtso/ dang po ltar na des sngags kyi nyams len byed pa'i tshe 'dul ba nas
bshad pa'i bslab bya srung sdom mi dgos par thal/ de'i tshe sngags gtso che ba'i phyir/ khyab pa khas/ 'dod na dge slong rdor 'dzin gyis rgyun du de ltar mi dgos par thal/
'dod pa gang zhig des rgyun du sngags kyi nyams len byed dgos pa'i phyir/ gzhan yang / phyi ru nyan thos spyod pa bsrung / /zhes pa dang / nyan thos spyod pa srung ba
po/ /zhes pa rnams kyang sngags kyi nyams len

byed pa po ma yin par 'gyur zhing / yang na nyan thos kyi spyod pa srung ba po ma yin par 'gyur ro/ /gzhan yang 'dul ba pa rnams kyis gsang ste spyod dgos pa med par thal/
des 'dul ba ji lta ba bzhin spyod pa'i phyir/ khyab pa khas/ 'dod mi nus te/ des gsang ste bar chad dri ba sogs spyod dgos pa yin pa'i phyir/ des na khyab pa 'di 'dra'i rigs
pa grangs med byas kyang mkhas pa rnams bzhad mo grangs med 'chor ba'i rgyur zad do/ rigs pa shes pa rnams kyis spros te dgag par bya'o zhes pa ni/ rigs pa shes pas 'di
'dra ba'i khyab pa mi 'cha' las che'o legs par dgongs 'tshal lo zhes gsungs so/ yang grub pa'i dga' ston du gzhan smras pa de dag ni phal cher skyon dang bcas pa ste/
rab byung gi tshogs 'khor bshad pa'i rjes su rnal 'byor pa rnams kyis kyang zhes pa de ltar na/ rnal 'byor pa yin na khyim pa yin dgos pa dang / rab byung yin pa rnal 'byor
pa ma yin dgos pa'i tha chad pa yin no zhes pa'i lan du/ rab byung dang rnal 'byor pa'i tshogs 'khor so sor bshad pa tsam gyis rab byung yin na rnal 'byor pa min dgos
zhes par mi 'gyur/ gal te 'gyur na rje btsun sa paN la ji ltar bya/ mi mtshungs te khyed kyi rab byung mchog dang / rnal 'byor pa khyim pa'am dman par bzung bas nongs la/
sa paN gyis ni so thar la bstun pa che chung gi sgo nas bzhag ste/ don la khyod dang dman mchog go log pas so zhe na/ nged kyi rnal 'byor pa yin na rab byung las dman pas
khyab pa dang / khyim pa yin pas khyab pa khas ma blangs shing / dman mchog

go log ces pa'ang rab byung yin na rnal 'byor pa las dman pas khyab pa la zer na/ shAkya thub pa rab byung min pa'am rnal 'byor pa las dman pa gang rung las ma 'das shing /
rgyud las/ rten ni gsum las dge slong mchog /'bring ni dge tshul yin par 'dod/ /khyim na gnas pa tha ma 'o/ /zhes sogs ma mthong bar zad do zhes gsungs so/ /yang rdo rje
gdan pa chen po'i grub pa'i dga' ston las rgya la sha chang dben par bsten pa gzhan gyis thos na ma dad kyis dogs na/ bsten dus mi bsten pa'i nyes par byed pa ni/ dam tshig
gi rdzas rnams ma bsten na rdo rje mkha' 'gro rnams mi mnyes par byed pa'o zhes rje btsun gyis gsungs pas/ mkha' 'gro ma ma mnyes pa dang 'jig rten pa ma dad pa gnyis
gang nyes pa che soms shig ces gsungs pa'i lan du/ chos rje bsod nams rab brtan gyi gsung de las khyed rang gi rtsod spong gi skabs su bshang gci sogs ni bdud rtsir mi nus
bzhin du zos na 'jig rten pas dmod par 'gyur zhing zhes sogs bris pa la'ang mtshungs te/ bshang gci sogs zos pa la 'jig rten pa ma dad pa dang / mkha' 'gro ma ma mnyes
pa gang nyes pa che soms shig ces gsungs/ yang grub pa'i dga' ston las dus 'khor dang 'gal ba'i rtsod spong gi tshe/ 'dir phyogs snga smra ba po la ni mang du smra ci dgos/
dus 'khor gyi chos skad rnams dang rgyud sde gzhan rnams mi mthun pa mang bas lugs phan tshun mi bsre bar chos skad rang rkang tshugs pa 'dod dgos so zhes smras na ci
zhig smra yongs zhes pa'i lan

du/ dgag lan der dus 'khor rang rkang gi nyams len byed pa'i gang zag des bla med spyi nas bshad pa'i rtsa ltung bcu gsum pa bsrung mi dgos par thal/ bla med spyi la tshogs
'khor gyi tshe sha chang ma bsten na rtsa ltung bcu gsum pa 'byung ba gang zhig des dus 'khor nas gsungs pa'i sha chang ma bsten pa'i tshogs 'khor byas pas de mtshan nyid
par 'gyur ba'i phyir/ rtags gnyis char khas/ 'dod na/ bla med kyi dkyil 'khor re re la bsrung bya rtsa ltung mi 'dra ba re re yod par 'gyur zhing / de 'dod na dus 'khor
gyi dkyil 'khor du thob pa'i sngags sdom la rtsa ltung gis ma gos la/ kye rdor gyi dkyil 'khor du thob pa'i sngags sdom la rtsa ltung gis gos pa'i gang zag yod dgos/ de'ang
'dod na rtsa ltung gis gos pa dang / des ma gos pa'i sngags sdom dang ldan pa'i gang zag yod pa 'dod dgos 'byung zhing / gzhan yang dus 'khor dang kye rdor gnyis char
gyi dbang thob pa'i rdor 'dzin des tshogs 'khor bya mi rung bar thal/ des sha chang la brten pa'i kye rdor sogs bla med spyi lugs kyi tshogs 'khor byas na dus 'khor dang
'gal/ sha chang med pa'i dus 'khor lugs kyi tshogs 'khor byas na bla med spyi dang 'gal bar 'gyur bas so zhes gsungs so/ /yang grub pa'i dga' ston du sa paN dang 'gal spong
gi skabs su khyed kyis rab byung mchog dang / rnal 'byor pa khyim pa'am dman par bzung bas nongs la zhes sogs kyi lan la/ rje bsod nams rab brtan gyis sngar gyi de 'dra
ba zhig gi lan 'debs gsungs shing / mdor na dkar po rnam gsum dang mi mthun

pa ni nyan thos la rtsod spong mdzad pas kyang shes te/ khyed ltar na nyan thos kyi rtsod spong don med pas so zhes gsungs pa'i lan du/ nyan thos kyi bslab ldan thams cad 'di'i
rtsod spong gi yul du bzung bas nyes te/ nyan thos lugs kyi bslab pa dang ldan cing bla med kyi rgyud smin pa'i dge slong rdor 'dzin med par thal/ nyan thos lugs kyi
bslab ldan yin na 'di'i rtsod spong gi yul yin dgos/ bla med kyi rdor 'dzin yin na de ma yin dgos pa'i phyir/ rtags dang po ni dkar po rnam gsum dang mi mthun pa ni zhes
sogs kyi rnam dpyad las khyed rang gis khas blangs/ des na nyan thos kyi sgra 'jug pa tsam la nyan thos kyi grub mtha' rang lugs su smra ba nyan thos sde gnyis lta bu dang
/ nyan thos kyi lta spyod dang ldan pa nyan thos rang rgyud pa gnyis las sa paN gyis tshogs 'khor rtsod spong mdzad pa'i yul ni snga ma rnams so/ nyan thos kyi bslab pa
dang ldan pa la 'di'i rtsod spong gi yul dang / de min pa gnyis su yod ces gsungs so/ /yang grub pa'i dka' ston du/ 'on te chos rjes rab tu byung ba sdom brtson gyi lugs
ni zhes sogs gsungs pa ci zhe na/ de ni rab byung dman pa rnams la thabs mkhas gsungs pa yin gyi/ des mchog la gzhan mi 'gegs pa ni zhes sogs kyi lan du/ rje bsod nams
rab brtan gyis 'di'i rab byung dman pa de rdo rje theg pa'i sgor ma zhugs pa'i rab byung la bya'am/ der bzhugs kyang rim gnyis mi brtan pa'i rab byung la bya/ dang po ltar
na dpyod mi dgos/ gnyis pa ltar na nged dang mthun te deng sang tshogs

'khor byed pa phal cher rim gnyis kyi ting nge 'dzin la brtan pa ma thob pa shas che ba'i phyir/ 'di la dgongs nas rje btsun sa paN dang kho bo cag gi yongs 'dzin gong ma rnams
kyis tshogs 'khor lugs gnyis gsungs pa yid ches pa'i gnas su gyis shig ting nge 'dzin la brtan pa thob pa'i tshogs 'khor la dgag bsgrub mi dgos te/ de dag gi mdzad pa
thams cad sa lam gyi grogs kho nar 'gyur ba'i phyir zhes bshad la/ yang grub pa'i dga' ston las gal te sa paN gyis klu sgrub yab sras/ thogs med sku mched/ jo bo rje dang
/ kho bo'i mkhan po bsod snyoms pa chen po la sogs pa rnams kyis tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i lugs 'di yin no/ /sdom brtson rnams dbang bskur ba la sogs pa'i dus su 'di ltar
byas na legs so zhes gsungs pas 'grub snyam na/ jo bo dang mkhan po sogs kyis bod rnams snod min du dogs nas mdzad pa yin gyi/ de rang lugs su ma nges zhes pa'i lan du/ rje
bsod nams rab brtan gyis 'di'ang 'brel med bzhad gad kyi gnas te jo bo dang mkhan pos de ltar yin zer na'ang / klu sgrub dang thogs med sogs kyis bod rnams snod min du
dogs nas rgya gar du de ltar mdzad ces pa la 'brel med pas so/ /gzhan yang jo bo sogs kyis bod rnams snod min du dogs nas tshogs 'khor de ltar mdzad pa la/ khyed kyis bod
rnams snod ldan du dgongs nas sha chang gtso bor bsten pa'i tshogs 'khor byed pa 'gal lo/ /gal te sa paN gyis sdom brtson gyi lugs bshad pa de brtan pa ma thob pa'i dbang
du byas pa yin na klu sgrub sogs der

'gyur ro zhe na/ de dag ni rang nyes pas gos dogs kyis tshogs 'khor de ltar mdzad pa ma yin gyi/ rjes 'jug brtan pa ma thob pa dag gis gsang sngags la khag btags nas rtsing
spyod dang du blangs na bstan pa dang rang gzhan la gnod par 'gyur bas de dgag pa'i phyir yin te/ dper na ston pas thun mong ma yin pa'i gdul bya la kha sbyor yan lag bdun
ldan gyi skur bstan nas/ thun mong ba la tshangs par spyod pa'i skur bstan pa bzhin no zhes sogs gsungs so/ yang grub pa'i dga' ston las sa paN gyis tshogs 'khor rnam
gzhag las rnal 'byor pa'i tshogs 'khor gsungs pa nas chos kyi rgyal po dpal ldan sa skya pa'i phyag len gyi rim pa bshad zin to zhes gsungs la/ snga phyi gnyis mi mthun na
phyi ma rang lugs su mdzad ces gsungs pa'i lan du/ chos rje bsod nams rab brtan gyis de la brtags na sa paN gyis tshogs 'khor la sdom brtson gyi lugs dang / rnal 'byor
pa'i lugs gnyis su gsungs pa'i phyi ma sa lugs dang mi mthun zhes par song 'dug pa/ de ltar na sa skya pa'i tshogs 'khor de klu sgrub sogs nas kha che paN chen gyi bar sogs
rgya gar gyi paN grub rnams dang mi mthun par smra ba ni ya nga ba'i gtam mo/ /lugs gnyis mi mthun zhes pa'ang gang zag gcig la ltos pa'i phyag len mi mthun pa ma yin
gyis gang zag so so la ltos nas mi mthun pa ste sdom brtson rdor 'dzin rnams kyis lugs snga ma ltar bya/ de las gzhan pa'i rdor 'dzin rnams kyis phyi ma ltar bya'o/ /de gnyis
char yang sa skya pa'i phyag len rnam par dag

pa'o zhes kho bo cag smra'o zhes sogs gsungs pa'i rjes su/ mdor na tshogs 'khor gyi rnam gzhag grub pa'i dga' ston las dgag pa'i ngal ba mang du gsungs ba de thams cad tshig
zin tsam la/ bdag cag rnams kyi 'dren pa kun dga'i mtshan can gyis gnang ba'i tshogs 'khor gyi rnam gzhag gsang ba kun rgyan dang / kun bzang rnam rol gnyis la dgag pa
brjod nas/ don la rje btsun sa paN gyis tshogs 'khor rnam gzhag tu rab byung sdom brtson gyi lugs gsungs pa de bkag par snang ste/ de'ang yid ches pa'i phyir du sa paN gyi
gsung bkod pa na ི zhes gsungs nas/ chos rje'i tshogs 'khor las sdom brtson gyi lugs gsungs pa de 'dren par mdzad do/ de dag ni ngor rdzong lugs gnyis kyi bzhed pa rags
pa tsam bkod pa yin pas skal bzang rnam dpyod dang ldan pa dag gis rje btsun khu dbon gnyis kyi tshogs 'khor gyi rnam gzhag dang / rje rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang pos
mdzad pa'i tshogs 'khor gyi rnam gzhag ston pa'i gsung rab gnyis/ rdo rje gdan pa chen po'i tshogs 'khor gyi rnam bshad grub pa'i dga' ston/ rje bsod nams rab brtan gyis
mdzad pa'i tshogs 'khor gyi rtsod spong log rtog gi brag ri 'joms pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba rnams la yang nas yang du lta rtog gyis la legs bshad kyi dga' ston slar yang spel
bar mdzad du gsol/de ltar grub pa'i dga' ston dang / de nyid kyi rtsod spong log rtog gi brag ri 'joms pa'i rdo rje gnyis kyi rtsod pa dang rtsod lan rnams kyi don so
so la dpyad rgyu 'ga' re snang yang yi ges 'jigs nas 'dir ma bris

la/ gzhan phal cher gsung rab kyi don la zhugs shing dgag bsgrub kyi sgo nas blang dor gyi gnad phyin ci ma log par ston pa'i legs bshad bla na ma mchis par snang mod/ 'on
kyang grub pa'i dga' ston du/ de bas rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan zhabs yang dag pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen du byed na smra ngan 'di'i 'gro ba cir 'gyur zhes
sogs dang / rje rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po la rtsa ba'i ltung ba bcu bzhi po thams cad byung ba dang / de la brten nas ngan song du skye bar 'gyur tshul gsungs pa
rnams ni ha cang rtsub mo'i gsung du snang bas/ rje btsun rdo rje gdan pa chen po rang nyid bslab pa dang dbang las rnam par grol nas nyes par mi 'gyur ba zhig yin na'ang
/ rjes 'jug mi shes pa dag gis 'di tsam gyi gsung la brten nas skyes bu dam pa la log lta dang skur 'debs kyis sdig gsog gi rgyur song dogs pa dang / de bzhin du rje bsod
nams rab brtan gyis rdo rje gdan pa'i gsung de'i lan du/ de ltar smra ba po rang nyid la nyan thos kyi bslab pa la ltos na dge 'dun lhag ma'i ltung ba dang / rdo rje theg
pa la ltos na rtsa ltung bzhi pa 'byung bar gsal te zhes sogs gsungs pa'ang 'jig rten ngan pa'i kha skad ltar du snang bas/ rang re rjes 'jug so skye rnams kyis grub mtha'i
rnam gzhag la bzhed pa 'thad mi 'thad kyi lung rigs kyi dpyad pa mdzad pa ni/ bstan pa la phan pa'i yan lag tu 'gyur zhing / de las gzhan skyes bu dam pa la ngan smra
dang sgro skur sogs kyi grub mtha'i bstan pa 'dzin mi nus pas mkhas pas spang bar bya

ste/ bdag nyid chen po sa skya paNDi tas/ des na mkhas pas grub mtha'i skyon/ /gzu bor brjod pas tshar gcod kyi/ /gang zag skyon dang bdag bstod pa/ /ngan 'gro'i rgyu phyir
mkhas pas smad/ /ces dang / chos dang mi mthun pa'i rtsod pa ngan 'gro'i rgyu yin pas mkhas pa rnams kyis spangs bar bya'o zhes sogs rgyas par gsungs pas so// //dgu pa gdan
gyi dag pa sogs gong ma'i bka' yin min gyi rnam gzhag la/ rje mus srad pa chen pos gong ma'i bka' bsgrub pa/ 'phags pa bsgrub pa/ bla ma dam pa bsgrub pa/ phyag len bsgrub
pa ste bzhi po la le'u re rer mdzad nas bsgrub pa rnam bzhi'i bstan bcos zhes mtshan du grags pa'i/ dang po gong ma'i bka' bsgrub pa zhes bya ba de nyid las/ sa chen
gyi bka' bsgrub pa/ rtse mo'i bka' bsgrub pa/ rje btsun gyi bka' bsgrub pa/ sa paN gyi bka' bsgrub pa dang bzhir mdzad nas/ dang po la rjes 'brangs kha cig rang gis bzhag
pa'i kyai rdo rje'i gzhung lugs dang / gzhung 'di 'gal bar mthong ste/ hwa shang gis dgongs pa nges 'grel gyi mdo bltas pa ltar rnam par dag pa ma yin par smra'o zhes
phyogs snga bkod nas/ de ni mi 'thad de/ dkar shAkya grags kyis mdzad pa'i dag ldan dang / 'phags pa rin po ches zhabs mdun ma gnyis g.yas brkyang zhing g.yon bskum pa zhes
gsungs pa dang / deng sang yan gyi sa skya pa rjes 'brangs dang bcas pa'i kye rdor man ngag lugs kyi bris sku dang bzhengs sku sogs mthong ba kun 'dir bshad pa'i gzhug
tshul kho na ltar snang bas de dag kun kyang yi ge 'di tshad mar

byed pa grub pa'i phyir dang / khyad par khyed rang gi bla ma shar chen gyis gur gyi sgrub thabs su'ang bzhugs tshul 'di kho na ltar bshad pa dang / grub chen buddha shrI'i
thugs dam ras bris la'ang 'di bzhin du yod par grags pas de dag kyang tshad mar mdzad pa gsal bas/ gang zag de tsam gyis tshad mar mdzad pas tshad mar mi 'gyur na ha cang
thal ba'i phyir ro zhes pa dang / rjes 'brangs kha cig slob dpon rin po che'i mtsho skyes kyi 'grel par de dag kyang mnyam par brtsegs pa'i snying gar zhabs g.yas pa gnyis
kyis mnan pa'o/ /rol mo'i tshul ni skyil krung phyed pa'o zhes dang / mtsho skyes dbang chog tu bdud bzhi brtsegs pa'i gdan la zhabs g.yas gnyis brkyang / g.yon gnyis
bskum pa'i gar stabs kyis bzhugs pa zhes gsungs pas/ bzhugs tshul 'di dang mi mthun pa'i phyir rnam par ma dag go zhes smra bar grag go zhes man ngag gi gsal byed las bshad
pa de phyogs sngar 'god par mdzad nas/ de ni lugs so sor ma phyed pa'i bab col yin te lugs de dag mtsho skyes kyi dgongs 'grel yin pa'i phyir zhes sogs dang / rin chen
'bar bar g.yas brkyang g.yon bskum lhag ma gar gyi tshul du bzhugs pa'i don yang / mdun ma gnyis g.yas pa'i brla la g.yon bskum ba'i sor mo sbyar ba dang / lhag ma rgyab
ma gnyis mdun ma lta bu'i gar stabs so zhes 'bru gnon du rung na slob dpon thams cad dgongs pa gcig par 'gyur ba'i shin tu legs kyi gzhan du na slob dpon 'di gnyis mi mkhas
par 'gyur ba'i skyon yod de rgyud dang

mi mthun pa'i phyir ro zhes 'byung bas bzhugs tshul mthun par sbyor bas skyon med do zhe na shin tu mi 'thad de/ mdun rgyab gnyis bzhugs stabs mthun pa la dum bur byas nas
tshig gis bstan pa la dgos pa ci zhig yod/ gzhan dag 'gog pa'i zol gyis rjes btsun gong ma rjes 'brangs dang bcas pa 'gog pa la 'bad par zad pa'i phyir ro zhes sogs gsungs
so/ /de la thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis tshangs pa'i rig sngags kyi don bsdus don brgyad par dbang rdzas yongs dag med pa'i brgal lan las 'phros nas/ tshul
'di bsgrub pa bzhi ldan gyi/ /lan du lung rigs dang bcas 'chad/ /ces gsungs nas sgrub pa bzhi po 'di la lan 'debs shig mdzad par dgongs kyang gsung rtsom gnang thub
pa zhig ma byung snang ba/ 'on kyang bka' bsgrub kyi rje btsun gyi bka' bsgrub pa la rdor dril gyi de nyid ston pa'i yi ge rje btsun gyis mdzad par grags pa de bka' ma yin
pa'i tshul ni tshangs pa'i rigs sngags su gsungs pas gong du bkod pa de dag gis lan dpyis phyin pa thebs pa yin la/ gzhan sgrub pa bzhi po 'di dag la ngor lugs kyi rjes
'brangs dag gis lan 'don mdzad pa'i gsung rab kho bos sngar ma mthong yang / mkhyen rab kyi dbang phyug glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub legs pa'i 'byung gnas kyis
bsgrub pa dang po 'di la lan du 'gyur ba tshig don mun sel zhes bya ba mdzad pa/ de las mus srad pa chen po'i gsung rags pa zhig thog mar bkod nas/ lan dngos la gzhi med
kyi skur ba btab par bstan pa dang / gdan dang

bzhugs tshul la spros pa bcad pa gnyis su mdzad nas/ dang po la rje btsun a nanda bha dra nyid kyis mdzad pa'i gong ma'i bka' 'bum gyi dkar chag na/ sa chen bka' 'bum gyi nang
du kye rdo rje'i gdan gyi dag pa zhes dngos su smos shing / kye rdor rgyud kyi byung tshul las kyang dag ldan las 'byung ba dang / gdan gyi dag pa las 'byung tshul cung
zad mi 'dra ba'i tshig gi khyad par dang bcas lung du drangs la/ ngor chen gyi gsung gang na'ang 'di tshad ldan min par ston pa tshig gcig kyang med/ 'di la mdzad byang
med pas sa chen dang rje btsun gyis bka' 'bum du bsgrigs pa ni ci rigs 'byung ngo / /sa chen gyi gsung rnams mdzad byang med pa shas che zhes rje btsun kun dga' dbang phyug
gsungs pas sa chen gyi bka' 'bum nang du 'jug pa 'thad dam snyam mo/ /yang rje ngor chen gyis kye rdor mngon rtogs bsdus par zhabs mdun ma gnyis g.yas brkyangs g.yon
bskum/ rgyab ma gnyis skyil krung phyed pa'i gar stabs zhes dngos su bshad cing / rje nyid kyi thugs dam bris sku la'ang rtsa ba'i bla ma gnyis kyi sku steng du bkram gdan
gyi tshul bris yod pas/ bkram gdan thams cad ma dag par gsung ngo zhes pa khyod kyis su las thos zhes gsungs la/ gnyis pa gdan dang bzhugs tshul la spros pa bcad pa la/
gdan gyi bdud bzhi ni rgya gzhung dag las mi 'dra ba mang yang rang rang gi bla ma grub thob kyi gsung 'gros yin pas dag ma dag gi dgag sgrub mi nus la/ 'khrul spong gi
mchod brjod las gtso bo'i gdan gsum pa 'jug sel te/ khyab 'jug

la bshad pa'ang yod pas rnam grangs mi 'dra ba cung zad la skyon du gzung bar mi bya'o/ /sa skya pa la kye rdor bka' babs bzhi byung ba'i mtsho skyes dang / man ngag lugs la
zhabs g.yas gnyis brkyangs pa'i brla la g.yon gnyis bskum pa'i sor mo gtad pa'i skyil krung phyed pa'i gar stabs kyis bzhugs pa yin te/ rtse mo'i mtsho skyes dkyil chog
tu de dngos su gsungs shing / mtsho skyes sgrub thabs dang / man ngag lugs kyi yan lag bzhi drug gnyis char du brtsegs gdan gsungs pas so/ gal te rtse mos g.yas brkyang
dang g.yon bskum skyil krung gis dag pa gsungs pas g.yas brkyang ba/ g.yon bskum pa/ rgyab ma gnyis skyil krung phyed pa bstan no snyam na skyil krung phyed pa de la g.yas
brkyang g.yon bskum tshang bas de'i dag pa ston pa ste mtsho skyes 'grel par/ de dag kyang mnyam par brtsegs pa'i snying gar zhabs g.yas pa gnyis kyis mnan pa'o/ /rol mo'i
tshul ni skyil krung phyed pa'o/ /de'i g.yas brkyang ba ni thugs rjes sems can la chags pa'o/ /g.yon bskum pa ni shes rab kyis chos gang yang mi 'dzin par btang ba'o
zhes gsungs so/ /gzhan du na bde mchog la rdor dril 'dzin pa'i phyag gnyis las gzhan pa'i phyag gnyis kyis yum la 'khyud dgos par 'gyur te/ rje btsun gyis rdor dril 'dzin
pa dang yum la 'khyud pa gsum gyis dag pa gsum so sor gsungs pa'i phyir ro/ /'grel lugs kyi gzhung rnams las gsal kha mi snang yang / rin chen 'bar bar nyi mar zhabs g.yas
zhes sogs kyi don mdun ma gnyis g.yas brkyang g.yon

bskum/ rgyab ma gnyis skyil krung phyed pa'i gar stabs su mngon te/ rje btsun gyis gdan gyi rnam gzhag las gtso bo'i zhabs phyed krung gis tshangs pa dang / g.yas brkyangs
pas dbang phyug g.yon bskums pas gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi bdud sdig can rnams kyi snying ga nas mnan pa dang / yum gyi g.yon pas brgya byin gyi snying ga nas mnan par
gsungs pa'ang 'di la dgongs pas bkram ldan gyi tshe yab kyi zhabs g.yas brkyang ba gsum dang / yum gyi g.yon brkyang bas bdud bzhi mnan nas/ bskum pa gnyis kyis mnan rgyu
med pa la bya dgos par snang ngo / /mdor na gsung tshul so so ma gtogs sbyar tshul gang la sbyar kyang yang dag pa re 'byung bas 'gal ba med pa 'dra'o zhes man ngag gi gsal
byed las gsungs pa 'dis log rtog thams cad sel nus la/ ku mu tir zhabs g.yas brkyangs pa'i brla la g.yon pa'i sor mo sleb cing / g.yas pa'i zhabs kyi rtses bdud bzhi'i
snying gar mnan pa gsal bar gsungs pa dang / rje btsun kun dga' bzang pos kye rdor bcu bdun ma'i mngon rtogs su gsungs pa'i bzhugs tshul 'khrul spong gi mchod brjod dang
/ mi thub zla ba'i bdud bzhi'i snying gar nyams dga'i gnas su sems can don mdzad dgyes zhes pa dang / sgyi chu ba'i dka' 'grel las kyang gtso bo bdud bzhi brtsegs pa'i
gdan zhes gsungs pa rnams kyis bdud bzhi mnyam par mnan pa'i bzhugs tshul 'di grub/ des na 'grel lugs kyi'ang ku mu ti dang yan lag drug par yang brtsegs gdan bshad pa khas

len dgos shing / rin chen 'bar ba dang / yan lag drug pa dang / ku mu tir bshad pa rnams grangs mi 'dra ba cung zad la 'gal ba med par kho bo sems so/ snying po don gsal las/
de slad khyod zhabs phyag dang phyag mtshan gzhan dbang kho nar bdag gis 'tshal/ /zhes bshad pa'i phyir ro zhes sogs gsungs so/ /gnyis pa rtse mo'i bka' bsgrub pa la/
mus srad pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis rjes 'brangs kha cig rang gis bzhag pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi tshad dang gzhal yas khang gi yi ge 'di 'gal bar mthong nas hwa shang gi dgongs
'grel ltar 'dir yang smra bar byed do zhes phyogs snga bkod nas mi 'thad de/ chos rje bla mas gong ma'i bka' 'bum bsgrigs pa'i nang du ma chud kyang / theg chen chos
rje'i phyag dpe'i mjug tu/ 'di la phyi mo du ma snang yang bka' 'bum snga ma rnams su ma bcug phyis sgo rum dpe khang nas kyang bla dpe rnying pa byung ba mthong nas yid
ches par byas te bka' 'bum phyi ma rnams su bzhugs su gsol ba yin no zhes gsungs pas tshad mar nges pa'i phyir zhes sogs gsungs pa'i lan du/ mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub
kyi tshig don mun sel las sgo rum dpe khang na bla dpe rnying pa yod pa dang / theg chen chos rjes bka' 'bum phyi ma rnams su bcug pas rje btsun sku mched kyis mdzad par
sgrub mi nus/ 'on kyang gzhung 'dir rgyud 'grel gyi lung dang bcas te gzhal yas khang gi gnas lugs la sgro 'dogs gcod pa rnam bshad zla zer du bshad pa bzhin mi snang
yang / sgrub pa po'i blo la bsgom bde zhing gnad ma 'khrugs pa zhig ni yin

nam snyam mo zhes gsungs shing / yang khyed rang ltar na yi ge de zhang bya ru bas mdzad do zer ba dang / gong ma'i yi ger mi gsal ba rnams rjes 'brangs kyi yi ger bshad pa
la tshad mar byed do zer bar grags pas dkyil 'khor gyi tshad 'chad pa na yi ge 'di tshad mar byed dgos te/ gzhan rtsis su byed pa'i gong ma rjes 'brangs dang bcas pa sus
kyang khung cung zad tsam yang med cing / zhang bya ru ba'i khrid kyi sngon 'gro mi byed pa tshad mar byed/ 'di tshad mar mi rung ba'i rgyu mtshan med pa'i phyir ro zhes
pa'i lan du/ glo bo mkhan chen rin po ches rje btsun khu dbon gyi slob ma zhang bya ru bas byas pa'i gzhal yas khang gi rnam gzhag kyang yod do gsungs pa/ rje rdo rje 'chang
gi dngos slob dag gsung ba thos kyi/ yi ge 'di zhang bya ru bas byas pa yin no gsung ba ma thos shing / zhang bya ru bas khrid kyi sngon 'gro mi byed pa'i rgyu mtshan
gsal po zhig khyed kyis gsungs shig de nas de'i lan 'don par 'gyur ro zhes gsungs so/ /gsum pa rje btsun gyi bka' bsgrub pa la mus srad pa chen pos de kho na nyid gsum
gyi man ngag rje btsun gyi bkar bsgrub pa dang / dbang po rab 'bring gsum gyis bkri ba'i gzhung shing rje btsun gyi bkar bsgrub pa gnyis su mdzad nas/ dang po la rjes 'brangs
kha cig bzlas pa'i skabs su 'phags pa rin po ches mdzad pa'i phar 'khor gyi man ngag bkag pas yi ge 'di nyid du phar 'khor gsal bar bshad pas rang gi de ma bden par
dogs nas yi ge 'di la skur pa btab pa yin no zhes phyogs snga bkod nas/ de mi

'thad de rje btsun gyis/ smin byed ltung ba'i rnam gzhag sgrub thabs bzhi/ /zhes sogs kyis yig cha'i grangs ston pa'i phyir/ rdo rje dril bu bgrang 'phreng dgang blugs dang
/ /zhes pa 'dis kyang lag len gyi yi ge ston byed yin na gzhan rnams la yi ge yod la/ 'di la med pa'i rgyu mtshan med la/ rgyud 'grel na yod pa la kha 'phangs zer na gzhan
rnams la'ang mtshungs so/ de dag bshad pa tsam dang lag len du bsgrigs pa'i khyad par yod na 'di la'ang mtshungs/ yi ge'i grangs ston pa ma yin par las dang po pa la dgos
pa bsgrigs pa tsam yin na bris sku dang glegs bam sogs mang du 'chad dgos pas nyung ba'i phyir dang / ye shes dang dam tshig gi dril bu go nor bas rnam dag min na/ gnad
kyi gsal byed du/ yang na ye shes ni rnam pa lnga ste/ rdo rje 'di'i rtse mo lnga pa'i rnam par dag pa'ang shes par 'gyur ro zhes bla ma gong ma rnams gsungs so zhes pa'ang
rnam dag min par 'gyur la/ gnad kyi gsal byed du lha'i rnam dag sbyar ba dang mi mthun pas zer na/ dbang chur de la de bzhin gshegs pa lnga dang / yum lnga dang / byang
chub sems dpa' dang / lha mo la sogs pa rdo rje'i de kho na nyid yongs su rdzogs pa mos pa bskyed la zhes gsungs pa'ang ma dag par 'gyur ro/ /de'i phyir rngog pa'i rjes
'brangs dag gi yi ge'o zhes pa ni/ gzhan rang tshig la yid ches bskyed pa'i zol tsam mo zhes gsungs so/ /de dag gi lan du mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub kyis/ de dag
ni mi rigs te da lta rje btsun gyis mdzad par grags pa'i de kho na nyid gsum gyi man ngag tu

grags pa 'di/ rje btsun gyi dngos slob spyil sgom tshul khrims rgyal mtshan gyis rje btsun gyi gsung sgros bskyar ba las/ rje btsun chen po'i zhal nas rdo rje dang dril bu'i
de kho na nyid ston pa'i yi ge zhig byed 'dod pa yin pa la ma grub ces gsung bar dngos su bshad 'dug pas/ rje btsun gyi dngos slob 'di nyid rje btsun gyi gsung la rgyus
che bar byed dgos so/ des na brgyud pa 'di pa rnams ni sambu Ta'i TIka chen du bshad pa gzhir byas nas rje btsun dang sa paN gnyis ka'i dngos slob shar pa shes rab 'byung
gnas kyis mdzad pa'i rdor dril gyi de kho na nyid zhib tu bshad pa de gtso che bar mdzad do zhes gsungs shing / yang gnyis pa dbang po rab 'bring gsum gyis bkri ba'i gzhung
shing rje btsun gyis bkar bsgrub pa la/ mus srad pa'i bka' sgrub le'ur rjes 'brangs kha cig lam 'bras kyi sngon 'gro'i khrid bkag pas phyis su yi ge 'di nyid dang 'gal
bar mthong ste rang gi grub mtha' la mi gnod pa'i phyir rje btsun gyi gsung ma yin no zhes dgag mod/ mi 'thad de/ rje btsun gyis dkar chag las gsungs pa ltar yi ge lhag
yod med phye nas rnam dag rnams phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs/ mkhas grub kyi slob ma mang po la bshad de deng sang gi bar du yi ge du ma dang bcas dar ba 'di la su zhig gis smyon
'ding na'ang rang gis de nyid ma go bar byed pa yin pa'i phyir dang / sa paN dang bla ma dam pa rnams kyis tshad mar bzhag pa'i phyir zhes gsungs pa'i lan du/ rje btsun
bsod nams lhun grub kyis bla ma chos rje rdo rje 'chang chen pos dpyad pa cung zad mdzad pa

'di la zhib tu gzigs la lan yod na drang por gsungs shig de'ang 'di ltar gsungs te/ gang zag gi bye brag gsum du bkri ba'i gzhung shing zhes pa 'di glegs bam phal mo cher ma
tshang la/ kha cig tu/ gang zag rigs kyi dbye bas lam gyi 'khrid/ /brjed pa'i dran pa gso phyir tho tsam bris/ /zhes pa'i tshig yod pa'i dpe chung mang ba zhig yod pa dang
/ glegs bam kha cig tu shog gcig ma chung ngu zhig bris pa ste mi 'dra ba gnyis snang ba las/ dang po dpe chung mang ba 'di ni rjes 'brang kha cig gis byas pa yin gyis/
rje btsun yab sras kyis mdzad pa ma yin te nor ba'i tshogs mang du snang ba'i phyir zhes sogs dpyad pa mdzad pa de bkod nas/ tho yig chung ngu 'dir dpyad pa mdzad par
snang ba 'di'i don la legs par soms shig ces gsungs la/ yang mus srad pa chen pos der ma zad rjes 'brangs de dag gis rje btsun gyi dkar chag las gzhung shing bzhi'i khrid
kyi yi ge yod par bshad cing / sngar gyi yi ge rnying pa de bkag pas de'i hor kong bsab pa'i don du rang blos sbyar ba'i dbang po rab 'bring gsum gyis bkri ba'i gzhung shing
gi yi ge byas gsungs nas tho yig de 'dri bar mdzad de sgo rum dpe khang nas rnyed do zhes zer ro zhes phyogs snga bkod nas/ de ni mi 'thad de khyed rang yan chad kyi
gang zag su la'ang de yod par ma grags la/ grags na lam 'bras dar ba ltar yi ge de'ang dar dgos pa las rnying pa re re tsam yang ma mthong zhing / don la'ang skyon cher
yod de zhes sgrub byed kyang 'god par mdzad do/ /de'i lan du glo bo mkhan chen rin po ches khyed kyis

nged kyi phyogs la rang dgar bris pa yin no zer ba'i yig 'phreng phyed gsum tsam byas pa'i tshig rnams ni nged rang gi lugs kyi glegs bam rnams kyi nang du bris pa med cing
/ de las cung zad tsam gyis mang ba'i shog gcig ma zhig yod pa la ni zhes gsungs nas yi ge de 'dri bar mdzad pa'i rjes su/ 'di mnga' ris gung thang gi sgo mang chen po'i
phyag dpe rnying pa zhig la bris pa'ang mthong zhing zhes gsungs nas/ yi ge de nyid kyi don yang bkrol bar mdzad la/ yang bzhi pa sa paN gyi bka' bsgrub la/ mus srad pa
chen pos rjes 'brang kha cig sngon 'gro'i khrid bkag pa dang pho brang drug tu 'dod pa gnyug ma dran gsal gyi lugs bsres pa yin no zhes pho brang drug dang / dbang po rab
'bring gsum gyis bkri ba'i gzhung shing gi yi ge bkag pa dang / yi ge 'dir de dag gsal bar bshad pas rang gi grub mtha' la gnod dogs nas dgag pa byed mod ces phyogs snga
brjod nas/ de 'gog pa na/ 'di'i gsal byed zang tsha'i zin bris yod pa dang / bla ma dam pas gzhung shing bzhi'i yi ger thun gyi sngon 'gro sogs 'di nyid tshad mar mdzad
nas bshad cing / ngo mtshar snang bar 'di'i mtshan nas smos pa dang / tshogs sgom pa'i slob ma nyan gnyags gnyis kyi khrid yig tu khrid kyi sngon 'gro dang / thun gyi sngon
'gro sogs 'di dang mthun par 'byung ba dang / chos rje gzungs pas bla ma klu pa'i dris lan du yi ge 'di tshad mar byas nas lan mdzad pas bla ma de dag 'di tshad mar bzhed
pa grub/ gang zag de tsam gyis tshad mar mdzad pas

tshad mar mi 'grub na ha cang thal la rje btsun gyis gdan sogs kyi yi ger pho brang lnga'am drug gi dbus ma de sangs rgyas dang rig ma'i gdan zhes gsungs pas pho brang drug
pa la gnyug ma dran gsal gyi lugs 'dres zer ba rje btsun bkag par song zhing / rje btsun gyis gsung de'i gsal byed du yi ge 'di med na pho brang drug gi bsgom tshul yang
mi shes par 'gyur bas khyed dag yi ge 'dir bstan pa'i zab gnad las ring du gyur pa'o zhes gsungs so/ /de'i lan du glo bo mkhan chen rin po ches tshig don mun sel du/ sa
paN gyis mdzad pa'i khrid kyi dkar chag ni rje a nanda'i gsung rab gang na'ang the tshom gyi dpyad gzhi mdzad pa cung zad kyang med/ zin bris 'ga' zhig tu dpyad gzhi byas
pa yod kyang de dag la blo gtad thub pa ci yang med/ sgo rum dpe khang na bzhugs pa'i sa pan gyi bka' 'bum rgya shog la bris pa'i gser rkyang ma rnying ba zhig yod pa de
dang / 'phags pa'i thugs dam bzhi thog na bzhugs pa'i gser ma la'ang 'di nyid bzhugs la/ gdung brgyud rtse gdong pa rnams kyi bka' 'bum gser dngul ma rnying pa la'ang 'di
nyid bzhugs shing / rje btsun A nanda'i gsan yig rgya mtshor khrid kyi dkar chag gi brgyud pa ni zhes gsungs shing / bla ma brgyud pa rnams kyang 'dren par mdzad de lan
gsungs so/ yang thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyi gsung ngag 'chad thabs kyi man ngag gsang ba sgo 'byed las 'phros pa'i dris lan zab don snying po las/ rje sa
paN gyi khrid kyi dkar chag ces pa brda don gsal ba'i khrid yig la ngos 'dzin par mdzad na

ni bshad ma thag pa de dang shin tu 'grig cing / rje sa paN gyis mdzad par grags pa'i dkar chag cig shos de ni lung phu ba kun rgyal gyis mdzad pa yin ces gsung sgros rnams
las 'byung la/ rgyud yig 'ga' zhig las shong ston khu dbon gyi slob ma lo tsA ba kun dga' rgyal mtshan zhes pa zhig 'byung gin snang ba de dang gcig pa 'dra zhing / dkar
chag de las snang ba gsum lam gyi gzhi bca' la sbyar ba'i tshe de'i sngon du dbang bskur 'gro dgos pa'i gsal kha ci yang mi snang mod/ spyir dkar chag 'di la tshig rigs
dang mdzad byang sogs 'dra mi 'dra sna tshogs zhig 'dug pas/ bsregs bcad brdar ba'i gser bzhin du legs par brtags nas blang dgos par mchis lags zhes gsungs nas dkar chag
gi yi ge de sa paN gyi gsung yin min dpyad gzhi can du bshad pa 'di dang / glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub kyis rtsod spong tshig don mun sel mdzad gong du/ rab 'byams
pa blo gros rab gsal gyi dris lan las sa paN gyis mdzad zer ba'i dkar chag gi yi ge 'di sa skya'i bla brang bzhi thog na yod pa'i sa paN gyi bka' 'bum rgya shog la bris
pa'i gser ma chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa tsam gyi dus su byung ba gcig yod pa de'i nang du'ang bris/ gzhan bka' 'bum rnying pa mang po'i nang du bcug yod cing / chos rje
dpal ldan bla ma dam pas kyang sa paN gyis mdzad par gsungs 'dug pa la/ rje btsun rdo rje 'chang kun dga'i gsung nas sa paN gyis mdzad nges pa zhig yin na brda don gsal
ba'i khrid kyi gsung tho dang / lho pa'i zin

bris sogs dang mthun pa zhig dgos rgyu yin pa la/ de dag dang mi mthun pa'i rim pa 'ga' re 'dug pas the tshom gyi gzhi yin gsung ba dang / de'i dpyad pa mdzad pa'i yi ge cung
zad cig kyang yod de dpe ma rnyed/ gsung sgros 'dzin pa phyi ma rnams kyang dpyad gzhir mdzad pa de kha shas che zhes dang / 'di 'dra'i rigs can la yin min gyi shan 'byed
pa shin tu dka' bar mchis zhes gsungs pa gnyis dgongs don gcig par byung yang / glo bo mkhan chen rin po che rang gi bzhed pa ltar na tshig don mun sel du khrid kyi dkar
chag sa paN gyi gsung yin pa lta bu zhig bshad pa de 'dod dgos pa 'dra ste/ dri lan de nyid las de la mus srad pa sogs kyi dkar chag bsgrub pa zer ba'i yi ge sogs byas
nas sa paN gyis mdzad nges pa yin zer ba'i shes byed mang po bkod pa yod tshod 'dug kyang lta rtog byas nas ji ltar yin nges pa ma byung zhing zhes gsungs pas dri lan 'di
mdzad dus bsgrub pa bzhi ma gzigs la/ phyis 'di dag spyan lam du mngon nas gzigs rtog dang dpyad pas dag par mdzad nas bka' sgrub le'u'i lan 'debs su tshig don mun sel
brtsams pa na sngar mdzad pa'i dri lan de las phyis mdzad pa'i tshig don mun sel 'di 'thad ldan du gzung bar bya dgos sam snyam mo/ /de ltar de dag gis ni dpal ldan sa skya
pa'i bstan 'dzin ngor rdzong rnam gnyis kyi gsung ngag rin po che'i phyag len gyi rim pa 'ga' zhig las brtsams te so so'i bzhed srol rnams legs par bshad pa lugs gnyis
gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba 'di'ang gangs can bstan pa'i bdag po'i bstan 'dzin mtha'

dag la phyogs lhung dang bral ba'i dad pa chen pos nye bar len pa'i rkyen byas te legs par bshad pa re zhig de tsam mo/ /'dir smras pa/ 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir thub dbang zas
gtsang sras/ /slar yang byon pa lta bu'i 'gro ba'i mgon/ /sa skya'i bla chen yab sras khu dbon bcas/ /bka' drin dran pas slar yang lan brgyar 'dud/ /gang gi bstan 'dzin
mkha' la nyi zla ltar/ /'dzin ma'i khyod 'dir ngor rdzong rnam gnyis zhes/ /snyan grags skye bo kun gyi khar rgyu ba'i/ /'gran bral skyes bu'i mchog rnams bsngags par 'os/
/snyigs dus dpal ldan sa skya'i bstan pa la/ /sa skya'i bla chen kun dga' snying po dang / /bka' drin mnyam pa'i sngags 'chang chos kyi rje/ /kun dga' rin chen zhabs kyis
slar yang skyongs/ /mgon de'i rigs sras bsod nams dbang po zhes/ /mthu stobs rdzu 'phrul bsam yas gang de dang / /yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas bstan pa'i srog /grags
pa'i mtshan gyis byang chub bar du srungs/ /rang sems gdod nas spros bral nam mkha'i ngang / /'on kyang 'khor 'das snang ba 'gag med 'char/ /shar yang ngo bos stong pa'i
blo 'das kyi/ /gdod ma'i mgon po mus pa chen po rgyal/ /e ma sngon byon mkhas pa rnams kyi gsung / /phyogs lhung 'khyog po'i bsam sbyor dang bral bar/ /kun la dang 'dod dad
pa'i blo mtsho las/ /legs bshad tshig gi me tog 'di 'khrungs so/ /tshul 'dir 'bad dang dus gsum dge ba'i mthus/ /bdag cag dpon slob 'gro drug mkha' mnyam gyi/ /shes rgyud
sgrib gnyis

bag chags dang bcas pa/ /ma lus byang nas don gnyis phun tshogs shog /bdag kyang rdo rje'i lus brtas dbang po gsal/ /rigs brgyud myur 'byung bstan la ches phan cing / /dpon
slob tshe mthar phyin nas phyi ma'i tshe/ /bde ldan zhing du lhan cig skye bar shog /gnas der sa lam rtogs pa mthar phyin te/ /gang 'dul sprul pas sngags 'chang yab sras
kyi/ /bstan 'di srid mtha'i bar du 'dzin pa sogs/ /yid la re ba'i don kun lhun grub shog /ces dpal ldan sa skya pa'i bstan 'dzin ngor rdzong rnam gnyis kyi gsung ngag rin
po che'i phyag len gyi rim pa 'ga' zhig las brtsams te so so'i bzhed srol rnams legs par bshad pa lugs gnyis gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba 'di'ang sa gsum gyi bla ma grub
thob kyi 'khor los sgyur ba 'jam pa'i dbyangs bsod nams dbang po'i zhal snga nas dang / yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rtsa lag sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/
brtan g.yo'i khyab bdag rdo rje sems dpa' nyid gzhan ngor ngur smrig gi bla gos 'chang ba rgyal ba mus pa chen po rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ sprul pa'i
sku spyan snga chos kyi spyan ldan kun dga' don grub/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa 'jam pa'i dbyangs ngag dbang chos grags la sogs te yongs 'dzin dam pa bka' drin can
rnams kyi gsung las skyes pa dpal sa skya pa shAkya'i dge gnyen paNDi ta mkhas pa/ sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos 'phags
pa'i yul na ba hu dhA nyaHste 'bru mang po zhes grags shing rgya nag lugs la sa pho

stag gi lo khrums kyi zla ba'i dkar phyogs rgyal ba dang po'i tshes la bod kyi rdo rje gdan dpal sa skya'i chos grwa chen po'i lha chen rig 'dzin pho brang gi rang gshong bsam
gtan khang bu 'chi med rdo rje'i gur khang du legs par sbyar ba'i yi ge pa ni skyes sbyangs kyi nyal slong shes rab kyi mngon brjod/ chen po dang ldan pas gsung rab mang
po'i mgrin pa can rab 'byams smra ba dge slong rdo rje 'dzin pa bsam gtan rgya mtshos dad gus kyi sgo nas mgyogs par bgyis so/ 'dis kyang bdag cag dpon slob rnams kyis
'di phyi'i don thams cad yid bzhin du 'grub pa'i rgyur gyur cig dharme u da ya mastu/chos 'di dar bar gyur cig ka lyan lbardhantu/dge legs 'phel bar gyur cig sarba mangga
